i þe feaderes ant i þe sunes ant i þe hali gastes nome her biginneþ ancrene wisse al þet gode religiuse doþ oþer werieþ efter þe uttre riwle al togedere is hervore al nis bute ase tole to timbrin hertowart al nis bute as þuften to servi þe leafdi to riwlin þe heorte þis an boc is todealet in eahte leasse bokes nu mine leove sustren þis boc ich todeale on eahte destinctiuns þet ȝe cleopieþ dalen ant euch wiþute monglunge spekeþ al bi himseolf of sunderliche þinges ant þah euchan riht falleþ efter oþer ant is þe leatere eaver iteiet to þe earre þe earste dale spekeþ al of ower servise þe oþer is hu ȝe schulen þurh ower fif wittes witen ower heorte þet ordre ant religiun ant sawle lif is inne i þis destinctiun aren chapitres five as fif stuchen efter fif wittes þe witeþ þe heorte as wakemen hwerse ha beoþ treowe ant spekeþ of euch wit sunderlepes o rawe þe þridde dale is of anes cunnes fuheles þe daviþ i þe sawter eveneþ himseolf to as he were ancre ant hu þe cunde of þe ilke fuheles beoþ ancren iliche þe feorþe dale is of fleschliche fondunges ant gasteliche baþe ant confort aȝeines ham ant of hare salven þe fifte dale is of schrift þe seste dale is of penitence þe seoveþe of schir heorte hwi me ah ant hwi me schal luvien ant hwet binimeþ us his luve ant let us him to luvien þe eahtuþe dale is al of þe uttre riwle earst of mete ant of drunch ant of oþre þinges þet falleþ þerabuten þerefter of þe þinges þe ȝe mahen undervon ant hwet þinges ȝe mahen witen oþer habben þerefter of ower claþes ant of swucche þinges as þerabuten falleþ þerefter of ower werkes of doddunge ant of blodletunge of ower meidnes riwle aleast hu ȝe ham schulen leofliche learen her biginneþ þe earste boc of ures ant ureisuns þe gode beoþ to seggen hwen ȝe earst ariseþ blesciþ ow ant seggeþ ant biginneþ anan wiþ up ahevene ehnen ant honden toward heovene buhinde o cneon forþ ward upo þe bedde ant seggeþ swa al þe ymne ut wiþ þe verset ant te ureisun herefter scheoiende ow ant claþinde ow seggeþ ant þis word seggeþ eaver aþet ȝe beon al greiþe þis word habbeþ muchel on us ant i muþ ofte euch time þet ȝe mahen sitten ȝe oþer stonden hwen ȝe beoþ al greiþe sprengeþ ow wiþ haliweater þet ȝe schulen eaver habben ant þenchen o godes flesch ant on his deorewurþe blod þet is abuve þe hehe weoved ant falleþ adun þertowart wiþ þeose gretunges alswa ȝe schule don hwen þe preost halt hit up ed te measse ant bivore þe hwen ȝe schule beon ihuslet efter þis falleþ o cneon to ower crucifix wiþ þeose fif gretunges ine munegunge of godes fif wunden ant wiþ þis word beateþ on ower breoste hwase ne con þeos five segge þe earste cneolinde fif siþen ant blesciþ ow wiþ euchan of þeose gretunges ant wiþ þeose wordes beateþ ower heorte ant cusseþ þe eorþe icruchet wiþ þe þume þe refter wendeþ ow to ure leafdi onlicnesse ant cneoliþ wiþ fif aleast to þe oþre ymagnes ant to ower relikes luteþ oþer cneoliþ nomeliche to þe halhen þe ȝe habbeþ to þurh luve iturnd ower weofdes swa muche þe reaþere ȝef ei is ihalhet þerefter ananriht ure leafdi uhtsong ant seggeþ o þis wise ȝef hit is werc dei falleþ to þer eorþe ȝef hit is halidei buhinde sumdeal duneward seggeþ ant ba stille rihteþ ow up þe refter ant seggeþ makieþ on ower muþ a creoiz wiþ þe þume ed a large creoiz wiþ þe þume ant wiþ þe twa fingres from buve þe forheaved dun to þe breoste ant falleþ to þe eorþe ȝef hit is wercdei wiþ oþer buheþ duneward ȝef hit is halidei aþet þus ed euch ant ed te biginnunge of þe ant i þe ed ant ed te ant hwerse ȝe eaver hereþ nome inempnet ant ed euch þet falle to ower ures ant to þe ant to þe collecte ed eavereuch tide ant ed te leatemeste vers of eavereuch ymne ant ed te leaste vers wiþuten an of þe salm ed alle þes ilke ȝef hit is halidei buheþ sumdel dunewart ȝef hit is wercdei falleþ to þer eorþe ed te biginnunge of eaver euch tide wiþ makieþ rodetaken as ich ear tahte ed buheþ oþer cneoliþ efter þet te dei is wiþ falleþ eaver adun ant ed tis word cusseþ þe eorþe ant alswa i þe ed tis word ant ed te messe i þe muchele ed ant euchan segge hire ures as ha haveþ iwriten ham ant euch tide sunderliche ase forþ as ȝe mahen seggeþ in his time ear to sone þen to leate ȝef ȝe ne mahen eaver halde þe time uhtsong bi niht i winter i sumer i þe dahunge þis winter schal biginnen ed te halirode dei ine hervest ant leasten aþet easter prime in winter earliche i sumer bi forþmarhen þe refter ȝef ȝe habbeþ neode for eani hihþe to speoken ȝe muhe seggen hit bivoren ant efter uhtsong anan ȝef hit swa neodeþ non eaver efter mete ant hwen ȝe slepeþ efter slep hwil þet sumer leasteþ bute hwen ȝe feasteþ i winter bivore mete hwen ȝe al veasteþ þe sunnedei þah efter mete for ȝe eoteþ twien ed te an salm ȝe schulen stonden ȝef ȝe beoþ eise ant ed te oþer sitten ant eaver wiþ rungen up ant buhen hwase mei stonden al on ure leafdi wurþschipe stonde o godes halve ed alle þe seove tiden singeþ ant ba bivoren ant efter efter euch tide bivore þe ed þreo tiden seggeþ wiþ bivoren uhtsong ant efter prime ant efter complie from ower complie aþet efter haldeþ silence efter evensong anan ower euche niht seggeþ hwen ȝe beoþ eise bute hit beo hali niht for feaste of nihe lesceuns þe cume ine marhen bivore cumplie oþer efter uhtsong wiþ þreo salmes ant wiþ þreo lesceuns euche niht sundri in aniversaries of ower leoveste freond seggeþ alle nihene i stude of ed euch psalmes ende ed sitteþ aþet alswa ed bute ed te lesceuns ant ed te ant from al ut i stude of seggeþ on ende ine marhen oþer i niht efter þe suffragies of uhtsong seggeþ commendaciun sittinde þe salmes cneolinde þe ureisuns oþer stondinde ȝef ȝe þus doþ euche niht bute ane sunneniht ȝe doþ muche betere in ameldei we seggeþ ba ant efter þe metegraces i twimeldei efter non ant ȝe alswa mote don seove psalmes seggeþ sittinde oþer cneolinde wiþ þe letanie fiftene psalmes seggeþ o þis wise þe earste five for owseolf ant for alle þe ow god doþ oþer unnen þe oþre five for þe peis of al hali chirche þe þridde five for alle cristene sawles efter þe forme five efter þe oþre five alswa efter þe þridde five þe ȝe schulen seggen wiþuten seove salmes ant þus þeose fiftene seggeþ abuten under for abute swuch time as me singeþ measse in alle religiuns ant ure laverd þolede pine upo þe rode ȝe ahen to beo nomeliche i beoden ant i bonen ant alswa from prime aþet midmarhen hwen preostes of þe worlt singeþ hare meassen ȝe mahen ȝef ȝe wulleþ seggen ower þis wise almihti godd feader sune hali gast as ȝe beoþ þreo an godd alswa ȝe beoþ an mihte an wisdom ant an luve ant þah is mihte iturnd to þe in hali writ nomeliche þu deorewurþe feader to þe wisdom seli sune to þe luve hali gast ȝef me an almihti godd þrile i þreo hades þes ilke þreo þinges mihte forte servi þe wisdom forte cweme þe luve ant wil to don hit mihte þet ich mahe don wisdom þet ich cunne don luve þet ich wulle don aa þet te is leovest as þu art ful of euch god alswa nis na god wone þeras þeose þreo beoþ mihte ant wisdom ant luve iveiet togederes þet tu ȝetti me ham hali þrumnesse i þe wurþschipe of þe þreo hwase hit haveþ oþer sum oþer of þe hali þrumnesse segge þe wulle a þin are for mine sunnen ahonget o rode for þe ilke fif wunden þe þu on hire bleddest heal mi blodi sawle of alle þe sunnen þet ha is wiþ iwundet þurh mine fif wittes i þe munegunge of ham þet hit swa mote beon deorewurþe laverd fif ȝef þu const oþer of þe creoiz sum oþer þis is an of þe beste for þe seove ȝiftes of þe hali gast þet ich ham mote habben ant for þe seove tiden þet hali chirche singeþ þet ich deale in ham slepe ich oþer wakie ant for þe seove bonen i þe aȝein þe seoven heaved ant deadliche sunnen þet tu wite me wiþ ham ant alle hare brokes ant ȝeove me þe seovene selie eadinesses þe þu havest laverd bihaten þine icorene i þin eadi nome seove for þe ten heastes þe ich ibroken habbe summe oþer alle ant meseolven towart te hwetse beo of oþerhwet untreoweliche iteoheþet i bote of þeose bruchen forte sahtni me wiþ þe deorewurþe laverd ten i þe wurþgunge of þine tweof apostles þet ich mote overal folhin hare lare þet ich mote habben þurh hare bonen þe tweolf bohes þe bloweþ of chearite as seinte writeþ blisfule laverd tweolf halhen þe ȝe luvieþ best in heore wurþgunge seggeþ oþer leas oþer ma as ow bereþ on heorte ant þet efterward wiþ hare collecte for alle þeo þe habbeþ eani god ido me iseid me oþer iunnen me ant for alle þe ilke þe wurcheþ þe six werkes of misericorde mearciable laverd six hwase wule segge þe salm bivore þe ant for alle þe sawlen þe beoþ forþfearen i þe bileave of þe fowr goddspelles þe haldeþ al cristendom upo fowr halves þet tu þe fowr marheȝeven ȝeove ham in heovene milzfule laverd fowr ȝef ȝe seggeþ nihene as þer beoþ nihene englene weoredes þet godd þurh his mearci hihi ham ut of pine to hare feolahredden ȝe doþ ȝet betere ant her alswa ȝe wulleþ seggeþ bivore þe ant bi dei sum time oþer bi niht gederiþ in ower heorte alle seke ant sarie þet wa ant poverte þolieþ þe pinen þe prisuns þolieþ ant habbeþ þer ha liggeþ wiþ irn hevie feþeret nomeliche of þe cristene þe beoþ in heaþenesse summe i prisun summe in ase muche þeowdom as oxe is oþer asse habbeþ reowþe of þeo þe beoþ i stronge temptatiuns alle hare sares setteþ in ower heorte ant sikeþ to ure laverd þet he neome reowþe of ham ant bihalde toward ham wiþ þe ehe of his are ant ȝef ȝe habbeþ hwile seggeþ þe salm i þe measse hwen þe preost heveþ up godes licome seggeþ þis vers stondinde ant þenne falleþ adun wiþ þeose gretunges ant swa al þe salm ut wiþ twien efter þe meassecos hwen þe preost sacreþ þer forȝeoteþ al þe world þer beoþ al ut of bodi þer i sperclinde luve bicluppeþ ower leofmon þe into ower breostes bur is iliht of heovene ant haldeþ him heteveste aþet he habbe iȝettet ow al þet ȝe eaver easkiþ þis ureisun bivore þe muchele rode is of muche strengþe abute middei hwase mei hwase ne mei þenne o sum oþer time þenche o godes rode ase muchel as ha eaver con mest oþer mei ant of his derve pine ant biginne þe refter þe ilke fif gretunges þe beoþ iwriten þe ruppe ant alswa cneolin to euch an ant blescin as hit seiþ þer ant beate þe breoste ant makie a þulli bone as ear eft biginne as ear alle five þe antefne as ear þe salm þe antefne as ear al ut ant tenne as ear to þe eorþe twien as ear þridde chearre riht alswa ant feorþe chearre ant fifte nawiht ne changeþ bute þe salmes ant te ureisuns þe forme salm þe oþer þe þridde þe feorþe þe fifte ant in euch beoþ fif vers þe fif ureisuns beoþ wiþ ant hwase ne con þeos fif ureisuns segge eaver an ant hwase þuncheþ to long leave þe salmes leafdi seinte for þe ilke muchele blisse þet tu hefdest inwiþ þe i þet ilke time þet godd godes sune efter þe engles gretunge nom flesch ant blod in þe ant of þe underfeng mi gretunge wiþ þe ilke ant make me telle lutel of euch blisse utewiþ ah frovre me inwiþ ant ernde me þeo of heovene ant ase wis as i þe ilke flesch þet he toc of þe nes neaver sunne ne i þin as me leveþ efter þe ilke tacunge hwetse bivore were clense mi sawle of fleschliche sunnen biginne þe aþet as me biginneþ antefne ant tenne þe salm ant efter þe salm al ut fif siþen ant þus to euch salm al ut fif siþen leafdi seinte for þe ilke muchele blisse þet tu hefdest þa þu sehe þe ilke blisfule bearn iboren of þi cleane bodi to moncunne heale wiþuten eavereuch bruche wiþ ihal meiþhad ant meidenes menske heal me þet am þurh wil tobroken as ich drede hwetse beo of dede ant ȝef me in heovene seon þi blisfule leor ant bihalde lanhure meidenes menske ȝef ich nam wurþe forte beon iblisset in hare ferredden as ear five leafdi seinte for þe ilke muchele blisse þet tu hefdest þa þu sehe þi deore deorewurþe sune efter his derve deaþ arisen to blisful lif his bodi sevevalt brihtre þen þe sunne ȝef me deien wiþ him ant arisen in him worltliche deien gasteliche libben dealen in his pinen feolahliche in eorþe forte beon i blisse his feolahe in heovene for þe ilke muchele blisse þet tu hefdest leafdi of his blisful ariste efter þi muchele sorhe efter mi sorhe þet ich am in her lead me to þi blisse fif siþen leafdi seinte for þe ilke muchele blisse þet tu hefdest þa þu sehe þi brihte blisfule sune þet te giws wenden forte aþrusmin i þruh se wurþliche ant se mihtiliche on hali þursdei stihe to his blisse into his riche of heovene ȝef me warpe wiþ him al þe worlt under fet ant stihennu heorteliche hwen ich deie gasteliche o domesdei al licomliche to heovenliche blissen fif siþen leafdi seinte for þe ilke muchele blisse þet fulde al þe eorþe þa he underveng þe into unimete blisse ant wiþ his blisfule earmes sette þe i trone ant cwene crune on heaved brihtre þen þe sunne heh heovenliche cwen underveng þeos gretunges of me swa on eorþe þet ich mote blisfulliche grete þe in heovene fif siþen ant þenne þet antefne antefne antefne antefne her sitteþ þe fifti oþer hundret oþer ma oþer leas efter þet me haveþ hwile on ende þet hwase wule mei stutten þe ruppe ananrihtes efter þe forme ureisun ant segge þenne hire tale of efter þe leaste salm eaver bivore þe salm biginnen an aþet ant segge stondinde þe salm þe salmes beoþ inumene efter þe fif leattres of ure leafdis nome hwasa nimeþ ȝeme ant al þis ilke ureisun efter hire fif heste blisses eorneþ bi five tele i þe antefnes ant tu schalt finden in ham gretunges five þe ureisuns þet ich nabbe buten ane imearket beoþ iwriten over al wiþute þe leaste leoteþ writen on a scrowe hwetse ȝe ne kunnen þus ich biginne mine oþer hwiles leafdi swete leafdi swetest alre leafdi leafdi leovest leafdi lufsumest leafdi leafdi seinte deorewurþe leafdi leafdi cwen of heovene leafdi cwen of are leafdi do me are leafdi meiden moder meiden godes moder moder meiden of milce moder of grace ant fallen to þer eorþe ant cussen hire wiþ þis leaste vers hwase is hal iheafdet ant tenne tene ant tene togederes þe teoheþe eaver þus forþ ant cusse þe eorþe on ende oþer degre oþer bench oþer sumhwet herres ant biginnen leafdi swete leafdi as ear þe forme tene þe fifti cneolinde up ant dun þe oþre cneolinde iriht up stille buten ed te sum semblant wiþ þe oþer cneo a lutel þe þridde tene adun ant upo þe elbohen riht to þer eorþe þe feorþe þe elbohen o degre oþer o bench ant eaver to þe lute wiþ þe heaved þe fifte tene stondinde ant eft biginne þe turn as i þe frumþe al þet ȝe eaver seggeþ of þulliche oþre bonen as ant on ower ahne wise salmes ant ureisuns ich am wel ipaiet euchan segge ase best bereþ hire on heorte verseilunge of sawter redunge of englisc oþer of frensch halie meditatiuns ower cneolunges hwense ȝe eaver mahen iȝemen ear mete ant efter eaver se ȝe mare doþ se godd ow eche forþre his deorewurþe grace ah lokiþ swa ich bidde ow þet ȝe ne beon neaver idel ah wurchen oþer reden oþer beon i bonen ant swa don eaver sumhwet þet god mahe of awakenin þe ures of þe hali gast ȝef ȝe ham wulleþ seggen seggeþ euch tide of ham bivoren ure leafdi tide toward te preostes tiden hercniþ se forþ as ȝe mahen ah wiþ him ne schule ȝe nowþer verseilin ne singen þet he hit mahe iheren ower graces stondinde bivore mete ant efter as ha beoþ iwriten ow ant wiþ þe gaþ bivoren ower weoved ant endiþ þear þe graces bitweone mel þe drinken wule segge ant blesci efterwart hwense ȝe gaþ to ower bedd i niht oþer in even falleþ o cneon ant þencheþ i hwet ȝe habbeþ i þe dei iwreaþet ure laverd ant crieþ him ȝeorne merci ant forȝevenesse ȝef ȝe habbeþ ei god idon þonkiþ him of his ȝeove wiþute hwam we ne mahen ne wel don ne wel þenchen ant seggeþ ant ant stondinde ant aleast þenne wiþ þreo creoiz wiþ þe þume upo þe forheaved ant þenne a large creoiz as ed wiþ ant tenne fowr creoiz o fowr half wiþ þeose fowre efter warde clauses on ende on owseolf ant o þe bedd baþe i bedd se vorþ se ȝe mahen ne do ȝe ne ne þenchen na þing bute slepen þe ne con oþer uhtsong oþer ne mei hit seggen segge for uhtsong þritti ant efter euch ant efter euch aleast hwase con for evensong twenti for euch oþer tide segge fiftene o þis ilke wise bute þet ed uhtsong schal seggen earst hwase con ant ed complie ed alle þe oþre tiden hwase is unheite forkeorve of uhtsong tene of euch of þe oþre five þe halvendal of euchan ȝef ha is seccre hwase is ful meoseise of al beo ha cwite neome hire secnesse nawt ane þolemodliche ah do swiþe gleadliche ant al is hiren þet hali chirche ret oþer singeþ þah ȝe ahen of godd þenchen in euch time meast þah in ower tiden þet ower þohtes ne beon fleotinde þenne ȝef ȝe þurh ȝemeles gluffeþ of wordes oþer misneomeþ vers neomeþ ower dun ed ter eorþe wiþ þe hond ane al fallen adun for muche misneomunge ant schawiþ ofte i schrift ower ȝemeles herabuten þis is nu þe forme dale þe haveþ ispeken hiderto of ower servise hwetse beo þerof þeose riwlen herefter ich walde ha weren of alle as ha beoþ of ow þurh godes grace ihalden her biginneþ þe oþer dale of þe heorte warde þurh þe fif wittes wiþ alles cunnes warde dohter seiþ wite wel þin heorte for sawle lif is in hire ȝef ha is wel iloket þe heorte wardeins beoþ þe fif wittes sihþe ant herunge smechunge ant smeallunge ant euch limes felunge ant we schulen speoken of alle for hwase wit þeose wel he deþ bode he wit wel his heorte ant his sawle heale þe heorte is a ful wilde beast ant makeþ moni liht lupe as seint seiþ na þing ne etfliþ mon sonre þen his ahne heorte daviþ godes prophete meande i sum time þet ha wes etsteart him þet is min heorte is edflohe me ant eft he blisseþ him ant seiþ þet ha wes icumen ham laverd he seiþ min heorte is icumen aȝein eft ich hire habbe ifunden hwense hali mon ant se wis ant se war lette hire edstearten sare mei anoþer of hire fluht carien ant hwer edbrec ha ut from daviþ þe hali king godes prophete hwer godd wat ed his ehþurl þurh a sihþe þet he seh þurh a bihaldunge as ȝe schulen efter iheren forþi mine leove sustren þe leaste þet ȝe eaver mahen luvieþ ower þurles alle beon ha lutle þe parlurs least ant nearewest þe claþ in ham beo twafald blac þet claþ þe cros hwit wiþinnen ant wiþuten þet blake claþ bitacneþ þet ȝe beoþ blake ant unwurþ to þe world wiþuten þet te soþe sunne haveþ utewiþ forculet ow ant swa wiþuten as ȝe beoþ unseowlich imaket ow þurh gleames of his grace þe hwite cros limpeþ to ow for þreo crosses beoþ read ant blac ant hwit þe reade limpeþ to þeo þe beoþ for godes luve wiþ hare blodschedunge irudet ant ireadet as þe martirs weren þe blake cros limpeþ to þeo þe makieþ i þe worlt hare peni tence for ladliche sunnen þe hwite limpeþ ariht to hwit meidenhad ant to cleannesse þet is muche pine wel forte halden pine is ihwer þurh cros idon to understonden þus bitacneþ hwit cros þe warde of hwit chastete þet is muche pine wel to biwitene þe blake claþ alswa teke þe bitacnunge deþ leasse eil to þe ehnen ant is þiccre aȝein þe wind ant wurse to seon þurh ant halt his heow betere for wind ant for oþer hwet lokiþ þet te parlures claþ beo on eavereuch half feaste ant wel itachet ant witeþ þer ower ehnen leaste þe heorte edfleo ant wende ut as of daviþ ant ower sawle seccli sone se heo is ute ich write muchel for oþre þet nawiht ne rineþ ow mine leove sustren for nabbe ȝe nawt te nome ne ne schulen habben þurh þe grace of godd of totilde ancres ne of tollinde locunges ne lates þet summe oþer hwiles weilawei uncundeliche makieþ for aȝein cunde hit is ant unmeaþ sulli wunder þet te deade dotie ant wiþ cwike worltmen wede þurh sunne me leove sire seiþ sum ant is hit nu se overuvel forte totin utwart ȝe hit leove suster for uvel þe þer kimeþ of hit is uvel ant overuvel to eavereuch ancre nomeliche to þe ȝunge ant to þe alde forþi þet ha to þe ȝungre ȝeoveþ uvel forbisne ant scheld to werien ham wiþ for ȝef ei edwit ham þenne seggeþ ha anan me sire þeo deþ alswa þet is betere þen ich am ant wat betere þen ich hwet ha haveþ to donne leove ȝunge ancre ofte a ful haher smiþ smeoþeþ a ful wac cnif þe wise folhe i wisdom ant nawt i folie an ald ancre mei do wel þet te þu dest uvele ah totin ut wiþuten uvel ne mei ower nowþer nim nu ȝeme hwet uvel beo icumen of totunge nawt an uvel ne twa ah al þe wa þet nu is ant eaver ȝete wes ant eaver schal iwurþen al com of sihþe þet hit beo soþ lo her preove þurh þet he seh ant biheold on himseolf his ahne feiernesse leop into prude ant bicom of engel eatelich deovel of eve ure alde moder is iwriten on alre earst in hire sunne inȝong of hire ehsihþe þet is eve biheold o þe forboden eappel ant seh hine feier ant feng to delitin i þe bihaldunge ant toc hire lust þertoward ant nom ant et þe rof ant ȝef hire laverd low hu hali writ spekeþ ant hu inwardliche hit teleþ hu sunne bigon þus eode sihþe bivoren ant makede wei to uvel lust ant com þe dede þerefter þet al moncun ifeleþ þes eappel leove suster bitacneþ alle þe þing þet lust falleþ to ant delit of sunne hwen þu bihaldest te mon þu art in eve point þu lokest o þe eappel hwase hefde iseid to eve þa ha weorp earst hire ehe þe ron a eve went te awei þu warpest ehe o þi deaþ hwet hefde ha iondsweret me leove sire þu havest woh hwerof chalengest tu me þe eappel þet ich loki on is forbode me to eotene ant nawt to bihalden þus walde eve inohreaþe habben iondsweret o mine leove sustren as eve haveþ monie dehtren þe folhiþ hare moder þe ondswerieþ o þisse wise me wenest tu seiþ sum þet ich wulle leapen on him þah ich loki on him godd wat leove suster mare wunder ilomp eve þi moder leop efter hire ehnen from þe ehe to þe eappel from þe eappel i parais dun to þer eorþe from þe eorþe to helle þer ha lei i prisun fowr þusent ȝer ant mare heo ant hire were ba ant demde al hire ofsprung to leapen al efter hire to deaþ wiþuten ende biginnunge ant rote of al þis ilke reowþe wes a liht sihþe þus ofte as me seiþ of lutel muchel waxeþ habbe þenne muche dred euch feble wummon hwen þeo þe wes riht ta iwraht wiþ godes honden wes þurh a sihþe biswiken ant ibroht into brad sunne þet al þe world overspreadde a meiden dyna het dohter as hit teleþ i eode ut to bihalden uncuþe wummen ȝet ne seiþ hit nawt þet ha biheold wepmen ant hwet come wenest tu of þet bihaldunge ha leas hire meidenhad ant wes imaket hore þe refter of þet ilke weren trowþen tobrokene of hehe patriarches ant a muchel burh forbearnd ant te king ant his sune ant te burhmen islein þe wummen ilead forþ hire feader ant hire breþren se noble princes as ha weren utlahen imakede þus eode ut hire sihþe al þullich þe hali gast lette writen o boc forte warni wummen of hare fol ehnen ant nim þerof ȝeme þet tis uvel of dyna com nawt of þet ha seh sichen emores sune þet ha sunegede wiþ ah dude of þet ha lette him leggen ehnen on hire for þet tet he dude hire wes i þe frumþe sare hire unþonkes alswa þurh þet ha unwreah hire i daviþes sihþe ha dude him sunegin on hire se hali king as he wes ant godes prophete nu kimeþ forþ a feble mon halt him þah ahelich ȝef he haveþ a wid hod ant a loke cape ant wule iseon ȝunge ancres ant loki nede ase stan hu hire wlite him liki þe naveþ nawt hire leor forbearnd i þe sunne ant seiþ ha mei baldeliche iseon hali men ȝe swucche as he is for his wide sleven me surquide sire ne herest tu þet daviþ godes ahne deorling bi hwam he seolf seide ich habbe ifunden quoþ he mon efter min heorte þes þe godd seolf seide bi þis deorewurþe sahe king ant prophete icuret of alle þes þurh an ehewurp to a wummon as ha wesch hire lette ut his heorte ant forȝet himseolven swa þet he dude þreo utnume heaved ant deadliche sunnen o spusbruche þe leafdi þet he lokede on treisun ant monslaht on his treowe cniht urie hire laverd ant tu a sunful mon art se swiþe hardi to keasten cang ehnen upo ȝung wummon ȝe mine leove sustren ȝef ei is anewil to seon ow ne wene ȝe þer neaver god ah leveþ him þe leasse nulle ich þet nan iseo ow bute he habbe of ower meistre spetiale leave for alle þe þreo sunnen þet ich spec of least ant al þet uvel of dina þet ich spec of herre al com nawt forþi þet te wummen lokeden cangliche o wepmen ah for heo unwriȝen heom in monnes echsiþþe ant duden hwarþurch ha machten fallen in sunne forþi wes ihaten on godes laȝe þet put were iwriȝen eaver ant ȝef ani were unwriȝen ant beast feolle þerin he þe unwreah þe put hit schulde ȝelden þis is a swiþe dredful word to wummon þet schaweþ hire to wepmones echne heo is bitacned bi þeo þet unwriþ þe put þe put is hire feire neb hire hwite swire hire lichte echnen hond ȝef ha halt forþ in his echȝesihþe ȝet beoþ hire word put bute ha beon þe bet iset al ȝet þe feaȝeþ hire hwetse hit eaver beo þurch hwat machte sonre fol luve awacnin al ure laverd put cleopeþ þis put he hat þet beo ilided þet beast þe rin ne falle ant druncni in sunne best is þe beastlich mon þet ne þenchet naut on god ne ne noteþ naut his wit as mon ach to donne ach secheþ for to fallen in þis put þet ich spec of ȝef he hit open fint ach þe dom is ful strong to þeo þe þe put unlideþ for heo schal ȝelde þe best þet þe rin biþ ifallen ha is witi of his deaþ biforen ure laverd ant schal for his saule ondsweren an domesdei ant ȝelde þe bestes lure hwenne ha navet oþer ȝeld þenne hireseolven strong ȝeld is her mid alle ant godes dom is ant his heste þet heo hit ȝelde allegate for heo unlidede þe put þet hit adrong inne þu þet unwrisd þis put þu þet dest ani þing þurch hwet mon is of þe fleschliche ifonded þach þu hit nute naut dred þis dom swiþe ant ȝef he is ifonded swa þet he sunege deadliche on ani wise þach hit ne beo naut wiþ þe bute wiþ wil toward þe oþer ȝef he secheþ to fullen ed sum oþer þe fondunge þet of þe þurch þi dede awacnede beo al siker of þe dom þu schalt ȝelde þe best for þe puttes openunge ant buten þu beo iscrive þerof acorien his sunne hund wule in bluþelich hwarse he fint open þet þe muþ ne mei for scheome þe licht echye spekeþ hit ant is as erendebeorere of þe lichte heorte ach nu is sum wummon þe nalde for nan þing wilni fulþe to mon ant þach ne rochte ha neaver þach he þochte toward hire ant were of hire ifondet ant nu deþ sein ba twa þeos in a cuple wilnin ant habbe wil forto beon iwilned ȝirni mon oþer habbe wil forto beon iȝirned of mon ba is haved sunne þe echnen beoþ þe forme arewen of lecheries prickes alswa ase men worreþ mid þreo cunes wepnes wiþ scheotung ant wiþ speres ord ant wiþ sweordes egge al richt wiþ þilke wepnen þet is wiþ schute of eche wiþ spere of wundinde word wiþ sweord of deadlich hond werreþ lecherie þe stinkinde hore upon þe lavedi chastete þet is godes spuse earest scheot þe arewen of þe licht echnen þe fleoþ lichtliche forþ ase flaa þet is iviþered ant stikeþ i þere heorte þerefter schakeþ hire spere ant neolachet upon hire ant mid schakinde word ȝeveþ speres wunde sweordes dunt is dunricht þet is þe hondlunge for sweord smit of nech ant ȝeveþ deaþes dunt ant hit is weilawei nech ido wiþ ham þe cumeþ swa nech togederes þet ouþer hondli oþer oþer ifele oþer hwase is wis ant seli wiþ þe schute wite hire þet is wite hire echnen for al þet uvel þerefter kimeþ of þe echne arewen ant nis ha muche chang oþer to folhardi þe hald hire heved baltliche ut of þe opene carnel hwil me wiþ utewiþ assailleþ þe castel sikerliche ure þe werreur of helle he scheot as ich wene ma to an ancre þenne to seovene ant fifti lavedis i þe worlde þe of þe castel beoþ hire husþurles as deþ com seiþ sein into þe world þorch sunne asswa deaþ þurch þeos echþurles haveþ inȝong to þe saule laverd as men walden steoke feste uh þurl of hire hus for hwon þet heo machten bisteoken deaþ þe rute ant an ancre nule naut tunen hire eilþurl aȝein þe deaþ of saule ant mid good richt muȝen ha beon ihaten eilþurles for ha habbeþ idon muchel eil to moni ancre al holi writ is ful of warningge of eie laverd he seiþ david went awei min echnen from þe worldes dweole ich abbe ifestned foreward seiþ mid min echnen þet ich ne misþenche hu dele þencheþ me mid echye god hit wat he seiþ wel for efter þe echye kimeþ þe þocht ant þerefter þe dede þet wiste wel þet mende þus weilawei he seiþ min eche haveþ irobbed al min saule hwenne godes prophete makede þulli mon of eche hwic man wenest þu þet beo icumen to moni mon ant to moni wumman sorege of heore echye þe wise askiþ hweþer ani þing harmi mare wimmon þenne deþ hire echye al þe leor he seiþ schal floȝen of teres for þe ehesichþe ane þis is nu of þis wit i noch iseid to warni þe seli we schulen þauh sone herefter speken herof more inwiþ þe gale heorte nawt ane euch fleschlich hondlunge ah ȝetten euch gal word is ladlich vilainie ant godes grome wurþe þah hit ne weoxe forþre bitweone mon ant ancre nu þurh riht godes wrake geaþ hit forþre ant forþre ant bikimeþ ofte ant ear me least wene into þet fule sunne we hit habbeþ weilawei iherd of inohe ne leve namon ancre þe let in monnes ehe to schawin hireseolven over al þet ȝe habbeþ iwriten in ower riwle of þinges wiþuten þis point þis article of wel to beo bitunde ich wulle beo best ihalden to wummon þe wilneþ hit openiþ ow o godes half ȝef ha ne spekeþ nawt þe rof leoteþ swa i wurþen bute ȝef ȝe dreden þet heo þe refter beo iscandlet of hire ahne suster haveþ sum ibeon itemptet in toward ower weoved ne beode ȝe na mon forte bihalden ah ȝef his devotiun bit hit ant haveþ grant draheþ ow wel inward ant te veil adun toward ower breoste ant sone doþ þe claþ aȝein ant festniþ heteveste ȝef he lokeþ toward bed oþer easkeþ hwer ȝe liggeþ ondswerieþ lihtliche sire þerof wel mei duhen ant haldeþ ow stille ȝef bischop kimeþ to seon ow hihiþ sone towart him ah sweteliche bisecheþ him ȝef he bit to seon ow þet ȝe moten þeronont halden ow towart him as ȝe habbeþ idon ant doþ to alle oþre ȝef he wule allegate habben a sihþe lokiþ þet hit beo ful scheort þe veil anan adun ant draheþ ow bihinden an ancre wearnde eadmodliche sein hire sihþe ant he þervore dude hire þe menske þet he neaver ne dude to nan oþer ant hervore hire word is aþet cume þis dei iboren in hali chirche for as we redeþ of hire hwase wule hire windowes witen wel wiþ þe uvele ha mot ec wiþ þe gode hwense ȝe moten to eani mon eawiht biteachen þe hond ne cume nawt ut ne ower ut ne his in ant ȝef hit mot cumen in ne rine nowþer oþer heo is siker seiþ hali writ þe feor from grunen draheþ hire ant þeo þe luveþ peril i peril ha schal fallen þe deofles grune is ofte itild þer me least weneþ nis nan þet nis dredful þet ha nis ilecchet for godd nule wite nan þet is se folhardi þet ha ne wit wearliche wiþ him hireseolven þis is nu of þis wit inoh i seid ed tis chearre to warnin þen seli we schulen þah sone herefter speoken herof mare spellunge ant smechunge beoþ i muþ baþe as sihþe is i þe ehe ah we schulen leten smechunge aþet we speoken of ower mete ant speoken nu of spellunge ant þerefter of herunge of ba imeane sumchearre as ha gaþ togederes on alre earst hwen ȝe schulen to ower parlurs þurl witeþ ed ower meiden hwa hit beo þet beo icumen for swuch hit mei beon þet ȝe schule essinien ow hwen ȝe alles moten forþ crossiþ ful ȝeorne muþ ehnen ant earen ant te breoste mid al ant gaþ forþ mid godes dred to preost on earst ant þe refter þet he ah to seggen hercniþ hise wordes ant haldeþ ow al stille þet hwen he parteþ from ow þet he ne cunne ower god ne ower uvel nowþer ne ne cunne ow nowþer lastin ne preisin sum is se wel ilearet oþer se wis iwordet þet ha walde he wiste hit þe sit ant spekeþ toward hire ant ȝelt him word aȝein word ant forwurþeþ meistre þe schulde beon ancre ant leareþ him þet is icumen hire forte learen walde bi hire tale beon sone wiþ wise icuþþet ant icnawen icnawen ha is for þurh þet ilke þet ha weneþ to beo wis ihalden he understont þet ha is sot for ha hunteþ efter pris ant kecheþ lastunge for ed te alre leaste hwen he is awei iwent þeos ancre he wule seggen is of muche speche eve heold i parais long tale wiþ þe neddre talde him al þe lesceun þet godd hefde ired hire ant adam of þe eappel ant swa þe feond þurh hire word understod ananriht hire wacnesse ant ifond wei toward hire of hire forlorenesse ure leafdi seinte dude al on oþer wise ne talde ha þen engel na tale ah easkede him scheortliche þing þet ha ne cuþe ȝe mine leove sustren folhiþ ure leafdi ant nawt te cakele eve forþi ancre hwetse ha beo hu muchel se ha eaver cunne halde hire stille nabbe ha nawt henne cunde þe hen hwen ha haveþ ileid ne con bute cakelin ah hwet biȝet ha þe rof kimeþ þe kaue ananriht ant reaveþ hire hire eairen ant fret of þet schulde forþ bringe cwike briddes al riht alswa þe cave deovel bereþ awei from cakelinde ancres ant forswolheþ al þe god þet ha istreonet habbeþ þet schulde as briddes beoren ham up towart heovene ȝef hit nere icakelet þe wrecche povre peoddere mare nurþ he makeþ to ȝeien his sape þen þe riche mercer al his deorewurþe ware as is iseid herefter to sum gastelich mon þet ȝe beoþ trusti upon as ȝe mahe beon o lut god is þet ȝe easki read ant salve þet he teache ow toȝeines fondunges ant i schrift schawiþ him ȝef he wule iheren ower greaste ant ower ladlukeste sunnen forþi þet him areowe ow ant þurh þe areownesse inwardluker crie mearci for ow ant habbe ow in his bonen ah witeþ ow ant beoþ warre he seiþ ure laverd for monie cumeþ to ow ischrud mid lombes fleos ant beoþ wedde wulves worltliche leveþ lut religiuse ȝet leas ne wilni ȝe nawt to muchel hare cuþþunge eve wiþute dred spec wiþ þe neddre ure leafdi wes offearet of speche ure freres prechurs ant ure freres meonurs beoþ of swuch ordre þet al folc mahte wundrin ȝef ei of ham wende ehe towart te wude lehe forþi ed euch time þet eani of ham þurh chearite kimeþ ow to learen ant to frovrin i godd ȝef he is preost seggeþ ear þen he parti ich schrive me to godd almihti ant to þe þet ich as ich drede riht repentant neaver nes of mine greaste sunnen þet ich habbe ischawet to mine schriftfeaderes ant tah min entente beo to beten ham herinne ich hit do se povreliche ant sunegi in oþre deihwamliche seoþþen ich wes nest ischriven ant þet wes þenne ant of þe ant nempnin ich habbe þus isunget ant segge o hwucche wise as hit is iwriten ow in ower schriftes boc towart te ende þe rof ant aleast seggeþ þis ant muche mare ant bide him undervo þe spetiale in his god ant þonke him of his inturn ant bisech him aleast greten þe ant te ant þet ha bidden for þe wiþuten witnesse of wummon oþer of wepmon þe ow mahe iheren ne speoke ȝe wiþ na mon ofte ne longe ant tah hit beo of schrift allegate i þe ilke hus oþer þer he mahe iseon toward ow sitte þe þridde bute ȝef þe ilke þridde oþer stude trukie þis nis nawt for ow leove sustren iseid ne for oþre swucche nawtforþi þe treowe is ofte mistrowet ant te saclese bilohen as josep i of þe gale leafdi for wone of witnesse me leveþ þe uvele sone ant te unwreaste bliþeliche liheþ o þe gode sum unseli haveþ hwen ha seide ha schraf hire ischriven hire al to wundre forþi ahen þe gode habben eaver witnesse for twa acheisuns nomeliche þe an is þet te ondfule ne mahe lihen on ham swa þet te witnesse ne pruvie ham false þe oþer is forte ȝeoven þe oþre forbisne ant reavi þe uvele ancre þe ilke unseli gile þet ich of seide ut þurh þe chircheþurl ne halde ȝe tale wiþ namon ah beoreþ þerto wurþmunt for þe hali sacrement þet ȝe seoþ þerþurh ant neomeþ oþerhwile to ower wummen þe huses þurl to oþre þe parlur speoken ne ahe ȝe bute ed tes twa þurles silence eaver ed te mete ȝef oþre religiuse as ȝe witen doþ hit ȝe ahen over alle ȝef ei haveþ deore geast do hire meidnes as in hire stude to gleadien hire feire ant heo schal habbe leave forte unsperren hire þurl eanes oþer twien ant makie sines toward hire of a glead chere summes curteisie is iturnt hire to uvel under semblant of god is ofte ihulet sunne ancre ant huses leafdi ah muchel to beon bitweonen euche fridei of þe ȝer haldeþ silence bute hit beo duble feaste ant tenne haldeþ hit sum oþer dei i þe wike i þe advenz ant i þe umbriwiken weodnesdei ant fridei i þe lenten þreo dahes ant al þe swiingwike aþet non on easter even to ower wummen ȝe mahen þah seggen wiþ lut word hwetse ȝe wulleþ ȝef eani god mon is of feorren icumen hercniþ his speche ant ondswerieþ wiþ lut word to his easkunges muche fol were þe mahte to his bihove hweþer se he walde grinden greot oþer hweate ȝef he grunde þe greot ant lette þe hweate hweate is hali speche as seint seiþ heo grint greot þe chafleþ þe twa cheken beoþ þe twa grindel stanes þe tunge is þe cleappe lokiþ leove sustren þet ower cheken ne grinden neaver bute sawle fode ne ower eare ne drinke neaver bute sawle heale ant nawt ane ower eare ah ower ehþurl sperreþ to aȝeines idel speche to ow ne cume na tale ne tidinge of þe worlde ȝe ne schule for na þing wearien ne swerien bute ȝef ȝe seggen witerliche oþer sikerliche oþer o sum swuch wise ne preachi ȝe to na mon ne mon ne easki ow cunsail ne ne telle ow readeþ wummen ane seint forbeot wummen to preachin na wepmon ne chastie ȝe ne edwiten him his unþeaw bute he beo þe overcuþre halie alde ancres hit mahe don summes weis ah hit nis nawt siker þing ne ne limpeþ nawt to ȝunge hit is hare meoster þe beoþ over oþre iset ant habbeþ ham to witene as hali chirche larewes ancre naveþ forte loken bute hire ant hire meidnes halde euch hire ahne meoster ant nawt ne reavi oþres moni weneþ to do wel þe deþ al to wundre for as ich seide ear under semblant of god is ofte ihulet sunne þurh swuch chastiement haveþ sum ancre arearet bitweonen hire ant hire preost oþer a falsinde luve oþer a muche weorre þet is þe ende of þe tale seiþ seneke þe wise ich chulle þet ȝe speoken seldene ant þenne lutel moni punt hire word forte leote ma ut as me deþ weater ed mulne swa duden freond þe weren icumen to frovrin him seten stille seoveniht ah þa ha hefden alles bigunnen to speokene þa ne cuþen ha neaver stutten hare cleappe swa hit is of monie as sein seiþ silence is wordes fostrilt ant bringeþ forþ chaffle on oþer half as he seiþ long silence ant wel iwist nedeþ þe þohtes up towart heovene alswa as ȝe mahe seon weater hwen me punt hit ant stoppeþ hit bivore wel þet hit ne mahe duneward þenne is hit inedd aȝein forte climben uppart ant ȝe al þisses weis pundeþ ower wordes forstoppiþ ower þohtes as ȝe wulleþ þet ha climben ant hehin toward heovene ant nawt ne fallen duneward ant tofleoten ȝont te worlt as deþ muchel chaffle hwen ȝe nede moten a lute wiht lowsiþ up ower muþes flodȝeten as me deþ ed mulne ant leoteþ adun sone ma sleaþ word þen sweord lif ant deaþ seiþ is i tunge honden hwa se witeþ wel his muþ he witeþ he seiþ his sawle hwase ne wiþhalt his wordes seiþ þe wise he is as þe burh wiþute wal þet ferde mei in over al þe feond of helle mid his ferd wend þurhut te tutel þe is eaver open into þe heorte i hit teleþ þet an hali mon seide þa me preisede ane breþren þet he hefde iherd of muche speche gode quoþ he ha beoþ ah hare wununge naveþ na ȝete hare muþ meaþeleþ eaver hwase eaver wule mei gan in ant leaden forþ hare asse þet is hare unwise sawle forþi seiþ sein þet is ȝef eni weneþ þet he beo religius ant ne bridli nawt his tunge his religiun is fals he gileþ his heorte he seiþ swiþe wel ne bridleþ nawt his tunge bridel nis nawt ane i þe horses muþ ah sit sum upo þe ehnen ant geaþ abute þe earen for alle þreo is muche neod þet ha beon ibridlet ah i þe muþ sit tet irn ant o þe lihte tunge for þear is meast neod hald hwen þe tunge is o rune ant ifole to eornen ofte we þencheþ hwen we foþ on to speoken forte speoke lutel ant wel isette wordes ah þe tunge is slubbri for ha wadeþ i wete ant slit lihtliche forþ from lut word into monie ant tenne as seiþ ne mei nawt muche speche ne ginne hit neaver se wel beo wiþute sunne for from soþ hit slit to fals ut of god into sum uvel from meosure into unimete ant of a drope waxeþ into a muche flod þe adrencheþ þe sawle for wiþ þe fleotinde word tofleoteþ þe heorte swa þet longe þe refter ne mei ha beon riht igederet togederes þis beoþ seint word in his ase neh as ure muþ is to worldlich speche ase feor he is godd hwen he spekeþ toward him ant bit him eani bone forþi is þet we ȝeiȝeþ upon him ofte ant he firseþ him awei frommard ure stevene ne nule nawt iheren hire for ha stinkeþ to him al of þe worldes meaþelunge ant of hire chafle hwase wule þenne þet godes eare beo neh hire tunge firsi hire from þe world elles ha mei longe ȝeiȝen ear godd hire ihere ant seiþ þurh þet is þah ȝe makien monifalde ower bonen to ward me ȝe þe pleieþ wiþ þe world nule ich ow nawt iheren ah ich wulle turne me awei hwen ȝe heoveþ toward me hehe ower honden ure deorewurþe leafdi seinte þe ah to alle wummen to beo forbisne wes of se lutel speche þet nohwer in hali writ ne finde we þet ha spec bute fowr siþen ah for se selt speche hire wordes weren hevie ant hefden muche mihte hire forme wordes þet we redeþ of weren þa ha ondswerede þen engel ant teo weren se mihtie þet wiþ þet ha seide ed tis word godes sune ant soþ godd bicom mon ant te laverd þet al þe world ne mahte nawt bifon bitunde him inwiþ hire meidnes wombe hire oþre wordes weren þa ha com ant grette hire mehe ant hwet mihte wes icud ed þeose wordes hwet þet a child bigon to pleien toȝeines ham þet wes sein in his moder wombe þe þridde time þet ha spec þet wes ed te neoces ant ter þurh hire bisocne wes weater iwent to wine þe feorþe time wes þa ha hefde imist hire sune ant eft him ifunde ant hu muche wunder folhede þeose wordes þet godd almihti beah to mon to ant to to a smiþ ant to a wummon ant folhede ham ase heoren hwider se ha walden neomeþ nu her ȝeme ant leorniþ ȝeorne herbi hu seltsene speche haveþ muche strengþe feole iwordet mon seiþ þe salmwruhte ne schal neaver leaden riht lif on eorþe forþi he seiþ elleshwer ypallage ant is as þah he seide ich chulle wite mine weies wiþ mi tunge warde wite ich wel mi tunge ich mei wel halden þe wei toward heovene for as seiþ þe tilunge of rihtwisnesse þet is silence silence tileþ hire ant heo itilet bringeþ forþ sawles eche fode for ha is undeadlich as witneþ forþi feieþ hope ant silence baþe togederes ant seiþ in ham schal stonden gastelich strengþe þet is i silence ant in hope schal beon ower strengþe neomeþ ȝeme hu wel he seiþ for hwase is muche stille ant halt silence longe ha mei hopien sikerliche þet hwen ha spekeþ toward godd þet he hire ihere ha mei ec hopien þet ha schal singen þurh hire silence sweteliche in heovene þis is nu þe reisun of þe veiunge hwi veieþ hope ant silence ant cupleþ ba togederes teke þet he seiþ i þe ilke auctorite þet i silence ant in hope schal beon ure strengþe i godes servise toȝein þe deofles turnes ant his fondunges ah lokiþ þurh hwet reisun hope is a swete spice inwiþ þe heorte þet sweteþ al þet bitter þet te bodi drinkeþ ah hwase cheoweþ spice ha schal tunen hire muþ þet te swote breaþ ant te strengþe þe rof leave wiþinnen ah heo þe openeþ hire muþ wiþ muche meaþelunge ant brekeþ silence ha spit hope al ut ant te swotnesse þe rof mid worltliche wordes ant leoseþ aȝein þe feond gastelich strengþe for hwet makeþ us stronge i godes servise ant ine fondunges forte drehe derf to wreastli stealewurþliche toȝein þe deofles swenges bute hope of heh mede hope halt te heorte hal hwetse þe flesch drehe as me seiþ ȝef hope nere heorte tobreke a þin are hu stont ham þe beoþ þeras alle wa ant weane is wiþuten hope of utcume ant heorte ne mei bersten forþi as ȝe wulleþ halden inwiþ ow hope ant te swete breaþ of hire þe ȝeveþ sawle mihte wiþ muþ itunet cheoweþ hire inwiþ ower heorte ne blawe ȝe hire nawt ut wiþ meaþelinde muþes wiþ ȝeoniende tuteles lokiþ seiþ sein þet ȝe nabben ȝicchinde nowþer tunge ne earen þet is to seggen þet ow ne luste nowþer speoken ne hercni worltlich speche hiderto is iseid of ower silence ant hu ower speche schal beo seltsene of silence ant of speche nis bute a lare ant for þi i writunge ha eorneþ ba togederes nu we schulen sumhwet speoken of ower herunge aȝein uvel speche þet ȝe þertogeines tunen ower earen ant ȝef ned is spearren ower þurles for al uvel speche mine leove sustren stoppiþ ower earen ant habbeþ wleatunge of þe muþ þe speoweþ ut atter uvel speche is þreofald attri ful ant idel idel speche is uvel ful speche is wurse attri is þe wurste idel is ant unnet al þet god ne kimeþ of ant of þulli speche seiþ ure laverd schal euch word beon irikenet ant iȝeve reisun hwi þe an hit seide ant te oþer hit lustnede ant þis is þah þet leaste uvel of þe þreo uveles hwet hu þenne schal me ȝelde reisun of þe wurse hwet hu of þe wurste þet is of attri ant of ful speche nawt ane þet hit spekeþ ah þet hit hercneþ ful speche is as of leccherie ant of oþre fulþen þet unweschene muþes speokeþ oþerhwiles þeose beoþ alle ischrapede ut of ancre riwle þe swuch fulþe spit ut in eani ancre earen me schulde dutten his muþ nawt wiþ scharpe sneateres ah wiþ hearde fustes attri speche is heresie þweartover leasunge bacbitunge ant fikelunge þeos beoþ þe wurste heresie godd have þonc ne rixleþ nawt in englelond leasunge is se uvel þing þet seint seiþ þet forte schilde þi feader from deaþ ne schuldest tu nawt lihen godd seolf seiþ þet he is soþ ant hwet is mare aȝein soþ þen is leas þe deovel is leas ant leasunge feader þe ilke þenne þe stureþ hire tunge i leasunge ha makeþ of hire tunge cradel to þe deofles bearn ant rockeþ hit ȝeornliche as his nurrice bacbitunge ant fikelunge ant eggunge to don uvel ne beoþ nawt monnes speche ah beoþ þe deofles bleas ant his ahne stevene ȝef ha ahen to beo feor alle worltliche men hwet hu ahen ancren heatien ham ant schunien þet ha ham ne iheren iheren ich segge for hwase spekeþ ham nis ha nawt ancre þe neddre seiþ stingeþ al stille ant þeo þe spekeþ bihinden þet ha nalde bivoren nis nawiht betere herst tu hu eveneþ bacbitere to stinginde neddre swa hit is witerliche ha is neddre cundel ant bereþ þeo þe uvel spekeþ atter i þe tunge þe fikelere blent mon ant put him preon i þe ehe þet he wiþ fikeleþ þe bac bitere cheoweþ ofte monnes flesch i fridei ant beakeþ wiþ his blake bile o cwike charoines as þe þet is þes deofles corbin of helle ȝef he walde pilewin ant toteoren wiþ his bile rotet stinkinde flesch as is reavenes cunde þet is walde he seggen uvel bi nan oþer bute bi þeo þe rotieþ ant stinkeþ al i fulþe of hare sunne hit were leasse wunder ah lihteþ upo cwic flesch tolimeþ ant tolukeþ hit þet is misseiþ bi swuch þet is cwic ine godd he is to ȝiver reven ant to bald mid alle on oþer half neomeþ nu ȝeme of hwucche twa meosters þes twa menestraws serviþ hare laverd þe deovel of helle ful hit is to seggen ah fulre forte beon hit ant swa hit is allegate ha beoþ þes deofles gongmen ant beoþ aa in his gonghus þe fikeleres meoster is to hulie þe gongþurl þet he deþ as ofte as he wiþ his fikelunge ant wiþ his preisunge wriþ mon his sunne þet stinkeþ na þing fulre ant he hit huleþ ant lideþ swa þet he hit nawt ne stinkeþ þe bacbitere unlideþ hit ant openeþ swa þet fulþe þet hit stinkeþ wide þus ha beoþ aa bisie i þis fule meoster ant eiþer wiþ oþer striveþ herabuten þulliche men stinkeþ of hare stinkinde meoster ant bringeþ euch stude o stench þet ha to nahiþ ure laverd schilde þet te breaþ of hare stinkinde þrote ne nahi ow neaver oþer spechen fuleþ ah þeose attriþ baþe þe earen ant te heorte þet ȝe bet icnawen ham ȝef ei kimeþ toward ow low her hare molden fikeleres beoþ þreo cunnes þe forme beoþ uvele inoh þe oþre þah beoþ wurse þe þridde þah beoþ wurst þe forme ȝef a mon is god preiseþ him bivoren himseolf ant makeþ him inohreaþe ȝet betere þen he beo ant ȝef he seiþ wel oþer deþ wel heveþ hit to hehe up wiþ overherunge þe oþer ȝef a mon is uvel ant seiþ ant deþ se muche mis þet hit beo se open sunne þet he hit ne mahe nanes weis allunge wiþseggen he þah bivore þe mon seolf makeþ his uvel leasse nis hit nawt nu he seiþ se over uvel as me hit makeþ nart tu nawt i þis þing þe forme ne þe leaste þu havest monie feren let iwurþe god mon ne geast tu nawt te ane moni deþ muche wurse þe þridde cunne of fikelere is wurst as ich seide for he preiseþ þe uvele ant his uvele dede as þe þe seiþ to þe cniht þe robbeþ his povre men a sire as þu dest wel for eaver me schal þene cheorl peolkin ant pilien for he is as þe wiþin þe spruteþ ut þe betere þet me hine croppeþ ofte þus þes false fikeleres ablendeþ þe ham hercniþ as ich ear seide ant wriheþ hare fulþe þet ha hit ne mahe stinken ant þet is hare muchel unselhþe for ȝef ha hit stunken ham walde wleatie þerwiþ ant eornen to schrift ant speowen hit ut þer ant schunien hit þe refter bacbiteres þe biteþ bihinde bac oþre beoþ of twa maneres ah þe leatere is wurse þe earre kimeþ al openliche ant seiþ uvel bi anoþer ant speoweþ ut his atter se muchel se him eaver to muþ kimeþ ant culcheþ al ut somet þet te attri heorte sent up to þe tunge ah þe leatere kimeþ forþ al on oþer wise wurse feond þen þe oþer is ant under freondes huckel warpeþ adun þet heaved feþ on forte siken ear he eawt segge ant makeþ drupi chere bisampleþ longe abuten forte beo bet i levet hwen hit alles kimeþ forþ þenne is hit ȝeolow atter weila ha seiþ wa is me þet he oþer heo habbeþ swuch word icaht inoh ich wes abuten ah ne healp me nawt to don herof bote ȝare is þet ich wiste þe rof ah þah þurh me ne schulde hit beon neaver mare iuppet ah nu hit is þurh oþre swa wide ibroht forþ þet ich ne mei hit nawt wiþsaken uvel me seiþ þet hit is ant ȝet hit is wurse sorhful ich am ant sari þet ich hit schal seggen ah for soþe swa hit is ant þet is muchel sorhe for i feole oþer þing he oþer heo is swiþe to herien ah onont þis þing wa is me þervore ne mei ham namon werien þis beoþ þe deofles neddren þe spekeþ of ure laverd þurh his grace halde ower earen feor hare attrie tungen ne leve ow neaver stinken þet fule put þet ha unwreoþ as þe fikeleres wreoþ ant hulieþ as ich seide unwreon hit to hamseolven þeo þe hit tolimpeþ ant hulien hit to oþre þet is a muche þeaw nawt to þeo þe hit schulden smeallen ant heatien þet fulþe nu mine leove sustren from al uvel speche þet is þus þreovald idel ful ant attri haldeþ feor ower eare me seiþ upon ancren þet euch meast haveþ an ald cwene to feden hire earen a meaþelilt þe meaþeleþ hire alle þe talen of þe lond a rikelot þe cakeleþ al þet ha siþ ant hereþ swa þet me seiþ i bisahe from mulne ant from chepinge from smiþþe ant from ancrehus me tidinge bringeþ wat þis is a sari sahe þet ancrehus þet schulde beon anlukest stude of alle schal beon ifeiet to þe ilke þreo studen þet meast is in of chaffle ah ase cwite as ȝe beoþ of þullich leove sustren weren alle oþre ure laverd hit uþe nu ich habbe sunderlepes ispeken of þes þreo limen of ehe of muþ of eare of eare is al þis leaste to ancre bihove for leflich þing nis hit nawt þet ancre beore swuch muþ ah muchel me mei dreden to swucche muþes sumcheare þet ha beie hire eare of sihþe of speche of hercnunge is iseid sunderlepes of euchan o rawe cume we nu eft aȝein ant speoken of alle imeane understond ancre hwas spuse þu art ant hu he is gelus of alle þine lates ich am he seiþ bi himseolf þe geluse godd ich am gelus of þe syon mi leofmon wiþ muche gelusie þuhte him nawt inoh iseid þet he is gelus of þe bute he seide þerto wiþ muche gelusie seiþ þe wise wite þe nu ful wel his eare is eaver toward te ant he hereþ al his ehe aa bihalt te ȝef þu makest ei semblant eani luvelates toward unþeawes syon þet is schawere he cleopeþ þe his schawere swa his þet nan oþres forþi he seiþ in schaw þi neb to me he seiþ ant to nan oþer bihald me ȝef þu wult habbe briht sihþe wiþ þine heorte ehnen bihald inward þer ich am ant ne sech þu me nawt wiþute þin heorte ich am wohere scheomeful ne nule ich nohwer bicluppe mi leofmon bute i stude dearne o þulli wise ure laverd spekeþ to his spuse ne þunche hire neaver wunder ȝef ha nis muchel ane þah he hire schunie ant swa ane þet ha putte euch worldlich þrung ant euch nurþ eorþlich ut of hire heorte for heo is godes chambre nurþ ne kimeþ in heorte bute of sum þing þet me haveþ oþer isehen oþer iherd ismaht oþer ismeallet ant utewiþ ifelet ant þet witeþ to soþe þet eaver se þes wittes beoþ mare isprengde utward se ha leasse wendeþ inward eaver se recluse toteþ mare utward se ha haveþ leasse leome of ure laverd inward ant alswa of þe oþre lo hwet sein seiþ hwase ȝemelesliche wit hire uttre ehnen þurh godes rihtwise dom ha ablindeþ i þe inre þet ha ne mei iseo godd mid gastelich sihþe ne þurh swuch sihþe icnawen ant þurh þe cnawleachunge over alle þing luvien for efter þet me cnaweþ his muchele godnesse ant efter þet me feleþ his swote swetnesse efter þet me luveþ him mare oþer leasse forþi mine leove sustren beoþ wiþute blinde as wes þe hali ant þe gode ant godd wule as he ȝef ham ȝeoven ow liht wiþinnen him to seon ant cnawen ant þurh þe cnawlechunge over alle þing him luvien þenne schule ȝe iseon hu al þe world is nawt hu hire frovre is fals þurh þet sihþe ȝe schule seon alle þe deofles wiheles hu he biwrencheþ wrecches ȝe schulen iseon in owseolf hwet beo ȝet to beten of ower ahne sunnen ȝe schulen bihalde sumcheare toward te pine of helle þet ow uggi wiþ ham ant fleo þe swiþere ham frommard ȝe schulen gasteliche iseon þe blissen of heovene þe ontenden ower heorte to hihin ham toward ȝe schulen as i schawere iseon ure leafdi wiþ hire meidnes al þe englene weoret al þe halhene hird ant him over ham alle þe blisseþ ham alle ant is hare alre crune þis sihþe leove sustren schal frovrin ow mare þen mahte ei worltlich sihþe hali men witen wel þe habbeþ hit ifondet þet euch eorþlich gleadunge is unwurþ hertoȝeines hit is a dearne healewi seiþ seint ewangeliste i þe apocalipse hit is a dearne healewi þet namon ne cnaweþ þet naveþ hit ismecchet þis smech ant tis cnawunge kimeþ of gastelich sihþe of gastelich herunge of gastelich speche þet ha schulen habben þe forgaþ for godes luve worldliche herunges eorþliche spechen fleschliche sihþen ant efter þet sihþe þet is nu dosc her ȝe schulen habbe þe ruppe þe brihte sihþe of godes neb þet alle gleadunge is of i þe blisse of heovene muche bivore þe oþre for þe rihtwise godd hit haveþ swa idemet þet euchanes mede þer ondswerie aȝein þe swinc ant aȝeines þe ennu þet ha her for his luve eadmodliche þolieþ forþi hit is semlich þet ancren þeos twa marheȝeoven habben bivoren oþre swiftnesse ant leome of a briht sihþe swiftnes aȝeines þet ha beoþ nu swa bipinnet leome of briht sihþe aȝeines þet ha her þeostriþ nu hamseolven ne nulleþ nowþer iseo mon ne of mon beon isehene alle þeo in heovene schule beon ase swifte as is nu monnes þoht as is þe sunne gleam þe smit from est into west as þe ehe openeþ ah ancres bisperret her schulen beo þer ȝef ei mei lihtre ba ant swiftre ant i se wide schakeles as me seiþ pleien in heovene large lesewen þet te bodi schal beon hwerseeaver þe gast wule in an hondhwile þis is nu þe an marheȝeove þet ich seide ancren schulden habben bivoren oþre þe oþer is of sihþe alle þeo in heovene seoþ i godd alle þing ant ancren schule brihtluker for hare blindfellunge her iseon ant understonde þer godes dearne runes ant his derve domes þe ne kepeþ nu to witen of þinges wiþuten wiþ eare ne wiþ ehe forþi mine leove sustren ȝef ei mon bit to seon ow easkiþ him hwet god þerof mahte lihten for moni uvel ich iseo þe rin ant nane biheve ȝef he is meadles leveþ him þe wurse ȝef ei wurþeþ swa awed þet he warpe hond forþ toward te þurl claþ swiftliche ananriht schutteþ al þet þurl to ant leoteþ him iwurþen alswa sone se eaver eani feleþ into ei luþer speche þet falle toward ful luve sperreþ þe þurl ananriht ne ondswerie ȝe him nawiht ah wendeþ awei wiþ þis vers þet he hit mahe iheren ant gaþ bivoren ower weoved wiþ þe ne chastie ȝe na swuch mon neaver on oþer wise for in wiþ þe chastiement he mahte ondswerie swa ant blawen se liþeliche þet sum sperke mahte acwikien na wohlech nis se culvert as o pleinte wise as hwase þus seide ich nalde forte þolie deaþ þenche fulþe toward te ant swereþ deope aþes ah þah ich hefde isworen hit luvien ich mot te hwa is wurse þen me moni slep hit binimeþ me nu me is wa þet tu hit wast ah forȝef me nu þet ich habbe hit itald te þah ich schule wurþe wod ne schalt tu neaver mare witen hu me stonde ha hit forȝeveþ him for he spekeþ se feire speokeþ þenne of oþerhwet ah eaver is þe ehe to þe wude lehe eaver is þe heorte i þe earre speche ȝet hwen he is forþe ha went in hire þoht ofte swucche wordes hwen ha schulde oþerhwet ȝeornliche ȝemen he eft secheþ his point forte breoke foreward swereþ he mot nede ant swa waxeþ þet wa se lengre se wurse for na feondschipe nis se uvel as is fals freondschipe feond þe þuncheþ freond is sweoke over alle forþi mine leove sustren ne ȝeove ȝe to swuch mon nan inȝong to speokene for as hali writ seiþ hare speche spreat ase cancre ah for alle ondsweres wendeþ ow frommard him alswa as ich seide þeruppe sawvin owseolven ne maten him betere ne mahe ȝe o nane wise lokiþ nu hu propreliche þe leafdi i godes deore spuse leareþ ow bi hire sahe hu ȝe schule seggen low ha seiþ hercne ich ihere mi leof speoken he cleopeþ me ich mot gan ant ȝe gan ananriht to ower deore leofmon ant meaneþ ow to his earen þe luveliche cleopeþ ow to him wiþ þes wordes þet is aris up hihe þe heonewart ant cum to me mi leofmon mi culvre mi feire ant mi schene spuse schaw to me þi leove neb ant ti lufsume leor went te from oþre sei hwa haveþ ido þe hwa haveþ ihurt mi deore sing i mine earen forþi þet tu ne wilnest bute to seo mi wlite ne speoke bute to me þi stevene is me swete ant ti wlite schene þis beoþ nu twa þinges þe beoþ iluvet swiþe swete speche ant schene wlite hwase ham haveþ togederes swucche cheoseþ to leofmon ant to spuse ȝef þu wult swuch beon ne schaw þu na mon þi wlite ne ne leote bliþeliche here þi speche ah turn ham ba to to þi deorewurþe spus as he bit þe ruppe as þu wult þet ti speche þunche him swete ant ti wlite schene ant habben him to leofmon þet is þusentfald schenre þen þe sunne hercniþ nu ȝeornliche mine leove sustren al anoþer speche ant frommard tis earre hercniþ nu hu spekeþ as o wreaþþe ant seiþ as o grim hoker ant o scarn to þe ancre þe schulde beon his leofmon ant secheþ þah gealunge utward ant frovre wiþ ehe oþer wiþ tunge þis beoþ þe wordes ȝef þu ne cnawest teseolf þu feier bimong wummen wend ut ant ga efter gateheorden ant lesewe þine tichnes bi heordemenne hulen of ris ant of leaves þis is a cruel word a grim word mid alle þet ure laverd seiþ as o grome ant o scarn to totinde ant to hercwile ant to speokele ancres hit is bileppet ant ihud ah ich hit wulle unvalden ȝef þu ne cnawest teseolf he seiþ ure laverd neomeþ nu gode ȝeme þet is ȝef þu nast hwas spuse þu art þet tu art cwen of heovene ȝef þu art me treowe as spuse ah to beonne ȝef þu þis havest forȝeten ant telest herof to lutel wend ut ant ga he seiþ hwider ut of þis hehschipe of þis muchele menske ant folhe heorde of geat he seiþ hwet beoþ heorde of geat þet beoþ flesches lustes þe stinkeþ ase geat doþ bivoren ure laverd ȝef þu havest forȝete nu þi wurþfule leafdischipe ga ant folhe þeos geat folhe flesches lustes nu kimeþ þe refter ant lesewe þine tichnes þet is as he seide fed tine ehnen wiþ uttotunge þi tunge wiþ chaflunge þine earen wiþ spellunge þi nease wiþ smeallunge þi flesch wiþ softe felunge þeos fif wittes he cleopeþ tichnes for alswa as of a ticchen þet haveþ swete flesch kimeþ a stinkinde gat oþer a ful bucke al riht alswa of a ȝung swete locunge oþer of a swote herunge oþer of a softe felunge waxeþ a stincinde lust ant a ful sunne hweþer ei totilde ancre fondede eaver þis þe beakeþ eaver utward as untohe brid i cage hweþer þe cat of helle cahte eaver towart hire ant lahte wiþ his cleavres hire heorte heved ȝe soþes ant droh ut al þe bodi efter wiþ clokes of crokede ant kene fondunges ant makede hire to leosen baþe godd ant mon wiþ brad scheome ant sunne ant bireafde hire ed an cleap þe eorþe ant ec þe heovene inoh sari lure to wraþer heale beakede eaver swa ut ancre he seiþ o grome ga ut as dude dyne dohter to himmere heile hire to wraþer heale þet is to seggen leaf me ant mi cunfort þet is inwiþ þi breoste ant ga sech wiþuten þe worldes frakele frovre þe schal endin eaver i sar ant i sorhe tac þerto ant leaf me hwen þe swa is leovere for ne schalt tu nanesweis þes ilke twa cunforz min ant te worldes þe joie of þe hali gast ant ec flesches frovre habbe togederes cheos nu an of þes twa for þe oþer þu most leten ȝef þu ne cnawest teseolf þu feier bimong wummen seiþ ure laverd þu feier bimong wummen ȝe nu her do þerto þet schalt ant tu wel wulle elles hwer beo feier nawt ane bimong wummen ah bimong engles þu mi wurþli spuse seiþ ure laverd schalt tu folhin geat o feld þet beoþ flesches lustes feld is willes breade schalt tu o þis wise folhi geat ȝont te feld þe schuldest i þin heorte bur biseche me cosses as mi leofmon þet seiþ to me i þet luveboc þet is cusse me mi leofmon wiþ þe coss of his muþ muþene swetest þis coss leove sustren is a swetnesse ant a delit of heorte swa unimete swete þet euch worldes savur is bitter þertoȝeines ah ure laverd wiþ þis coss ne cusseþ na sawle þe luveþ ei þing buten him ant te ilke þinges for him þe helpeþ him to habben ant tu þenne godes spuse þet maht heren herbivoren hu sweteliche þi spus spekeþ ant cleopeþ þe to him se luveliche þe refter hu he went te lof ant spekeþ swiþe grimliche ȝef þu ut wendest hald te i þi chambre ne fed tu nawt wiþuten þine gate tichnes ah hald wiþinnen þin hercnunge þi speche ant ti sihþe ant tun feaste hare ȝeten muþ ant ehe ant eare for nawt ha beoþ bilokene inwiþ wah oþer wal þe þes ȝeten openiþ bute aȝein godes sonde ant liveneþ of sawle over alle þing þenne as þe leareþ ant ich seide feor bivoren i þe frumþe of þis dale mine leove sustren witeþ ower heorte þe heorte is wel iloket ȝef muþ ant ehe ant eare wisliche beon ilokene for heo as ich seide þer beoþ þe heorte wardeins ant ȝef þe wardeins wendeþ ut þe ham biþ biwist uvele þis beoþ nu þe þreo wittes þet ich habbe ispeken of speoke we nu scheortliche of þe twa oþre þah nis nawt speche þe muþes wit ah is smechunge þah ba beon i muþe smeal of nease is þe feorþe of þe fif wittes of þis wit seiþ seint of smealles he seiþ ne fondi ich nawt mucheles ȝef ha beoþ neh o godes half ȝef feor me ne recche ure laverd þah þurh þreateþ ham wiþ helle stench þe habbeþ delit her i fleschliche smealles þertoȝeines ha schulen habben heovenliche smealles þe habbeþ her of irnes swat oþer of heren þet ha beoreþ oþer of swati hettren oþer of þicke eir in hire hus ant muhlinde þinges stench oþerhwiles ant strong breaþ i nease þerof beoþ iwarnet mine leove sustren þet oþerhwile þe feond makeþ sum þing to stinken þet ȝe schulden notien forþi þet he walde þet ȝe hit schulden schunien oþerhwile þe wiheleare of sum dearne þing þet ȝe ne mahe nawt iseon as dust of dearne sedes makeþ a swote smeal cumen as þah hit were of heovene for ȝe schulden wenen þet godd for ower hali lif sende ow his elne ant leote wel to ow seolf ant leapen into prude smeal þe kimeþ o godes half frovreþ þe heorte mare þen þe nease þeos ant oþre truiles þet he bitruileþ monie schulen beon ibroht to nawt wiþ haliweater ant wiþ þe hali rodetaken hwase þohte hu godd seolf wes i þis wit idervet ha walde þe derf þe rof þuldeliche þolien i þe munt of calvarie þer ure laverd hongede wes þe cwalmstowe þer leien ofte licomes irotet buven eorþe ant stunken swiþe stronge he as he hongede mahte habben hare breaþ wiþ al his oþer wa riht amidden his nease alswa as he wes idervet in alle his oþre wittes in his sihþe þa he seh his deore wurþe moder teares ant sein ewangeliste ant te oþre ant þa he biheold hu his deore deciples fluhen alle from him ant leafden him ane he weop him seolve þrien wiþ his feire ehnen he þolede al þuldeliche þet me him blindfeallede hwen his ehnen weren þus i schendlac iblintfeallet forte ȝeove þe ancre þe brihte sihþe of heovene þah þu þine ehnen for his luve ant i munegunge þe rof blintfealli on eorþe to beoren him feolahreadden nis na muche wunder amid þe muþ me gurde him sumcheare inohreaþe as me tobeot his cheken ant spitte him o scarne ant an ancre is for a word ut of hire witte hwen he þolede þuldeliche þet te giws dutten as ha buffeteden him his deorewurþe muþ wiþ hare dreori fustes ant tu for þe luve of him ant for þin ahne muchele biheve þi tutelinde muþ dute wiþ þine lippen teke þet he smahte galle on his tunge forte learen ancre þet ha ne grucchi neaver mare for na mete ne for na drunch ne beo hit swa unorne ȝef ha hit mei eoten eote ant þonki godd ȝeorne ȝef ha ne mei nawt beo sari þet ha mot sechen estfulre ah ear þen þet biddunge areare eani scandle ear deie martir in hire meoseise deaþ me ah forte fleon ase forþ as me mei wiþute sunne ah me schal ear deien þen me do eani heaved sunne ant nis hit muche sunne to makien þet me segge estful is þeos ancre muchel is þet ha bid ȝet is wurse ȝef me seiþ þet ha is grucchilit ant fulitohe ant erveþ forte paien were ha imid te world ha moste beo sumchearre ipaiet inohreaþe mid leasse ant mid wurse muchel hofles hit is cumen into ancrehus into godes prisun willes ant waldes to stude of meoseise for te sechen eise þe rin ant meistrie ant leafdischipe mare þen ha mahte habben inoh reaþe ihaved i þe worlde þenc ancre hwet tu sohtest þa þu forsoke þe world i þi biclusunge biwepen þine ahne ant oþres sunnen ant forleosen alle þe blissen of þis lif forte cluppen blisfulliche þi blisfule leofmon i þe eche lif of heovene o seiþ sein o wei lawei weilawei hu is gold iþeostret hu is feherest heow biturnd ant forweolewet þe apostle spekeþ to swucche grimliche as o wreaþþe me hwuch unseli gast haveþ swa bimalscret ow þet ȝe i gast bigunnen ant i flesch wulleþ endin þe gastelich lif bigunnen i þe hali gast beoþ bicumene al fleschliche al fleschliche i wurþen lahinde lihte ilatet ane hwile lihte iwordet anoþer luþere iwordet estfule ant sarcurne ant grucchildes meanildes ant ȝet þet wurse is cursildes ant chidildes bittre ant attrie wiþ heorte tobollen bihofde nawt þet swuch were leafdi of castel hoker ant hofles þing is þet a smiret ancre ant ancre biburiet for hwet is ancrehus bute hire burinesse ant heo schal beo greattre ibollen leafdiluker leoten of þen a leafdi of hames ȝef ha makeþ hire wraþ aȝeines gult of sunne ha shulde setten hire wordes swa efne þet ha ne þunche oversturet ne nawt ilead over skile ah inwardliche ant soþliche wiþuten hihþe ant hehschipe in a softe stevene þis is sahe þet hit limpe to ei of ow godd ne leve neaver cang dohter iwurþ as mone i wonunge þriveþ as þe cangun se lengre se wurse ȝe as ȝe wulleþ waxen ant nawt wenden hindward sikerliche ȝe moten rowen aȝein stream wiþ muchel swinc breoken forþ ant gasteliche earmes stealewurþliche sturien ant swa ȝe moten alle for alle we beoþ i þis stream i þe worldes wode weater þe bereþ adun monie sone se we eaver wergiþ ant resteþ us i slawþe ure bat geaþ hindward ant we beoþ þe cang dohter þe gaþ woniende þe wlecche þe godd speoweþ as is iwriten herefter þe bigunnen i gast ant i flesch endiþ nai nai ah as seiþ þe delveþ efter golþord eaver se he mare nahheþ hit se his heortes gleadschipe makeþ him mare lusti ant mare fersch to diggin ant delven deoppre ant deoppre aþet he hit finde ower heorte nis nawt on eorþe for þi ne þurve ȝe nawt delven dunewardes ah heoven uppart þe heorte for þet is þe uprowunge aȝein þis worldes stream driven hire aȝeinward to delven þe golþord þet up is in heovene ant hwet is þet delvunge ȝeornful sechinde þoht hwer hit beo hwuch hit beo hu me hit mahe ifinden þis is þe delvunge beon bisiliche ant ȝeornfulliche eaver herabuten wiþ anewil ȝirnunge wiþ heate of hungri heorte waden up of unþeawes creopen ut of flesch breoken up over hire astihen up on ow seolf wiþ heh þoht toward heovene swa muchel þe neodeluker þet ower feble tendre flesch heardes ne mei þolien nu þenne þeraȝein ȝeoveþ godd ower heorte i softnesse i swetnesse in alles cunnes meoknesse ant softest eadmodnesse nawt nu granin ant peonsin þe refter hehi stevene wreaþen hire unweneliche sinetin hire wordes wrenchen aweiward wenden þe schuldre keaste þe heaved swa þet godd heateþ hire ant mon hire scarneþ nai nai ripe wordes lates ripe ant werkes bilimpeþ to ancre hwen wordes beoþ eadmodliche ant soþfestliche iseide nawt fulitoheliche ne babanliche þenne habbeþ ha burþerne to beo riht understonden nu is þis al iseid þet ȝe efter þe me gurde ine muþ ant galle ȝef to drinken wiþ muþes sunne witen ow ant þolieþ sum derf i þet wit as he wes þe rin idervet in his eare he hefde þe heovenliche laverd al þe edwit ant te upbrud al þe scarn ant al þe scheome þet eare mahte iheren ant he seiþ bi himseolf us forte learen ich heold me he seiþ stille as dumbe ant deaf deþ þet naveþ nan ondswere þah me him misdo oþer missegge þis is þi leofmonnes sahe ant tu seli ancre þe art his leove spuse leorne hit ȝeorne of him þet tu hit cunne ant mahe soþliche seggen nu ich habbe ispeken of ower fowre wittes ant of godes fowre hu he þurh hise frovreþ ow as ofte as ȝe in ower feleþ eani weane nu hercniþ of þe fifte þet is meast neod elne for þe pine is meast þe rin þet is i felunge ant te licunge alswa ȝef hit swa turneþ þe fifte wit is felunge þis ilke an wit is in alle þe oþre ant ȝont al þe licome ant forþi hit is neod to habben best warde ure laverd wiste hit wel ant forþi he walde meast i þet wit þolien al forte frovrin us ȝef we þolieþ wa þe rin ant forte wenden us frommard te licunge þet flesches lust easkeþ nomeliche i felunge mare þen in oþre ure laverd i þis wit nefde nawt in a stude ah hefde over al pine nawt ane ȝond al his bodi ah hefde ȝet inwiþ in his seli sawle in hire he felde þe stiche of sari sorhe ant sorhful þet dude him sike sare þis stiche wes þreovald þe ase þreo speren smat him to þe heorte þe an wes his modres wop ant te oþre þe flowen o teares þe oþer þet his ahne deore deciples ne lefden him na mare ne ne heolden for godd forþi þet he ne healp himseolf in his muchele pine ant fluhen alle from him ant leafden him as fremede þe þridde wes þet muchele sar ant te ofþunchunge þet he hefde inwiþ him of hare forlorenesse þe drohen him to deaþe þet he seh onont ham al his swinc forloren þet he swonc on eorþe þeos ilke þreo stichen weren in his sawle in his licome euch lim as seint seiþ þolede sundri pine ant deide ȝond al his bodi as he ear ȝond al his bodi deaþes swat sweatte ant her seiþ sein þet he ne weop nawt ane wiþ ehnen ah dude as wiþ alle his limen for se ful of angoisse wes þet ilke nedswat þet lihte of his licome aȝein þe angoisuse deaþ þet he schulde þolien þet hit þuhte read blod on oþer half swa largeliche ant swa swiþe fleaw þet ilke blodi swat of his blisfule bodi þet te streames urnen dun to þer eorþe swuch grure hefde his monliche flesch aȝein þe derve pinen þet hit schulde drehen þet nes na feorlich wunder for eaver se flesch is cwickre se þe reopunge þe rof ant te hurt is sarre a lutel hurt i þe ehe derveþ mare þen deþ a muchel i þe hele for þe flesch is deaddre euch monnes flesch is dead flesch aȝein þet wes godes flesch as þet te wes inumen of þe tendre meiden ant na þing neaver nes þe rin þet hit adeadede ah eaver wes iliche cwic of þet cwike goddhead þe wunede þe rinne forþi in his flesch wes þe pine sarre þen eaver eani mon in his flesch þolede þet his flesch wes cwic over alle flesches lo hwuc an essample a mon for uvel þet he haveþ ne let him nawt blod o þe seke halve ah deþ þe hale to heale þe seke ah in al þe world þe wes o þe fevre nes bimong al mon cun an hal dale ifunden þe mahte beon ilete blod bute godes bodi ane þe lette him blod o rode nawt o þe earm ane ah dude o fif halve forte healen moncun of þe secnesse þet te fif wittes hefden awakenet þus lo þe hale half ant te cwike dale droh þet uvele blod ut frommard te unhale ant healde swa þe seke þurh blod is in hali writ sunne bitacnet þe reisuns hwi beoþ efter sutelliche ischawet ah þerof neomeþ ȝeme mine leove sustren þet ower deorewurþe spus þe luvewurþe laverd þe healent of heovene godd godes sune þe wealdent of al þe world þa he wes þus ilete blod understondeþ þet dei hwuch wes his diete i þe ilke blodletunge se baleful ant se bitter þe ilke þet he bledde fore ne brohten ha him to present ne win ne ale ne weater ȝet þa he seide ant meande as he bledde of þurst o þe rode ah duden bitter galle hwer wes eaver iȝeven to eani blodleten se povre pitance ant tah ne gruchede he nawt ah underveng hit eadmodliche forte learen hise ant ȝet he dude mare us to forbisne dude his deore muþ þerto ant smahte þe rof þah he hit notie ne mahte hwa is þenne efter þis ant ancre hure ant hure þe gruccheþ ȝef ha naveþ nawt oþer mete oþer drunch efter hire eise ant siker hwase gruccheþ ha offreþ ȝet ure laverd his luþere pitance as duden þa þe giws ant is giwes fere to beoden him in his þurst drunch of sur galle his þurst nis bute ȝirnunge of ure sawle heale ant grucchunge of bitter ant of sur heorte is him surre ant bittrure nu þen wes þa þe galle ant tu his deore spuse ne beo þu nawt giwes make forte birlin him swa ah ber him feolahreadden ant drinc wiþ him bliþeliche al þet ti flesch þuncheþ sur oþer bitter þet is pine ant wone ant alle meoseises ant he hit wule þe ȝelden as his treowe fere wiþ healewi of heovene þus wes þe almihti godd in alle his fif wittes derfliche ipinet ant nomeliche i þis leaste þet is i felunge for his flesch wes al cwic as is þe tendre ehe ant ȝe witen þis wit þet is flesches felunge over alle þe oþre godes honden weren ineilet o rode þurh þe ilke neiles ich halsi ow ancres nawt ow ah do oþre for hit nis na neod mine leove sustren haldeþ ower honden inwiþ ower þurles hondlunge oþer ei felunge bitweone mon ant ancre is þing swa uncumelich ant dede se scheomelich ant se naket sunne to al þe world se eatelich ant se muche scandle þet nis na neod to speoken ne writen þertoȝeines for al wiþute writunge þet ful is to etscene godd hit wat as me were muche deale leovere þet ich isehe ow alle þreo mine leove sustren wummen me leovest hongin on a gibet forte wiþbuhe sunne þen ich sehe an of ow ȝeoven anlepi cos eani mon on eorþe swa as ich meane ich am stille of þet mare nawt ane monglin honden ah putten hond utward bute hit beo for nede is wohunge efter godes grome ant tollunge of his eorre hireseolf bihalden hire ahne hwite honden deþ hearm moni ancre þe haveþ ham to feire as þeo þe beoþ foridlet ha schulden schrapien euche dei þe eorþe up of hare put þet ha schulen rotien in godd hit wat þet put deþ muche god moni ancre for as seiþ þeo þe haveþ eaver hire deaþ as bivoren hire ehnen þet te put munegeþ ȝef þet ha þencheþ wel o þe dom of domesdei þer þe engles schule cwakien ant te eche ant te eateliche pinen of helle ant over al ant al o passiun hu he wes ipinet as is sumdeal iseid in alle his fif wittes lihtliche nule ha nawt folhi flesches licunge efter willes lust ne drahen in toward hire nan heaved sunne wiþ hire fif wittes þis is nu inoh iseid of þe fif wittes þe beoþ ase wardein wiþuten of þe heorte þet sawle lif is inne as we seiden þeruppe on earst þet seide nu beoþ have þonc þe twa dalen overcumen ga we nu wiþ his help upo þe þridde mine leove sustren alswa as ȝe witeþ wel ower wittes utewiþ alswa over alle þing lokiþ þet ȝe beon inwiþ softe ant milde ant eadmode swete ant swote iheortet ant þolemode aȝein woh of word þet me seiþ ow ant werc þet me misdeþ ow leste ȝe al leosen aȝein bittre ancres daviþ seiþ þis vers ich am he seiþ as pellican þe wuneþ bi him ane pellican is a fuhel se weamod ant se wreaþful þet hit sleaþ ofte o grome his ahne briddes hwen ha doþ him teone ant þenne sone þe refter hit wurþ swiþe sari ant makeþ swiþe muche man ant smit himseolf wiþ his bile þet he sloh ear his briddes wiþ ant draheþ blod of his breoste ant wiþ þet blod acwikeþ eft his briddes isleine þis fuhel pellican is þe weamode ancre hire briddes beoþ hire gode werkes þet ha sleaþ ofte wiþ bile of scharp wreþþe ah hwen ha swa haveþ idon do as deþ þe pellican ofþunche hit swiþe sone ant wiþ hire ahne bile beaki hire breoste þet is wiþ schrift of hire muþ þet ha sunegede wiþ ant sloh hire gode werkes drahe þet blod of sunne ut of hire breoste þet is of þe heorte þet sawle lif is inne ant swa schulen eft acwikien hire isleine briddes þet beoþ hire gode werkes blod bitacneþ sunne for alswa as a mon bibled is grislich ant eatelich i monnes ehe alswa is þe sunfule bivore godes ehe on oþer half namon ne mei juggi wel blod ear hit beo icolet alswa is of sunne hwil þe heorte walleþ inwiþ of wreaþþe nis þer na riht dom oþer hwil þe lust is hat toward eani sunne ne maht tu nawt te hwiles deme wel hwet hit is ne hwet ter wule cumen of ah let lust overgan ant hit te wule likin let þet hate acolin as deþ þe wule iuggi blod ant tu schalt demen ariht þe sunne ful ant ladlich þet te þuhte feier ant uvel se muchel cumen þe rof ȝef þu hit hefdest idon hwil þet hate leaste þet tu schalt deme wod teseolf þa þu þertoward þohtest þis is of euch sunne soþ hwi blod hit bitacneþ ant nomeliche of wreaþþe wreaþþe hit seiþ hwil hit least ablindeþ swa þe heorte þet ha ne mei soþ icnawen wreaþþe is a forschuppilt as me teleþ i spelles for ha reaveþ mon his wit ant changeþ al his chere ant forschuppeþ him from mon into beastes cunde wummon wraþ is wulvene mon wulf oþer liun oþer unicorne hwil þet eaver wreaþþe is i wummone heorte versaili segge hire ures ne deþ ha bute þeoteþ naveþ ha bute as þeo þet is iwent to wulvene i godes ehnen wulvene stevene in his lihte earen wreaþþe is a wodschipe wraþ mon nis he wod hu lokeþ he hu spekeþ he hu feareþ his heorte inwiþ hwucche beoþ utewiþ alle hise lates he ne cnaweþ namon hu is he mon þenne mon cundelich is milde sone se he leoseþ mildheortnesse he leoseþ monnes cunde ant wreaþþe þe forschuppilt forschuppeþ him into beast as ich ear seide ant hwet ȝef eni ancre spuse is forschuppet into wulvene nis þet muche sorhe nis þer bute sone forwarpe þet ruhe fel abute þe heorte ant wiþ softe sahtnesse makien hire smeþe ant softe as is cundeliche wummone hude for wiþ þet wulvene fel na þing þet ha deþ nis gode licwurþe lo her aȝeines wreaþþe monie remedies frovren a muche floc ant misliche boten ȝef me misseiþ þe þench þet tu art eorþe ne totret me eorþe ne bispit me eorþe þah me dude swa bi þe me dude þe eorþe rihte ȝef þu berkest aȝein þu art hundes cunnes ȝef þu stingest aȝein þu art neddre cundel ant nawt spuse þench dude he swa efter alle þe schendfule pinen þet he þolede o þe longe friniht me leadde him ine marhen to hongin o wearitreo ant driven þurh his fowr limen irnene neiles ah na mare þen a schep as þe hali writ seiþ cwich ne cweþ he neaver þench ȝet on oþer half hwet is word bute wind to wac ha is istrengþet þet a windes puf a word mei afellen ant warpen into sunne ant hwa nule þunche wunder of ancre windfeallet on oþer half ȝetten ne schaweþ ha þet ha is dust ant unstable þing þe wiþ a lute wordes wind is anan toblawen þe ilke puf of his muþ ȝef þu hit wurpe under þe hit schulde beore þe uppart toward te blisse of heovene ah nu is muche wunder of ure muchele meadschipe understondeþ þis word seint mahte þolien þet te hearde rode heve him toward heovene ant luveliche biclupte hire sein alswa þolede þet te gridil heve him uppardes wiþ bearninde gleden seinte stefne þolede þe stanes þet me sende him ant underveng ham gleadliche ant bed for ham þe ham senden him wiþ hommen ifalden ant we ne mahe nawt þolien þet te wind of a word beore us towart heovene ah beoþ wode aȝeines ham þe we schulden þonkin as þe ilke þe serviþ us of muche servise þah hit beo hare unþonkes al þet te unwreaste ant te uvele deþ for uvel al is þe gode to god al is his biheve ant timbrunge toward blisse let him ant þet gleadliche breide þi crune þench hu þe hali mon i custe ant blescede þe oþres hond þe hefde him ihearmet ant seide se inwardliche cussinde hire ȝeorne iblescet beo eaver þeos hond for ha haveþ itimbret me þe blissen of heovene ant tu segge alswa bi hond þe misdeþ þe ant bi þe muþ alswa þe ewt misseiþ þe iblescet beo þi muþ sei for þu makest lome þe rof to timbri mi crune wel me is for mi god ant wa þah for þin uvel for þu dest me freame ant hearmest teseolven ȝef ei mon oþer wummon misseide oþer misdude ow mine leove sustren swa ȝe schulden seggen ah nu is muche wunder ȝef we wel bihaldeþ hu godes halhen þoleden wunden on hare bodi ant we beoþ wode ȝef a wind blawe a lutel toward us ant te wind ne wundeþ nawt bute þe eir ane for nowþer ne mei þe wind þet is þet word þet me seiþ ne wundi þe i þi flesch ne fule þi sawle þah hit puffe upo þe bute þe seolf hit makie wel þu maht underȝeoten þet ter wes lute fur of chearite þet leiteþ al of ure
