laverdes luve lute fur wes þer þet a puf acwencte for þear as muche fur is hit waxeþ wiþ winde aȝein misdede oþer missahe lo her on ende þe beste remedie ant cunneþ þis essample a mon þe leie i prisun oþer ahte muche rancun ne o nane wise ne schulde ut bute hit were to hongin ear he hefde his rancun fulleliche ipaiet nalde he cunne god þonc a mon þe duste uppon him of peonehes a bigurdel forte reimin him wiþ ant lesen him of pine þah he wurpe hit ful hearde aȝeines his heorte al þe hurd were forȝeten for þe gleadnesse o þis ilke wise we beoþ alle i prisun her ant ahen godd greate deattes of sunne forþi we ȝeiȝeþ to him i þe laverd we seggeþ forȝef us ure deattes alswa as we forȝeoveþ ure deatturs woh þet me deþ us oþer of word oþer of werc þet is ure rancun þet we schule reimin us wiþ ant cwitin ure deattes toward ure laverd þet beoþ ure sunnen for wiþute cwitance up of þis prisun nis nan inumen þet nis anan ahonget oþer i purgatoire oþer i þe pine of helle ant ure laverd seolf seiþ forȝef ant ich forȝeove þe as þah he seide þu art endeattet toward me swiþe wiþ sunnen ah wult tu god foreward al þet eaver ei mon misseiþ þe oþer misdeþ þe ich wulle neomen onward þe deatte þe þu ahest me nu þenne þah a word culle þe ful hearde upo þe breoste ant as þe þuncheþ on earst hurte þin heorte þench as þe prisun walde þe þe oþer hurte sare wiþ þe bigurdel ant underveng hit gleadliche forte acwiti þe wiþ ant þonke þe þe hit sent te þah godd ne cunne him neaver þonc of his sonde he hearmeþ him ant freameþ þe ȝef þu hit const þolien for as daviþ seiþ swiþe wel wiþ alle godd deþ in his tresor þe unwreaste ant te uvele forte hure wiþ ham as me deþ wiþ gersum þeo þe wel fehteþ eft upon oþer half pellican þis fuhel haveþ anoþer cunde þet hit is aa leane forþi as ich seide daviþ eveneþ him þerto in ancre persone in ancre stevene ich am pellican ilich þe wuneþ bi him ane ant ancre ah þus to seggen ant beon ilich pellican onond þet hit is leane bitund inne as hit teleþ in hire boc leadde swiþe heard lif feaste ant werede here bitund inne bitacneþ bitund ancre þe ah to leaden heard lif as dude þe leafdi efter hire evene nawt ase swin ipund i sti to feattin ant to greatin aȝein þe cul of þe axe twa cunnes ancren beoþ þet ure laverd spekeþ of ant seiþ i þe godspel of false ant of treowe þet is foxes habbeþ hare holen ant briddes of heovene habbeþ hare nestes þe foxes beoþ false ancres ase fox is beast falsest þeose habbeþ he seiþ holen þe holieþ inward eorþe wiþ eorþliche unþeawes ant draheþ into hare hole al þet ha mahen reopen ant rinnen þus beoþ gederinde ancres of godd i þe godspel to voxes ievenet fox ec is a frech beast ant freotewil mid alle ant te false ancre draheþ into hire hole ant fret ase fox deþ baþe ges ant hennen habbeþ efter þe vox a simple semblant sumchearre ant beoþ þah ful of gile makieþ ham oþre þen ha beoþ ase vox þe is ypocrite weneþ forte gili godd as ha bidweolieþ simple men ant giliþ meast hamseolven gealstriþ as þe vox deþ ant ȝelpeþ of hare god hwerse ha durren ant mahen chaffliþ of idel ant se swiþe worltliche iwurþeþ þet on ende hare nome stinkeþ as fox þer he geaþ forþ for ȝef ha doþ uvele me seiþ bi ham wurse þeos eoden into ancrehus as dude saul into hole nawt as daviþ þe gode ba ha wenden into hole saul ant daviþ as hit teleþ i ah saul wende þider in forte don his fulþe þe rin as deþ bimong monie sum unseli ancrewent into hole of ancre hus to bifule þet stude ant don dearnluker þe rin fleschliche fulþen þen ha mahten ȝef ha weren amidde þe worlde for hwa haveþ mare eise to don hire cweadschipes þen þe false ancre þus wende saul into hole to bidon þet stude ah daviþ wende þider in ane forte huden him from saul þet him heatede ant sohte to sleanne swa deþ þe gode ancre þe saul þet is þe feond heateþ ant hunteþ efter ha deþ hire in to huden hire from hise kene clokes ha hud hire in hire hole ba from worltliche men ant worltliche sunnen ant forþi ha is gasteliche daviþ þet is strong toȝein þe feond ant hire leor lufsum to ure laverdes ehnen for swa muchel seiþ þis word daviþ on ebreische ledene þe false ancre is saul efter þet his nome seiþ for saul on ebreisch is misnotunge on englisch ant te false ancre misnoteþ ancre nome ant al þet ha wurcheþ þe gode ancre is as we ear seiden þet is bitund as heo wes ant alswa as heo dude feasteþ wakeþ swinkeþ ant wereþ hearde ha is of þe briddes þet ure laverd spekeþ of efter þe voxes þe wiþ hare lustes ne holieþ nawt duneward ase doþ þe voxes þet beoþ false ancres ah habbeþ on heh ase brid of heovene iset hare nestes þet is hare reste treowe ancres beoþ briddes icleopede for ha leaveþ þe eorþeþet is þe luve of alle worltliche þinges ant þurh ȝirnunge of heorte to heovenliche þinges fleoþ uppart toward heovene ant tah ha fleon hehe wiþ heh lif ant hali haldeþ þah þe heaved lah þurh milde eadmodnesse as brid fleonninde buheþ þet heaved leoteþ al noht wurþ þet ha wel wurcheþ ant seggeþ as ure laverd learde alle hise hwen ȝe al habbeþ wel i don he seiþ ure laverd seggeþ þet ȝe beoþ unnete þrealles fleoþ hehe ant haldeþ þah þet heaved eaver lahe þe wengen þe uppard beoreþ ham þet beoþ gode þeawes þet ha moten sturien into gode werkes as brid hwen hit fleo wule stureþ hise wengen þe treowe ancres ȝetten þe we to briddes eveniþ nawt we þah ah deþ godd ha spreadeþ hare wengen ant makieþ creoiz of hamseolf as brid deþ hwen hit fliþ þet is i þoht of heorte ant i bitternesse of flesch beoreþ godes rode þeo briddes fleoþ wel þe habbeþ lutel flesch as þe pellican haveþ ant feole fiþeren þe strucion for his muchele flesch ant oþre swucche fuheles makieþ a semblant to fleon ant beateþ þe wengen ah þe vet eaver draheþ to þer eorþe alswa fleschlich ancre þe liveþ i flesches lustes ant folheþ hire eise þe hevinesse of hire flesch ant flesches unþeawes bineomeþ hire hire fluht ant tah ha makie semblant ant muche nurþ wiþ wengen oþres nawt hiren þet is leote of as þah ha fluhe ant were an hali ancre hwase ȝeorne bihalt lahheþ hire to bismere for hire vet eaver as doþ þe strucions þet beoþ hire lustes draheþ to þer eorþe þeos ne beoþ nawt ilich þe leane fuhel pellican ne ne fleoþ nawt on heh ah beoþ eorþbriddes ant nisteþ on eorþe ah godd cleopeþ þe gode ancres briddes of heovene as ich ear seide foxes habbeþ hare holen ant briddes of heovene habbeþ hare nestes treowe ancres beoþ ariht briddes of heovene þe fleoþ on heh ant sitteþ singinde murie o þe grene bohes þet is þencheþ uppart of þe blisse of heovene þe neaver ne faleweþ ah is aa grene ant sitteþ o þis grene singinde murie þet is resteþ ham i þulli þoht ant ase þeo þe singeþ habbeþ murhþe of heorte brid tah oþerhwile forte sechen his mete for þe flesches neode lihteþ to þer eorþe ah hwil hit sit on eorþe hit nis neaver siker ah biwent him ofte ant bilokeþ him aa ȝeornliche abuten alswa þe gode ancre ne fleo ha neaver se hehe ha mot lihten oþerhwiles dun to þer eorþe of hire bodi eoten drinken slepen wurchen speoken heren of þet hire neodeþ to of eorþliche þinges ah þenne as þe brid deþ ha mot wel biseon hire bilokin hire on euch half þet ha nohwer ne misneome leste ha beo icaht þurh sum of þe deofles grunen oþer ihurt summesweis þe hwil ha sit se lahe þeos briddes habbeþ nestes he seiþ ure laverd nest is heard utewiþ of prikinde þornes inwiþ nesche ant softe swa schal ancre ute wiþ þolien heard on hire flesch ant prikiende pinen swa wisliche þah ha schal swenche þet flesch þet ha mahe seggen wiþ þe psalmwruhte þet is ich chulle wite mi strengþe laverd to þine bihove forþi beo flesches pine efter euchanes evene þet nest beo heard wiþuten ant softe ant swete þe heorte wiþinnen þeo þe beoþ of bitter oþer of heard heorte ant nesche to hare flesch ha makieþ frommard hare nest softe wiþuten ant þorni wiþinnen þis beoþ þe weamode ant te estfule ancres bittre wiþinnen as þet swete schulde beon ant estfule wiþuten as þet hearde schulde beon þeos i þulli nest mahen habben uvel rest hwen ha ham wel biþencheþ for leate ha schulen bringe forþ briddes of swuch nest þet beoþ gode werkes þe fleon toward heovene cleopeþ nest þe ancre hus ant seiþ as he were ancre þet is ich chulle deien i mi nest beon ase dead þe rin for þet is ancres rihte ant wunien aþet deaþ þe rin þet ich nulle neaver slakien hwil þe sawle is i þe buc to drehen heard wiþuten alswa as nest is ant softe beo wiþinnen of dumbe beastes leorne wisdom ant lare þe earn deþ in his nest a deorewurþe ȝimstan achate hatte for nan attri þing ne mei þe stan nahhin ne hwil he is i þe nest hearmin his briddes þis deorewurþe stan þet is ase stan treowe ant ful of alle mihtes over alle ȝimstanes he is þe achate þet atter of sunne ne nahhede neaver do him i þi nest þet is i þin heorte þench hwuch pine he þolede on his flesch wiþuten hu swote he wes iheortet hu softe wiþinnen ant swa þu schalt driven ut euch atter of þin heorte ant bitternesse of þi bodi for i þulli þoht ne beo hit neaver se bitter pine þet tu þolie for þe luve of him þe droh mare for þe schal þunche þe swote þes stan as ich seide afleieþ attrie þinges habbe þu þes stan inwiþ þi breoste þer godes nest is ne þearf þu noht dreden þe attri neddre of helle þine briddes þet beoþ þine gode werkes beoþ al sker of his atter hwase ne mei þes ȝimstan habben ne halden i þe nest of hire heorte lanhure i þe nest of hire ancrehus habbe his iliche þet is þe crucifix bihalde ofte þe ron ant cusse þe wundestuden i swote munegunge of þe soþe wunden þe he o þe soþe rode þuldeliche þolede se vorþ se ha mei beo þet is libben hearde beon cnawen ofte to godd his muchele toward hire ant hire fawtes toward him þet ha him ȝelt hit uvele crie him ȝeorne þe rof mearci ant are ant schrive hire ilome þenne is ha þe sloh for on ebreisch is schrift on englisch þet sleaþ gasteliche þen deovel of helle forþi seiþ ancre to euch preost on alre earst ant schriveþ hire ofte forte beo ant slean þet is þe deofles strengþe for ase muchel seiþ þis nome as stinkinde in helle on ebreische ledene is þe feond þe makeþ feble ant unstrong feat kealf ant to wilde þet is þet flesch þe awildgeþ sone se hit eaver featteþ þurh eise ant þurh este mi leof is ifeatted he seiþ ure laverd ant smit me wiþ his hele sone se flesch haveþ his wil hit regibeþ anan ase feat meare ant idel þis featte kealf haveþ þe feond strengþe to unstrengen ant buhen toward sunne for swa muche seiþ þis nome ah ancre schal beo þurh heard lif ant þurh soþ schrift ant slean as dude þes uvele temie ful wel hire flesch sone se ha ifeleþ þet hit awilgeþ to swiþe mid feasten mid wecchen wiþ here wiþ heard swinc wiþ hearde disceplines wisliche þah ant wearliche þet is in euch sacrefise he seiþ ure laverd offriþ me salt eaver veaste wecche ant oþre swucche as ich nempnede nu beoþ mi sacrefises salt bitacneþ wisdom for salt ȝeveþ mete smech ant wisdom ȝeveþ savur al þet we wel wurcheþ wiþute salt of wisdom þuncheþ godd smechles alle ure deden on oþer half wiþute salt flesch gedereþ wurmes stinkeþ swiþe fule ant forroteþ sone alswa wiþute wisdom flesch as wurm forfret hire ant wasteþ hireseolven forfeareþ as þing þe forroteþ ant sleaþ hire on ende ah þulli sacrefise stinkeþ ure laverd þah þe flesch beo ure hit is us ihaten þet we halden hit up wa we moten don hit as hit is wel ofte wurþe ah nawt fordon mid alle for hu wac se hit eaver beo þenne is hit swa icuplet ant se feste ifeiet to ure deorewurþe gast godes ahne furme þet we mahten sone slean þet an wiþ þet oþer ant tis is an of þe measte wundres on eorþe þet te heste þing under godd þet is monnes sawle as seint witneþ schal beo se feste ifeiet to flesch þet nis bute fen ant a ful eorþe ant þurh þet ilke limunge luvien hit se swiþe þet ha for te cwemen hit in his fule cunde geaþ ut of hire hehe heovenliche cunde ant forte paien hire wreaþeþ hire schuppere þe scheop hire efter himseolf þet is king ant keiser of eorþe ant of heovene wunder over wunder ant hokerlich wunder þet se unimete lah þing for neh nawt seiþ seint schal drahen into sunne se unimete heh þing ase sawle is þet seint awstin cleopeþ þet is for neh hest þing wiþute godd ah godd nalde nawt þet ha lupe i prude ne wilnede to climben ant feolle as dude for he wes bute charge ant teide forþi a clot of hevi eorþe to hire as me deþ þe cubbel to þe ku oþer to þe oþer beast þet is to recchinde ant renginde abuten þis is þet seide laverd he seiþ þu havest imaket foþer to feþerin wiþ þe sawlen þet is þet hevie flesch þet draheþ hire duneward ah þurh þe hehschipe of hire hit schal wurþe ful liht lihtre þen þe wind is ant brihtre þen þe sunne ȝef hit folheþ hire her ne ne draheþ hire to swiþe into hire lahe cunde leove sustren for his luve þet ha is ilich to beoreþ hire menske ne leote ȝe nawt þe lahe flesch meistrin hire to swiþe ha is her in uncuþþe iput in a prisun bitund in a cwalmhus ne nis nawt edscene of hwuch dignete ha is hu heh is hire cunde ne hwuch ha schal þunche ȝet in hire ahne riche þet flesch is her ed hame as eorþe þe is in eorþe ant is forþi cointe ant cover as me seiþ þet curre is kene on his ahne mixne ha haveþ to much meistrie weilawei o monie ah ancre as ich habbe iseid ah to beon al gastelich ȝef ha wule wel fleon as brid þet haveþ lutel flesch ant feole fiþeren nawt ane ȝet tis ah teke þet ha temeþ wel hire fulitohe flesch ant strengeþ ant deþ menske þe wurþfule sawle teke þis ha mot ȝet þurh hire forbisne ant þurh hire hali beoden ȝeoven strengþe oþre ant uphalden ham þet ha ne fallen i þe dunge of sunne ant forþi daviþ anan efter þet he haveþ ievenet ancre to pellican he eveneþ hire to nihtfuhel þe is under evesunges þe nihtfuhel i þe evesunges bitacneþ recluses þe wunieþ forþi under chirche evesunges þet ha understonden þet ha ahen to beon of se hali lif þet al hali chirche þet is cristene folc leonie ant wreoþie upon ham ant heo halden hire up wiþ hare lif halinesse ant hare eadie bonen forþi is ancre ancre icleopet ant under chirche iancret as ancre under schipes bord forte halden þet schip þet uþen ant stormes hit ne overwarpen alswa al hali chirche þet is schip icleopet schal ancrin o þe ancre þet heo hit swa halde þet te deofles puffesþet beoþ temptatiuns ne hit overwarpen euch ancre haveþ þis o foreward ba þurh nome of ancre ant þurh þet ha wuneþ under þe chirche to understiprin hire ȝef ha walde fallen ȝef ha brekeþ foreward loki hwam ha lihe ant hu continuelement for ha ne stureþ neaver ancre wununge ant hire nome ȝeieþ eaver þis foreward ȝet hwen ha slepeþ on oþer half þe nihtfuhel fliþ bi niht ant biȝet i þeosternesse his fode alswa schal ancre fleon wiþ contemplatiun þet is wiþ heh þoht ant wiþ hali bonen bi niht toward heovene ant biȝeote bi niht hire sawle fode bi niht ah ancre to beon waker ant bisiliche abuten gastelich biȝete forþi kimeþ anan þe refter ich wes waker seiþ daviþ in ancre persone ant ilich spearewe under rof ane ich wes waker for þet is ancre rihte muchel forte wakien na þing ne awealdeþ wilde flesch ne ne makeþ hit tomre þen muche wecche wecche is in hali writ i feole studen ipreiset alswa as ȝe nulleþ nawt fallen into fondunge he seiþ ure laverd wakieþ ant ibiddeþ ow þet schal don ow stonden eft he seiþ eadi is þe ilke þet hwen ure laverd kimeþ ifint wakiende ant he himseolf sumchearre wakede i beoden al niht ant swa he tahte us wecche nawt ane wiþ his lare ah dude wiþ his dede eahte þinges nomeliche leaþieþ us to wakien eaver i sum god ant beo wurchinde þis scheorte lif þis stronge wei ure god þet is se þunne ure sunnen þe beoþ se monie deaþ þet we beoþ siker of ant unsiker hwenne þet sterke dom of domes dei ant se nearow mid alle þet euch idel word biþ þer ibroht forþ ant idele þohtes þe neren ear her ibette loke nu hwet beo of unwreaste willes ant sunfule werkes ȝet þe seoveþe þing þe munegeþ us to wakien þet is þe sorhe of helle þer bihald þreo þing þe untaleliche pinen þe echnesse of euchan þe unimete bitternesse þe eahtuþe þing hu muchel is þe mede i þe blisse of heovene world buten ende hwase wakeþ her wel ane hond hwile hwase haveþ þeos eahte þing ofte in hire heorte ha wule schaken of hire slep of uvel slawþe i þe stille niht hwen me ne siþ nawiht nowþer ne ne hereþ þet lette þe bone þe heorte is ofte se schir for na þing nis witnesse of þing þet me þenne deþ bute godes engel þe is i swuch time bisiliche abuten to eggin us to gode for þer nis nawt forloren as is bi dei ofte hercniþ nu leove sustren hu hit is uvel to uppin ant hu god þing hit is to heolen goddede ant fleo bi niht as nihtfuhel ant gederin bi þeostre þet is i privite ant dearnliche sawle fode þet is hesteres bone þe cwen wes þe king assuer licwurþe ant icweme hester on ebreisch þet is ihud on englisch ant is to understonden þet bone ant oþer goddede þet is idon on hudles is assuer i cweme þet is þe king of heovene for assuer on ebreisch is eadi on englisch þet is ure laverd þe is eadi over alle daviþ spekeþ to ancre þe wes iwunet in hudles wel forte wurchen ant seoþþen o sum wise uppeþ hit ant schaweþ þet is hwi drahest tu ut þin hond ant ȝet ti riht hond of midde þi bosum on ende riht hond is god werc bosum is privite ant is as þah he seide þe riht hond þet tu heolde ancre i þi bosum þet is þi gode werc þet tu hefdest idon privement as þing is dearne i bosum hwi drahest tu hit ut on ende þet is þet ti mede endi se sone þi mede þet were endeles ȝef þi goddede ihole were hwi openest tu hit ant nimest se scheort mede hure þet is agan in an hondhwile þu havest iuppet þi god he seiþ ure laverd witerliche þu havest undervo þi mede sein awundreþ him ant seiþ þet men beoþ wode þe trochiþ swa uvele muchel meadschipe hit is he seiþ don wel ant wilni word þe rof don hwerþurh he buþ þe kinedom of heovene ant sullen hit for a windes puf of wordes hereword of monnes herunge forþi mine leove sustren haldeþ ower riht hond in wiþ ower bosum leste mede endeles neome scheort ende we redeþ in hali writ þet hond godes prophete sone se he hefde idrahen hire ut of his bosum bisemde þe spiteluvel ant þuhte lepruse þurh hwet is bitacnet þet goddede idrahe forþ nis nawt ane forloren þurh þet uppinge ah þuncheþ ȝet eatelich bivore godes ehe as spiteluvel is eatelich bivore monnes sihþe lo a feorli god word þet te hali seiþ i mi bosum he seiþ is al min hope i halden as þah he seide hwet god se ich do were hit ut of bosum iuppet ant idrahe forþ al min hope were edslopen ah forþi þet ich hit heole ant hude as i bosum ich hopie to mede forþi ȝef ei deþ eani god ne drahe ha hit nawt utward ne ȝelpe na wiht þe rof for wiþ a lutel puf wiþ a wordes wind hit mei beon al toweavet ure laverd i meaneþ him swiþe of þeo þe forleoseþ ant spilleþ al hare god þurh wilnunge of hereword ant seiþ þeos wordes allas seiþ ure laverd þeos þe schaweþ hire god haveþ bipilet mi fier irend al þe rinde of despuilet hire steort naket ant iwarpen awei ant te grene bohes beoþ fordruhede ant forwurþen to drue hwite rondes þis word is dosc ah neomeþ nu ȝeme hu ich hit wulle brihtin fier is a cunnes treo þe bereþ swete frut þet me cleopeþ figes þenne is þe fier bipilet ant te rinde irend of hwen goddede is iuppet þenne is þe lif ut þenne adeadeþ þe treo hwen þe rinde is awei ne nowþer ne bereþ hit frut ne greneþ þe refter i lufsume leaves ah druhieþ þe bohes ant wurþeþ hwite rondes to na þing betere þen to fures fode þe boh hwen hit adeadeþ hit hwiteþ utewiþ ant adruheþ inwiþ ant warpeþ his rinde alswa goddede þe wule adeadin forwarpeþ his rinde þet is unhuleþ him þe rinde þe wriþ hit is þe treoes warde ant wit hit i strengþe ant i cwicnesse alswa þe hulunge is þe goddedes lif ant halt hit i strengþe ah hwen þe rinde is offe þenne as þe boh deþ hwiteþ hit utewiþ þurh worltlich hereword ant adruheþ inwiþ ant leoseþ þe swetnesse of godes grace þe makede hit grene ant lic wurþe godd to bihalden for grene over alle heowes frovreþ meast ehnen hwen hit is swa adruhet þenne nis hit to nawt se god as to þe fur of helle for þe earste bipilunge hwerof al þis uvel is nis bute of prude ant nis þis muche reowþe þet te fier þe schulde wiþ hire swete frut þet is goddede fede godd gasteliche þe laverd of heovene schal adruhien rindeles þurh þet hit is unhulet ant wurþen buten ende helle fures fode ant nis ha to unseli þe wiþ þe wurþ of heovene buþ hire helle ure laverd i þe godspel seolf eveneþ heoveriche to goldhord þe hwase hit fint as he seiþ hudeþ hit golþord is goddede þe is to heovene ievenet for me hit buþ þerwiþ ant þis golþord bute hit beo þe betere ihud ant iholen hit is forlore sone for as sein seiþ þe bereþ tresor openliche i wei þet is al ful of reaveres ant of þeoves him luste leosen hit ant beon irobbet þis world nis bute a wei to heovene oþer to helle ant is al biset of hellene mucheres þe robbiþ alle þe golþordes þet ha mahen underȝeoten þet mon oþer wummon i þis wei openeþ for ase muchel wurþ is as hwase seide ant ȝeide as he eode ich beore golþord ich beore golþord lowr hit her read gold hwit seolver inoh ant deore wurþe stanes a sapere þe ne bereþ bute sape ant nelden ȝeiȝeþ hehe þet he bereþ a riche mercer geaþ forþ al stille freiniþ hwet itidde of þe gode king for þi þet he schawde þe celles of his aromaz his muchele þinges his deorewurþe tresor nis hit nawt for nawt iwriten i þe hali godspel of þe þreo kinges þe comen to offrin þe deore þreo lakes þet tet ha walden offrin him ha heolden eaver ihud aþet ha comen bivoren him þa earst ha unduden þe presenz þet ha beren for þi mine leove sustren bi niht as þe nihtfuhel þet ancre is to ievenet beoþ ȝeorne sturiende niht ich cleopie privite þis niht ȝe mahen habben euch time of þe dei þet al þe god þet ȝe eaver doþ beo idon as bi niht ant bi þeosternesse ut of monnes ehe ut of monnes eare þus i niht beoþ fleonninde ant sechinde ower sawle heovenliche fode þenne ne beo ȝe nawt ane ah beoþ ec ȝet is ancre ievenet her to spearewe þet is ane under rof as ancre spearewe is a chiterinde brid chitereþ aa ant chirmeþ ah forþi þet moni ancre haveþ þet ilke unþeaw daviþ ne eveneþ hire nawt to spearewe þe haveþ fere ah deþ to spearewe ane ich am he seiþ bi ancre as spearewe þet is ane for swa ah ancre hire ane in anlich stude as ha is chirmin ant chiterin eaver hire bonen ant understondeþ leofliche mine leove sustren þet ich write of anlich lif forte frovrin ancren ant ow over alle hu god is to beon ane is ba i þe alde lahe ant i þe neowe isutelet for i baþe me i fint þet godd his dearne runes ant heovenliche privitez schawde his leoveste freond nawt i monne floc ah dude þer ha weren ane bi hamseolven ant heo hamseolf alswa as ofte as ha walden þenchen schirliche of godd ant makien cleane bonen ant beon in heorte gasteliche ihehet toward heovene aa me ifint þet ha fluhen monne sturbunge ant wenden bi ham ane ant þer godd edeawde ham ant schawde himseolf to ham ant ȝef ham hare bonen forþi þet ich seide þet me ifint tis ba i þe alde testament ant ec i þe neowe ich chulle of ba twa schawin forbisne þe patriarche forte þenche deopliche sohte anlich stude ant wende bi him ane as teleþ ant swa he imette wiþ þe eadi þet is wiþ godes grace alswa þe eadi þa ure laverd schawde him his deorewurþe nebscheft ant ȝef him his blesceunge ant wende his nome betere he wes iflohe men ant wes him al ane neaver ȝete i monne floc ne cahte he swuch biȝete bi ant bi helye godes deorewurþe freond is sutel ant edscene hwuch baret ant hu dredful lif is eaver imong þrung ant hu godd his privitez schaweþ to þeo þe beoþ privement ham ane me schal leove sustren þeose estoires tellen ow for ha weren to longe to writen ham here ant þenne schule ȝe al þis brihte understonden þe eadi seiþ he sit ane ant seiþ þe reisun for hwi ure laverd hefde ifullet him of his þreatunge godes þreatunge is wontreaþe ant weane i licome ant i sawle worlt buten ende þe were of þis þreatunge as he wes wel ifullet nere þer nan empti stude i þe heorte to underfon fleschliche lahtren forþi he bed wealle of teares þet ha ne adruhede neaver na mare þen wealle forte biwepe slei folc þet is meast al þe world þet is gasteliche islein mid deadliche sunnen ant to þis wop lokiþ nu he bit anlich stude þe hali prophete forte schawi witerliche þet hwase wule biwepen hire ahne ant oþres sunnen as ancre ah to donne ant hwase wule ifinden ed te nearewe domesmon mearci ant are a þing þet let him meast is beowiste þet is wununge bimong men ant þet swiþest furþreþ hit þet is anlich stude mon oþer wummon eiþer to beon ane ȝet spekeþ of anlich stude mare me schal sitten he seiþ him ane ant beo stille of þis stilnesse he spekeþ þerbivoren lutel god hit is i silence ikepen godes grace ant þet me beore godes ȝeoc anan from his ȝuheþe ant þenne kimeþ þe refter hwase swa wule don ha schal sitten ane ant halden hire stille ant swa heoven hireseolf buven hireseolven þet is wiþ heh lif hehi toward heovene over hire cunde teke þis hwet oþer god cume of þis anlich sittunge þet spekeþ of ant of þis seli stilþe kimeþ anan efter ha wule he seiþ þe swa liveþ aȝeines þe smitere beode forþ þe cheke ant beo þurhfullet wiþ schentfule wordes her beoþ i þeos word twa eadi þeawes to noti swiþe ȝeorne þe limpeþ ariht to ancre þolemodnesse i þe earre half i þe leatere eadmodnesse of milde ant meoke heorte for þolemod is þe þuldeliche abereþ woh þet me him deþ eadmod is þe þolie mei þet me him missegge þeos þe ich habbe inempnet her weren of þe alde testament cume we nu to þe neowe sein baptiste bi hwam ure laverd seide þet bimong wives sunen ne aras neaver herre he kenneþ us openliche bi his ahne dede þet anlich stude is baþe siker ant biheve for þah þe engel hefde his burde ibocket al were he ifullet of þe hali gast anan inwiþ his moder wombe al were he þurh miracle of baraigne iboren ant in his i nobr borenesse unspende his feader tunge into prophecie for al þis ne durste he ȝet wunie bimong men se dredful lif he seh þe rin þah hit nere of nawt elles bute of speche ane ant forþi hwet dude he ȝung of ȝeres fleh awei into wildernesse leste he wiþ speche sulde his cleane lif for swa is in his ymne he hefde as hit þuncheþ iherd þe meande him ant seide wumme wa is me he seiþ þe hali prophete for ich am a mon of sulede lippen ant seiþ þe acheisun hwervore ant þet is forþi he seiþ þet ich wunie bimong men þe suleþ hare lippen mid misliche spechen lo hu godes prophete seiþ he wes isulet þurh beowiste bimong monne swa hit is sikerliche beo neaver se briht or metal gold seolver irn stel þet hit ne schal drahe rust of anoþer þet is i rustet forhwon þet ha longe liggen togedere forþi fleh sein þe feolahschipe of fule men leste he were ifulet ah ȝet forte schawin us þet me ne mei þe uvele fleon bute me fleo þe gode he fleh his hali cun icoren of ure laverd ant wende into anli stude ant wunede i þe wildernesse ant hwet biȝet he þer he biȝet þet he wes godes baptiste o þe muchele hehnesse þet he heold i fulluht under hise honden þe laverd of heovene þe halt up al þe world wiþ his anes mihte þer þe hali trinite þrumnesse on englisch schawde hire al to him þe feader in his stevene þe hali gast i culvre heow þe sune in his honden in anlich lif he biȝet þreo preminences privilegie of preachur merite of martirdom meidenes mede þeos þreo manere men habbeþ in heovene wiþ overfullet mede crune upo crune ant te eadi in anlich stude as he wes alle þeose þreo estaz ofearnede him ane ure leove leafdi ne leadde ha anlich lif ne fond te engel hire in anli stude al ane nes ha nowher ute ah wes biloken feste for swa we ifindeþ þet is þe engel wende into hire þenne wes heo inne in anli stude hire ane engel to mon i þrung ne edeawede neaver ofte on oþer half þurh þet nowher in hali writ nis iwriten of hire speche bute fowr siþen as is iseid þe ruppe sutel prufunge hit is þet ha wes muchel ane þe heold swa silence hwet seche ich oþer of godd ane were inoh forbisne to alle þe wende himseolf into anli stude ant feaste þeras he wes ane i wildernesse forte schawin þerbi þet bimong monne þrung ne mei nan makien riht penitence þer in anli stude him hungrede hit seiþ ancre to frovre þet is meoseise þer he þolede þet te feond fondede him feoleweis ah he overcom him alswa forte schawin þet te feond fondeþ muchel þeo þe leadeþ anlich lif for onde þet he haveþ to ham ah he is þer overcumen for ure laverd seolf þer stont bi ham i fehte ant bealdeþ ham hu ha schulen stonden strongliche aȝein ant ȝeveþ ham of his strengþe he as hali writ seiþ þet na nurþ ne þrung of folc ne mahte letten him of his beoden ne desturbin his god he þah no þeleatere hwen he walde beon i beoden he fleh nawt ane oþre men ah dude ȝet his halie deorewurþe apostles ant wende ane upon hulles us to forbisne þet we schule turne bi usseolf ant climben wiþ him on hulles þet is þenchen hehe ant leaven lahe under us alle eorþliche þohtes hwiles we beoþ i bonen ant ant sincletice ant sare ant oþre swucche monie men ant wummen baþe fondeden witerliche ant underȝeten soþliche þe biȝete of anlich lif as þeo þe duden wiþ godd al þet ha walden sein nu leate seiþ bi himseolven as ofte as ich eaver wes he seiþ bimong men ich wende from ham leasse mon þen ich ear wes forþi seiþ þe wise þet is ne þunche þe neaver god imong monne floc for þer is eaver sunne ne seide þe stevene to arsenie of heovene arseni flih men ant tu schalt beon iborhen ant eft hit com ant seide þet is arseni flih beo stille ant wune studevestliche i sum stude ut of monne nu ȝe habbeþ iherd mine leove sustren forbisne of þe alde lahe ant ek of þe neowe hwi ȝe ahen anlich lif swiþe to luvien efter þe forbisnes hereþ nu reisuns hwi me ah to fleo þe world eahte ed te leaste ich ham segge scheortliche neomeþ þe betere ȝeme þe forme is sikernesse ȝef a wod liun urne ȝont te strete nalde þe wise bitunen hire sone ant seinte seiþ þet helle liun rengeþ ant reccheþ eaver abuten forte sechen inȝong sawle to forswolhen ant bid us beo wakere ant bisie in hali beoden leste he us lecche þis is seinte word þet ich ear seide forþi beoþ ancren wise þe habbeþ wel bitund ham aȝein helle liun for te beo þe sikerure þe oþer reisun is þe bere a deore licur a deorewurþe wet as basme is in a feble vetles healewi i bruchel gles nalde ha gan ut of þrung bute ha fol were þis bruchele vetles þet is wummone flesch þah noþeleatere þe basme þe healewi is meidenhad þet is þe rin oþer efter meiþlure chaste cleannesse þis bruchele vetles is bruchel as is eani gles for beo hit eanes tobroken ibet ne biþ hit neaver ibet ne hal as hit wes ear na mare þene gles ah ȝet hit brekeþ mid leasse þen bruchel gles do for gles ne tobrekeþ nawt bute sum þing hit rine ant hit onont meiþlure mei leosen his halnesse wiþ a stinkinde wil swa vorþ hit mei gan ant leaste se longe ah þis manere bruche mei beon ibet eft ase hal allunge as hit wes eaver halest þurh medecine of schrift ant bireowsunge nu þe preove herof sein ewangeliste nefde he brud ibroht ham nefde he iþoht þa ȝef godd nefde ilet him meiþhad to forleosen seoþþen þah nes he meiden neaver þe unhalre ah wes meiden bitaht meiden to witene nu as ich segge þis deorewurþe healewi i bruchel vetles is meiþhad ant cleannesse in ower bruchele flesch bruchelure þen eani gles þet ȝef ȝe weren i worldes þrung wiþ a lutel hurlunge ȝe mahten al leosen as þe wrecches i þe world þe hurliþ togederes ant breokeþ hare vetles ant cleannesse schedeþ forþi ure laverd cleopeþ þus leaveþ þe world ant cumeþ to me for þer ȝe schulen beon i þrung ah reste ant peis is in me þe þridde reisun of þe worldes fluht is þe biȝete of heovene þe heovene is swiþe heh hwase wule biȝeoten hit ant areachen þerto hire is lutel inoh forte warpen al þe world under hire fotes forþi alle þe halhen makeden of al þe world as a scheomel to hare vet to areache þe heovene þis is sein word ewangeliste i þe apocalipse ich iseh a wummon ischrud mid te sunne ant under hire vet þe mone þe mone woneþ ant waxeþ ne nis neaver studevest ant bitacneþ forþi worltliche þinges þe beoþ as þe mone eaver i change þes mone mot te wummon halden under hire vet þet is worldliche þinges totreoden ant forhohien þe wule heovene areachen ant beo þer ischrud mid te soþe sunne þe feorþe reisun is preove of noblesce ant of largesce noble men ant gentile ne beoreþ nane packes ne ne feareþ itrusset wiþ trussews ne wiþ purses hit is beggilde riht to beore bagge on bac burgeise to beore purse nawt godes spuse þe is leafdi of heovene trussen ant purses baggen ant packes beoþ worltliche þinges alle eorþliche weolen ant worltliche rentes þe fifte resiun is noble men ant wummen makieþ large relef ah hwa mei makie largere þen þe oþer þeo þe seiþ wiþ seinte laverd forte folhi þe we habbeþ al forleavet nis þis large relef nis þis muche lave mine leove sustren kinges ant keisers habbeþ hare liveneþ of ower large relef þet ȝe ileavet habbeþ laverd forte folhi þe seiþ seinte we habbeþ al forleavet as þah he seide we wulleþ folhi þe i þe muchele genterise of þi largesce þu leafdest to oþre men alle richesces ant makedest of al relef ant lave se large we wulleþ folhi þe we wulleþ don alswa leaven al as þu dudest folhi þe on eorþe i þet ant in oþerhwet forte folhi þe ec into þe blisse of heovene ant ȝet tear over al folhi þe hwiderward se þu eaver wendest as nane ne mahen bute ane meidnes þe seste reisun is hwi ȝe habbeþ þe world iflohen familiarite muche cun redden forte beo prive wiþ ure laverd for þus he seiþ bi osee ich chulle leade þe he seiþ to his leofmon into anli stude ant ter ich chulle luveliche speoke to þin heorte for me is laþ preasse þe seoveþe reisun is forte beo þe brihtre ant brihtluker seon in heovene godes brihte nebscheft for ȝe beoþ iflohe þe world ant hudeþ ow for hire her ȝet terteken þet ȝe beon swifte as þe sunne gleam for ȝe beoþ wiþ bitund as i sepulcre bibarret as he wes o þe deore rode as is iseid þe ruppe þe eahtuþe reisun is to habben cwic bone ant lokiþ ȝeorne hwervore þe eadmode cwen hester bitacneþ ancre for hire nome seiþ ihud on englische ledene as me ret in hire boc ha wes þe king assuer over al icweme ant þurh hire bone arudde of deaþ al hire folc þe wes to deaþ idemet þis nome assuer is ispealet eadi as is ear iseid ant bitacneþ godd eadi over alle he ȝetteþ hester þe cwen þet is þe treowe ancre þet is riht hester þet is riht ihud he hereþ ant ȝetteþ hire alle hire benen ant sawveþ þurh ham muche folc monie schulde beo forloren þe beoþ þurh þe ancre benen iborhen as weren þurh hesteres forhwon þet ha beo hester ant halde hire as heo dude mardochees dohter mardoche is ispealet þet is bitterliche totreodinde þene scheomelese scheomeles is þe mon þe seiþ eani untu oþer deþ bivoren ancre ȝef eani þah swa do ant heo breoke bitterliche his untohe word oþer his fol dede totreode ham ananriht wiþ unwurþ tellunge þenne is ha hester mardochees dohter bitterliche breokinde þene scheomelese bitterluker ne betere ne mei ha him neaver breoken þen is itaht þeruppe wiþ oþer mid tis vers ant wende inward anan toward hire weovede ant halde hire ed hame as hester þe ihudde semei i hefde deaþ ofservet ah he criede mearci ant forȝef hit him þah þurh swuch a foreward þet he ed hame heolde him i as he wunede ant hudde him in his huse ȝef he ohwider wende ut swuch wes þe foreward þet he were eft al ful ant to deaþ idemet he þah brec foreward þurh his unselhþe his þrealles edfluhen him ant edbreken him ut ant he folhede ham ant wende ut efter ham hwet wult tu mare wes sone forwreiet to þe king ant for þe foreward tobroken wes fordemet to deaþe understondeþ ȝeorne þis mine leove sustren semeȝ bitacneþ þe utwarde ancre nawt hester þe ihudde for semeȝ seiþ þet is herinde on ure ledene þet is þe recluse þe haveþ asse earen longe to here feor þet is hercninde efter ut runes semeis stude wes þet he schulde in huden him ȝef he walde libben þis word spealeþ sihþe of peis ant bitacneþ ancrehus for þe rinne ne þearf ha seon bute peis ane ne beo neaver semei þet is þe recluse swa swiþe forgult toward te soþe þet is ure laverd halde hire ed hame i þet ha nawiht nute of þe worldes baret ȝetteþ hire bliþeliche his are ah ȝef ha entremeateþ hire of þinges wiþuten mare þen ha þurfte ant hire heorte beo ute wiþ þah a clot of eorþe þet is hire licome beo inwiþ þe fowr wahes ha is iwend wiþ semei ut of alswa as he dude efter his þrealles þeos þrealles beoþ þe eþele fif wittes þe schulden beon et hame ant servin hare leafdi þenne ha serviþ wel þe ancre hare leafdi hwen ha notieþ ham wel in hare sawle neode hwen þe ehe is o þe boc oþer o sum oþer god þe eare to godes word þe muþ in hali bonen ȝef ha wit ham uvele ant let ham þurh ȝemeles etfleon hire servise ant folhi ham utwart wiþ hire heorte as hit bitimeþ eaver meast þet gan þe wittes ut þe heorte geaþ ut efter ha brekeþ foreward wiþ þe unseli semeȝ ant is to deaþ idemet forþi mine leove sustren ne beo ȝe nawt semeȝ ah beoþ hester þe ihudde ant ȝe schule beon ihehet i þe blisse of heovene for þe nome of hester ne seiþ nawt ane þet is nawt ane ihud ah deþ þerteken þet is i folc ihehet ant swa wes hester as hire nome cwiddeþ ihehet to cwen of a povre meiden i þis word hester beoþ hudunge ant hehnesse ifeiet togederes ant nawt ane hehnesse ah hehnesse over folc forte schawin witerliche þet teo þe hudeþ ham ariht in hare ancrehus ha schulen beon in heovene over oþres cunnes folc wurþliche ihehet ba hesteres nome ant hire hehunge pruvieþ þet ich segge on oþer half understondeþ ȝe beoþ i ȝe beoþ iflohe to chirche griþ for nis ower nan þet nere sumchearre godes þeof me weiteþ ow þet wite ȝe ful ȝeorne wiþuten as me deþ þeoves þe beoþ ibroke to chirche haldeþ ow feaste inne nawt te bodi ane for þet is þe unwurþest ah ower fif wittes ant te heorte over al ant al þer þe sawle lif is for beo ha bitrept utewiþ nis þer bute leade forþ toward te gealforke þet is þe wearitreo of helle beoþ ofdred of euch mon alswa as þe þeof is leste he drahe ow utwart þet is biswike wiþ sunne ant weiti forte warpen upon ow his cleches bisecheþ ȝeornliche godd as þeof ibroke to chirche þet he wite ant wardi ow wiþ alle þe ow weitiþ chiteriþ ower beoden aa as spearewe deþ þet is ane for þis an word is iseid of anlich lif of anlich stude þer me mei beon hester ihud ut of þe world ant do betere þen i þrung euch gastelich biȝete forþi eveneþ daviþ ancre to pellican þet leat anlich lif ant to spearewe ane spearewe haveþ ȝet a cunde þet is biheve ancre þah me hit heatie þet is þe fallinde uvel for muche neod is þet ancre of hali lif ant of heh habbe fallinde uvel þet uvel ne segge ich nawt þet me swa nempneþ ah fallinde uvel ich cleopie licomes secnesse oþer temptatiuns of flesches fondunges hwerþurh hire þunche þet ha falle duneward of hali hehnesse ha walde awilgin elles oþer to wel leoten of hireseolven ant swa to noht iwurþen þe flesch walde awilgin ant bicumen to fulitohen toward hire leafdi ȝef hit nere ibeaten ant makie sec þe sawle ȝef secnesse hit ne temede wiþ uvel oþer wiþ sunne þe licome ne þe gast ȝef hare nowþer nere sec as hit timeþ seldene orhel walde awakenin þet is þe measte dredfule secnesse of alle ȝef godd fondeþ ancre wiþ ei uvel utewiþ oþer þe feonde inwiþ wiþ gasteliche unþeawes ase prude wreaþþe onde oþer wiþ flesches lustes ha haveþ þet fallinde uvel þet me seiþ is spearewe uvel godd hit wule forþi þet ha beo eaver eadmod ant wiþ lah haldunge of hireseolven falle to þer eorþe leste ha falle i prude nu we hurteþ leove sustren to þe feorþe dale þet ich seide schulde beon of feole fondunges for þer beoþ uttre ant inre ant eiþer monivalde salve ich bihet to teachen toȝeines ham ant bote ant hu hwase haveþ ham mei gederin of þis dale cunfort ant frovre toȝeines ham alle þet ich þurh þe lare of þe hali gast mote halden foreward he hit ȝetti me þurh ower bonen ne wene nan of heh lif þet ha ne beo itemptet mare beoþ þe gode þe beoþ iclumben hehe itemptet þen þe wake ant þet is reisun for se þe hul is herre se þe wind is mare þe ron se þe hul is herre of hali lif ant of heh se þe feondes puffes þe windes of fondunges beoþ strengre þeron ant mare ȝef ei ancre is þe ne veleþ nane fondunges swiþe drede i þet puint þet ha beo overmuchel ant overswiþe ifondet for swa sein seiþ sec mon haveþ twa estaz swiþe dredfule þet an is hwen he ne feleþ nawt his ahne secnesse ant forþi ne secheþ nawt leche ne lechecreft ne easkeþ namon read ant asteorveþ ferliche ear me least wene þis is þe ancre þe nat nawt hwet is fondunge to þeos spekeþ þe engel i þe apocalipse þu seist þe nis neod na medecine ah þu art blind iheortet ne ne sist nawt hu þu art povre ant naket of halinesse ant gastelich wrecche þet oþer dredfule estat þet te seke haveþ is al frommard þis þet is hwen he feleþ se muchel angoise þet he ne mei þolien þet me hondli his sar ne þet me him heale þis is sum ancre þe feleþ se swiþe hire fondunges ant is se sare ofdred þet na gastelich cunfort ne mei hire gleadien ne makien to understonden þet ha mahe ant schule þurh ham þe betere beon i borhen ne teleþ hit i þe godspel þet te hali gast leadde ure laverd seolf into anlich stude to leaden anlich lif forte beon itemptet of þe unwine of helle ah his temptatiun þe ne mahte sunegin wes ane wiþuten understondeþ þenne on alre earst leove sustren þet twa cunne temptatiuns twa cunne fondunges beoþ uttre ant inre ant ba beoþ feolevalde uttre fondunge is hwerof kimeþ licunge oþer mislicunge wiþuten oþer wiþinnen mislicunge wiþuten ase secnesse meoseise scheome unhap ant euch licomlich derf þet te flesch eileþ wiþinnen heorte sar grome ant wreaþþe alswa onont þet ha is pine licunge wiþuten licomes heale mete drunch claþ inoh ant euch flesches eise onont swucche þinges licunge wiþinnen as sum fals gleadschipe oþer of monne hereword oþer ȝef me is iluvet mare þen anoþer mare iolhnet mare idon god oþer menske þis dale of þis temptatiun þet is uttre icleopet is swikelure þen þe oþer half ba beoþ a temptatiun ant eiþer wiþinnen ant wiþuten baþe of hire twa dalen ah ha is uttre icleopet for ha is eaver oþer i þing wiþuten oþer of þing wiþuten ant te uttre þing is þe fondunge þeos fondunge kimeþ oþerhwile of godd of mon oþerhwiles of godd as of freondes deaþ secnesse oþer on ham oþer o þeseolven poverte mishapnunge ant oþre swucche heale alswa ant eise of mon as mislich woh oþer of word oþer of werc o þe oþer o þine alswa hereword oþer goddede þeos cumeþ alswa of godd ah nawt as doþ þe oþre wiþuten euch middel ah wiþ alle he fondeþ mon hu he him drede ant luvie inre fondunges beoþ misliche unþeawes oþer lust towart ham oþer þohtes swikele þe þuncheþ þah gode þeos inre fondunge kimeþ of þe feond of þe world of ure flesch oþerhwile to þe uttre temptatiun is neod patience þet is þolemodnesse to þe inre is neod wisdom ant gastelich strengþe we schulen nu speoken of þe uttre ant teachen þeo þe habbeþ hire hu ha mahen wiþ godes grace ifinde remedie þet is elne aȝeines hire to frovrin hamseolven eadi is ant seli þe haveþ i temptatiun þolemodnesse for hwen ha is ipruvet hit seiþ ha schal beon i crunet mid te crune of lif þe godd haveþ bihaten his leove icorene hwen ha is ipruvet hit seiþ wel is hit iseid for alswa pruveþ godd his leove i corene as þe goltsmiþ fondeþ þet gold i þe fure þet false gold forwurþeþ þerin þet gode kimeþ ut brihtre secnesse is a brune hat forte þolien ah na þing ne clenseþ gold as hit deþ þe sawle secnesse þet godd send nawt þet sum lecheþ þurh hire ahne dusischipe deþ þeose six þinges i wescheþ þe sunnen þe beoþ ear iwrahte wardeþ toȝein þeo þe weren towardes pruveþ pacience halt in eadmodnesse muchleþ þe mede eveneþ to martir þene þolemode þus is secnesse sawlene heale salve of hire wunden scheld þet ha ne kecche ma as godd siþ þet ha schulde ȝef secnesse hit ne lette secnesse makeþ mon to understonden hwet he is to cnawen himseolven ant as god meister beat forte leorni wel hu mihti is godd hu frakel is þe worldes blisse secnesse is þi goldsmiþ þe i þe blisse of heovene overguldeþ þi crune se þe secnesse is mare se þe goltsmiþ is bisgre ant se hit lengre least se he brihteþ hire swiþere to beo martirs evening þurh a hwilinde wa hwet is mare grace to þeo þe hefde ofearnet þe pinen of helle world abuten ende nalde me tellen him alre monne dusegest þe forseke a buffet for a speres wunde a nelde pricchunge for an bihefdunge a beatunge for an hongunge on helle wearitreo aa on ecnesse godd hit wat leove sustren al þe wa of þis world is ievenet to helle alre leaste pine al nis bute balplohe al nis nawt swa muchel as is a lutel deawes drope toȝeines þe brade sea ant alle worldes weattres þe mei þenne edstearten þet ilke grisliche wa þe eateliche pinen þurh secnesse þet ageaþ þurh ei uvel þet her is seliliche mei ha seggen on oþer half leorniþ monivalde frovren aȝein þe uttre fondunge þe kimeþ of monnes uvel for þeos þe ich habbe iseid of is of godes sonde hwase eaver misseiþ þe oþer misdeþ þe nim ȝeme ant understond þet he is þi vile þe lorimers habbeþ ant fileþ al þi rust awei ant ti ruhe of sunne for he fret himseolven weilawei as þe file deþ ah he makeþ smeþe ant brihteþ þi sawle on oþer wise þench hwaseeaver hearmeþ þe oþer eni wa deþ þe scheome grome teone he is godes ȝerde for swa he seiþ þurh sein muþ i þe apocalipse ne beat he nan bute hwamse he luveþ ant halt for his dohter namare þen þu waldest beaten a fremede child þah hit al gulte ah nawt ne leote he wel of þet is godes ȝerde for as þe feader hwen he haveþ inoh ibeaten his child ant haveþ hit ituht wel warpeþ þe ȝerde i þe fur for ha nis noht namare alswa þe feder of heovene hwen he haveþ ibeaten wiþ an unwreast mon oþer an unwrest wummon his leove child for his god he warpeþ þe ȝerde þet is þe unwreste into þe fur of helle forþi he seiþ elleshwer þet is min is þe wrake ich chulle ȝelden as þah he seide ne wreoke ȝe nawt owseolven ne grucchi ȝe ne wearien hwen me gulteþ wiþ ow ah þencheþ anan þet he is ower feadres ȝerde ant þet he wule ȝelden him ȝerde servise ant nis þet child fulitohen þet scratleþ aȝein ant bit upo þe ȝerde þet deboneire child hwen hit is ibeaten ȝef þe feader hat hit hit cusseþ þe ȝerde ant ȝe don alswa mine leove sustren for swa hat ower feader þet ȝe cussen nawt wiþ muþ ah wiþ luve of heorte þeo þe he ow wiþ beateþ þis is godes heste þet him is muchel leovre þen þet tu eote gruttene bred oþer weredest hearde here luvieþ ower vamen he seiþ ant doþ god ȝef ȝe mahen to þeo þet ow weorriþ ȝef ȝe elles ne mahen biddeþ ȝeorne for þeo þet ow eni eil doþ oþer misseggeþ ant te apostle leareþ ne ȝelde ȝe neaver uvel for uvel ah doþ god eaver aȝein uvel as dude ure laverd seolf ant alle his hali halhen ȝef ȝe þus haldeþ godes heaste þenne beo ȝe his hende child ant cusseþ þe ȝerde þe he haveþ ow wiþ iþorschen nu seiþ oþerhwile sum his sawle oþer hiren ich chulle wel luvien his bodi o nane wise ah þet nis nawt to seggen þe sawle ant te licome nis bute a mon ant ba ham tit a dom wult tu dealen o twa þe godd haveþ to an isompnet he forbeot hit ant seiþ ne wurþe nan se wod þet he todeale þe þing þe godd haveþ iveiet þencheþ ȝet þisses weis þet child ȝef hit spurneþ o sum þing oþer hurteþ me beat þet hit hurte on ant þet child is wel ipaiet forȝeteþ al his hurt ant stilleþ hise teares forþi frovriþ owseolven godd schal o domesdei don as þah he seide dohter hurte þes þe dude he þe spurnen i wreaþþe oþer in heorte sar i scheome oþer in eani teone loke dohter loke he seiþ hu he hit schal abuggen ant þer ȝe schule seon bunkin him wiþ þes deofles betles þet wa biþ him þes lives ȝe schulen beo wel ipaiet þe rof for ower wil ant godes wil schal swa beon iveiet þet ȝe schulen wullen al þet he eaver wule ant he al þet ȝe wulleþ over alle oþre þohtes in alle ower passiuns þencheþ eaver inwardliche up godes pinen þet te worldes wealdent walde for his þrealles þolien swucche schendlakes hokeres buffez spatlunge blindfeallunge þornene crununge þet set him i þe heaved swa þet te blodi strundes striken adun ant leaveden dun to þer eorþe his swete bodi ibunden naket to þe hearde piler ant ibeate swa þet tet deorewurþe blod ron on euche halve þet attri drunch þet me him ȝef þa him þurste o rode hare heafde sturunge upon him þa heo on hokerunge gredden se lude lo her þe healde oþre lo hu he healeþ nu ant helpeþ himseolven turneþ þe ruppe þer ich spec hu he wes ipinet in alle his fif wittes ant eveneþ al ower wa secnesse ant oþerhwet woh of word oþer of werc ant al þet mon mei þolien to þet tet he þolede ant ȝe schulen lihtliche iseon hu lutel hit reacheþ nomeliche ȝef ȝe þencheþ þet he wes al ladles ant þet he droh al þis nawt for himseolven for he ne agulte neaver ȝef ȝe þolieþ wa ȝe habbeþ wurse ofservet ant al þet ȝe þolieþ al is for owseolven gaþ nu þenne gleadluker bi strong wei ant bi swincful toward te muchele feaste of heovene þeras ower gleade freond ower cume ikepeþ þenne dusie worldes men gaþ bi grene wei toward te wearitreo ant te deaþ of helle betere is ga sec to heovene þen hal to helle to murhþe wiþ meoseise þen to wa wiþ eise nawt forþi witerliche wrecche worltliche men buggeþ deorre helle þen ȝe doþ þe heovene a þing to soþe wite ȝe a misword þet ȝe þolieþ a deies longunge a secnesse of a stunde ȝef me chapede ed ow an of þeos o domesdei þet is þe mede þe ariseþ þe rof ȝe hit nalden sullen for al þe world of golde for þet schal beon ower song bivoren ure laverd þet is wel is us for þe dahes þet tu lahedest us wiþ oþer monne wohes ant wel is us nu laverd for þe ilke ȝeres þet we weren seke in ant sehen sar ant sorhe euch worltlich wa hit is godes sonde heh monnes messager me schal hehliche undervon ant makien him glead chere nomeliche ȝef he is prive wiþ his laverd ant hwa wes mare prive wiþ þe king of heovene hwil he her wunede þen wes þes sondesmon þet is worldes weane þe ne com neaver from him aþet his lives ende þes messager hwet teleþ he ow he frovreþ ow o þis wise godd as he luvede me he send me to his leove freond mi cume ant mi wununge þah hit þunche attri hit is halwende nere þet þing grislich hwas schadewe ȝe ne mahte nawt wiþuten hurt felen hwet walde ȝe seggen bi þet eisfule wiht þet hit of come wite ȝe to soþe þet al þe wa of þis world nis bute schadewe of þe wa of helle ich am þe schadewe seiþ þes messager þet is worldes weane nedlunge ȝe moten oþer undervo me oþer þet grisliche wa þet ich am of schadewe hwase underveþ me gleadliche ant makeþ me feier chere mi laverd send hire word þet ha is cwite of þet þing þet ich am of schadewe þus spekeþ godes messager forþi seiþ sein alle blisse haldeþ hit to fallen i misliche of þeose fondunges þe uttre beoþ ihaten ant seint alle þe ilke fondunges þe we beoþ nu i beaten wiþ þuncheþ wop nawt wunne ah ha wendeþ efterward to weole ant to eche blisse þe inre fondunge is twavalt alswa as is þe uttre for þe uttre is adversite ant prosperte ant þeos cundleþ þe inre mislicunge in adversite ant i prosperite licunge þe limpeþ to sunne þis ich segge forþi þet sum licunge is ant sum mislicunge þe ofearneþ muche mede as licunge i godes luve ant mislicunge for sunne nu as ich segge þe inre fondunge is twavald fleschlich ant gastelich fleschlich as of leccherie of glutunie of slawþe gastelich as of prude of onde ant of wreaþþe alswa of ȝiscunge þus beoþ þe inre fondunges þe seoven heaved sunnen ant hare fule cundles flesches fondunge mei beon ievenet to fotwunde gastelich fondunge þet is mare dred of mei beon for þe peril i cleopet breostwunde ah us þuncheþ greattre flesliche temptatiuns forþi þet heo beoþ eþfele þe oþre þah we habben ham ofte nute we hit nawt ant beoþ þah greate ant grisliche i godes ehe ant beoþ muchel forþi to drede þe mare for þe oþre þe me feleþ wel secheþ leche ant salve þe gasteliche hurtes ne þuncheþ nawt sare ne ne salviþ ham wiþ schrift ne wiþ penitence ant draheþ to eche deaþ ear me least wene hali men ant wummen beoþ of alle fondunges swiþest ofte itemptet ant ham to goder heale for þurh þe feht toȝeines ham ha biȝeoteþ þe blisfule kempene crune lo þah hu ha meaneþ ham i þet is ure wiþeriwines swiftre þen earnes upo þe hulles ha clumben efter us ant þer fuhten wiþ us ant ȝet i þe wildernesse ha spieden us to sleanne ure wiþeriwines beoþ þreo þe feond þe worlt ure ahne flesch as ich ear seide lihtliche ne mei me nawt oþerhwile icnawen hwuch of þeos þreo him weorreþ for euch helpeþ oþer þah þe feond proprement eggeþ to atternesse as to prude to overhohe to onde ant to wreaþþe ant to hare attri cundles þe herefter beoþ inempnet þe flesch sput proprement toward swetnesse eise ant softnesse þe world bit mon ȝiscin worldes weole ant wurþschipe ant oþre swucche give gaven þe bidweolieþ cang men to luvien a schadewe þeos wiþeriwines hit seiþ folhiþ us on hulles ant weitiþ i wildernesse hu ha us mahen hearmin hul þet is heh lif þer þe deofles asawz ofte beoþ strengest wildernesse is anlich lif of ancre wununge for alswa as i wildernes beoþ alle wilde beastes ant nulleþ nawt þolien monne nahunge ah fleoþ hwen ha heom ihereþ alswa schulen ancres over alle oþre wummen beo wilde o þisse wise ant þenne beoþ ha over oþre leove to ure laverd ant swetest him þuncheþ ham for of all flesches is wilde deores flesch leovest ant swetest bi þis wildernesse wende ure laverdes folc as exode teleþ toward te eadi lond of þet he ham hefde bihaten ant ȝe mine leove sustren wendeþ bi þe ilke wei toward te hehe þe kinedom þet he haveþ bihaten his i corene gaþ þah ful warliche for i þis wildernesse beoþ uvele beastes monie liun of prude neddre of attri onde unicorne of wreaþþe beore of dead slawþe vox of ȝisceunge suhe of ȝivernesse scorpiun wiþ þe teil of stinginde leccherie þet is galnesse her beoþ nu o rawe itald þe seoven heaved sunnen þe liun of prude haveþ swiþe monie hwelpes ant ich chulle nempni summe þet is hwase let wel of ei þing þet ha deþ oþer seiþ oþer haveþ wlite oþer wit god acointance oþer word mare þen anoþer cun oþer meistrie ant hire wil forþre ant hwet is wlite wurþ her gold ring i suhe nease acointance i religiun wa deþ hit ofte al is þe let eawiht wel of ant walde habben word þe rof ant is wel ipaiet ȝef ha is ipreiset mispaiet ȝef ha nis itald swuch as ha walde anoþer is þet is þe þuncheþ hokerlich of ei þing þet ha siþ bi oþer oþer hereþ ant forhoheþ chastiement oþer ei lahres lare þe þridde hwelp is þe makeþ hire betere þen ha is þe feorþe is þe nimeþ mare on hond þen ha mei overcumen oþer entremeteþ hire of þing þet to hire ne falleþ oþer is to overtrusti upo godes grace oþer on hireseolven to bald upon ei mon þet is fleschlich as heo is ant mei beon itemptet þe fifte hwelp hatte inobedience nawt ane þe ne buheþ ah þe oþer grucchinde deþ oþer targeþ to longe þet child þe ne buheþ ealdren underling his prelat paroschien his preost meiden hire dame euch lahre his herre þe seste is þe fedeþ þis hwelp þe is of muche speche ȝelpeþ demeþ oþre liheþ oþerhwile gabbeþ upbreideþ chideþ fikeleþ stureþ lahtre þe seoveþe is blasphemie þis hwelpes nurrice is þe swereþ greate aþes oþer bitterliche curseþ oþer misseiþ bi godd oþer bi his halhen for ei þing þet he þoleþ siþ oþer hereþ þe eahtuþe is inpatience þis hwelp fet þe nis þolemod aȝein alle wohes ant in alle uveles þe niheþe is contumace ant þis fet hwase is anewil i þing þet ha haveþ undernume to donne beo hit god beo hit uvel þet na wisure read ne mei bringen hire ut of hire riote þe teoheþe is þet is strif to overcumen þet te oþer þunche underneoþen awarpen ant cravant ant heo meistre of þe mot ant crenge ase champiun þe haveþ biȝete þe place i þis unþeaw is upbrud ant edwitunge of al þet uvel þet ha mei bi þe oþer ofþenchen ant eaver se hit biteþ bittrure se hire likeþ betere þah hit were of þing þe wes bivore ȝare amendet her imong beoþ oþerhwiles nawt ane bittre wordes ah beoþ fule stinkinde scheomelese ant schentfule sumchearre mid great sware monie ant prude wordes wiþ warinesses ant bileasunges herto falleþ evenunge of hamseolf of hare cun of sahe oþer of dede þis is among nunnen ant gaþ wiþ swuch muþ seoþþen ear schrift ham habbe iweschen to herie godd wiþ loftsong oþer biddeþ him privee bonen me þinges amansede nuten ha þet hare song ant hare bonen to godd stinkeþ fulre to him ant to alle his halhen þen ei rotet dogge þe ealleofte hwelp is ifed wiþ supersticiuns wiþ semblanz ant wiþ sines as beoren on heh þet heaved crenge wiþ swire lokin o siden bihalden on hokere winche mid ehe binde seode mid te muþ wiþ hond oþer wiþ heaved makie scuter signe warpe schonke over schench sitten oþer gan stif as ha istaket were luve lokin o mon speoken as an innocent ant wlispin for þen anes herto falleþ of veil of heaved claþ of euch oþer claþ to overgart acemunge oþer in heowunge oþer i pinchunge gurdles ant gurdunge o dameiseles wise scleaterunge mid smirles fule fluþrunges heowin her litien leor pinchen bruhen oþer bencin ham uppart wiþ wete fingres monie oþre þer beoþ þe cumeþ of weole of wunne of heh cun of feier claþ of wit of wlite of strengþe of heh lif waxeþ prude ant of hali þeawes monie ma hwelpes þen ich habbe inempnet haveþ þe liun of prude ah abute þeose studieþ wel swiþe for ich ga lihtliche over ne do bute nempni ham ah ȝe eaver ihwer se ich ga swiþere vorþ leaveþ þer lengest for þer ich feþeri on a word tene oþer tweolve hwaseeaver haveþ eani unþeaw of þeo þe ich her nempnede oþer ham iliche ha haveþ prude sikerliche huseeaver hire curtel beo ischapet oþer iheowet heo is þe liunes make þet ich habbe ispeken of ant fet hire wode hwelpes inwiþ hire breoste þe neddre of attri onde haveþ seove hwelpes þis cundel bret hwase nis icnawen goddede ah teleþ lutel þe rof oþer forȝet mid alle goddede ich segge nawt ane þet mon deþ him ah þet godd deþ him oþer haveþ idon him oþer him oþer hire mare þen ha understont ȝef ha hire wel biþohte of þis unþeaw me nimeþ to lutel ȝeme ant is þah of alle an laþest godd ant meast aȝein his grace þe oþer cundel is þet is heatunge oþer great heorte þe bret hit i breoste al is attri to godd þet he eaver wurcheþ þe þridde cundel is ofþunchunge of oþres god þe feorþe gleadschipe of his uvel þe fifte wreiunge þe seste bacbitunge þe seoveþe upbrud oþer scarnunge þe eahtuþe is þet is misortrowunge bi mon oþer bi wummon wiþuten witer tacne þenchen þis semblant ha makeþ þis ha seiþ oþer deþ me forte gremien hokerin oþer hearmin ant þet hwen þe oþer neaver þiderward ne þencheþ herto falleþ falsdom þet godd forbeot swiþe as þenchen oþer seggen ȝe ne luveþ ha me nawt herof ha wreide me lo nu ha speokeþ of me þe twa þe þreo oþer þe ma þe sitteþ togederes swuch ha is ant swuch ant for uvel ha hit dude i þulli þoht we beoþ ofte bichearret for ofte is god þet þuncheþ uvel ant forþi beoþ al dei monnes domes false herto limpeþ alswa luþere neowe fundles ant leasunges ladliche þurh niþ ant þurh onde þe niheþe cundel is sawunge of unsibsumnesse of wreaþþe ant of descorde þeo þe saweþ þis deofles sed ha is of godd amanset þe teoheþe is luþer stilþe þe deofles silence þet te an nule for onde speoken o þe oþer ant þis spece is alswa cundel of wreaþþe for hare teames beoþ imengt ofte togederes hwer as ei of þeos wes þer wes þe cundel oþer þe alde moder of þe attri neddre of onde þe unicorne of wreaþþe þe bereþ on his nease þe þorn þet he asneaseþ wiþ al þet he areacheþ haveþ six hwelpes þe earste is chast oþer strif þe oþer is wodschipe bihald te ehnen ant te neb hwen wod wreaþþe is imunt bihald hire contenemenz loke on hire lates hercne hu þe muþ geaþ ant tu maht demen hire wel ut of hire witte þe þridde is schentful upbrud þe feorþe is wariunge þe fifte is dunt þe seste is wil þet him uvel tidde oþer on him seolf oþer on his freond oþer on his ahte þe seoveþe hwelp is don for wreaþþe mis oþer leaven wel to don forgan mete oþer drunch wreoken hire wiþ teares ȝef ha elles ne mei ant wiþ weariunges hire heaved spillen o grome oþer on oþer wise hearmin hire i sawle ant i bodi baþe þeos is homicide ant morþre of hireseolven þe beore of hevi slawþe haveþ þeose hwelpes is þe forme þet is wlech heorte unlust to eni þing þe schulde leitin al o lei i luve of ure laverd þe oþer is þet is to povre heorte ant to earh mid alle ei heh þing to underneomen in hope of godes help ant i trust on his grace nawt of hire strengþe þe þridde is þis haveþ hwase wurcheþ god ant deþ hit tah mid a dead ant mid an hevi heorte þe feorþe is ydelnesse hwase stut mid alle þe fifte is heorte grucchunge þe seste is a dead sorhe for lure of ei worltlich þing oþer for eni unþonc bute for sunne ane þe seoveþe is ȝemelesschipe oþer to seggen oþer to don oþer to biseon bivoren oþer to þenchen efter oþer to miswiten eni þing þet ha haveþ to ȝemen þe eahtuþe is unhope þis leaste beore hwelp is grimmest of alle for hit tocheoweþ ant tofret godes milde milce ant his muchele mearci ant his unimete grace þe vox of ȝisceunge haveþ þeose hwelpes triccherie ant gile þeofþe reaflac wite ant herrure strengþe false witnesse oþer aþ dearne symonie gavel oker festschipe prinschipe of ȝeove oþer of lane þis is icluht heorte unþeaw gode laþest þe ȝef us al himseolven monslaht oþerhwile þis unþeaw is to vox for moni reisun ievenet twa ich chulle seggen muche gile is i vox ant swa is i ȝisceunge of worltlich biȝete anoþer þe vox awurieþ al a floc þah he ne mahe buten an frechliche swolhen alswa ȝisceþ a ȝiscere þet tet moni þusent mahten bi flutten ah þah his heorte berste ne mei he bruken on himseolf bute a monnes dale al þet mon wilneþ mare oþer wummon þen ha mei rihtliche leade þet lif bi euch efter þet ha is al is ȝisceunge ant rote of deadlich sunne þet is riht religiun þet euch efter his stat borhi ed tis frakele world se lutel se ha least mei of mete of claþ of ahte of alle hire þinges notiþ þet ich segge euch efter his stat for þet word is ifeþeret ȝe mote makien þet wite ȝe i moni word muche strengþe þenchen longe þerabuten ant bi þet ilke an word understonden monie þe limpeþ þerto for ȝef ich schulde writen al hwenne come ich to ende þe suhe of ȝivernesse haveþ gris þus inempnet to earliche hatte þet an þet oþer to esteliche þet þridde to frechliche þet feorþe hatte to muche þet fifte to ofte i drunch mare þen i mete beoþ þeos gris iferhet ich speoke scheortliche of ham for nam ich nawt ofdred mine leove sustren leste ȝe ham feden þe scorpiun of leccherie þet is of galnesse haveþ swucche cundles þet in a wel itohe muþ hare summes nome ne sit nawt forte nempnin for þe nome ane mahte hurten alle wel itohene earen ant sulen cleane heorten þeo þah me mei nempnin wel hwas nomen me icnaweþ wel ant beoþ mare hearm is to monie al to cuþe horedom eawbruche meiþlure ant incest þet is bituhe sibbe fleschliche oþer gasteliche þet is o feole idealet ful wil to þet fulþe wiþ skiles ȝettunge helpen oþre þiderward beo weote ant witnesse þerof hunti þe refter wiþ wohunge wiþ toggunge oþer wiþ eni tollunge wiþ gigge lahtre hore ehe eanie lihte lates wiþ ȝeove wiþ tollinde word oþer wiþ luvespeche cos unhende grapunge þet mei beon heaved sunne luvie tide oþer stude forte cumen i swuch keast ant oþre foreridles þe me mot nede forbuhen þe i þe muchele fulþe nule fenniliche fallen as seint seiþ þet is hwase wule hire inwit witen hal ant fere ha mot fleon þe foreridles þe weren iwunet ofte to openin þe inȝong ant leoten in sunne ich ne dear nempnin þe uncundeliche cundles of þis deofles scorpiun attri iteilet ah sari mei ha beon þe bute fere oþer wiþ haveþ swa ifed cundel of hire galnesse þet ich ne mei speoken of for scheome ne ne dear for drede leste sum leorni mare uvel þen ha con ant beo þe rof itemptet ah þenche on hire ahne aweariede fundles in hire galnesse for hu se hit eaver is icwenct wakinde ant willes wiþ flesches licunge bute ane i wedlac hit geaþ to deadlich sunne i ȝuheþe me deþ wundres culche hit i schrift ut utterliche as ha hit dude þe feleþ hire schuldi oþer ha is idemet þurh þet fule brune cwench to þet eche brune of helle þe scorpiunes cundel þe ha bret in hire bosum schake hit ut wiþ schrift ant slea wiþ deadbote ȝe þe of swucches nute nawt ne þurve ȝe nawt wundrin ow ne þenchen hwet ich meane ah ȝeldeþ graces godd þet ȝe swuch uncleannesse nabbeþ ifondet ant habbeþ reowþe of ham þe i swuch beoþ ifallen inoh is etscene hwi ich habbe ievenet prude to liun onde to neddre ant of þeo alle þe oþre wiþute þis leaste þet is hwi galnesse beo to scorpiun ievenet ah lo her þe skile þe rof sutel ant etscene scorpiun is a cunnes wurm þe haveþ neb as me seiþ sumdeal ilich wummon ant neddre is bihinden makeþ feier semblant ant fikeþ mid te heaved ant stingeþ mid te teile þis is leccherie þis is þe deofles beast þet he leat to chepinge ant to euch gederunge ant chepeþ forte sullen ant biswikeþ monie þurh þet ha ne bihaldeþ nawt bute þe feire neb oþer þet feire heaved þet heaved is þe biginnunge of galnesse sunne ant te licunge hwil hit least þe þuncheþ swiþe swote þe teil þet is þe ende þerof is sar ofþunchunge ant stingeþ her wiþ atter of bitter bireowsunge ant of deadbote ant seliliche mahen ha seggen þe þe teil swuch ifindeþ for þet atter ageaþ ah ȝef hit ne suheþ her þe teil ant te attri ende is þe eche pine of helle ant nis he fol chapmon þe hwen he wule buggen hors oþer oxe ȝef he nule bihalden bute þet heaved ane forþi hwen þe deovel beodeþ forþ þis beast beot hit to sullen ant bit ti sawle þervore he hut eaver þe teil ant schaweþ forþ þe heaved ah þu ga al abuten ant schaw þe ende forþ mid al hu þe teil stingeþ ant swiþe flih þerfrommard ear þu beo iattret þus mine leove sustren i þe wildernesse þer ȝe gaþ in wiþ godes folc toward lond þet is þe riche of heovene beoþ þulliche beastes þulliche wurmes ne nat ich na sunne þet ne mei beon ilead oþer to an of ham seovene oþer to hare streones unsteaþelvest bileave aȝein godes lare nis hit te spece of prude inobedience herto falleþ sygaldren false teolunges lefunge swefne o nore ant on alle wicchecreftes neomunge of husel in eani heaved sunne oþer ei oþer sacrement nis hit te spece of prude þet ich cleopede ȝef me wat hwuch sunne hit is ȝef me hit nat nawt þenne is hit ȝemeles under þet ich slawþe cleopede þe ne warneþ oþer of his uvel oþer of his biȝete nis hit slaw ȝemeles oþer attri onde teoheþi mis edhalden cwide fundles oþer lane oþer þerwiþ misfearen nis hit spece of ȝisceunge ant anes cunnes þeofþe edhalden oþres hure over his rihte terme nis hit strong reaflac hwase ȝelden hit mei þe is under ȝisceunge ȝef me ȝemeþ wurse ei þing ileanet oþer bitaht to witene þen he wene þe ah hit nis hit oþer triccherie oþer ȝemeles of slawþe alswa is dusi heast oþer folliche ipliht trowþe longe beon unbischpet falsliche gan to schrift oþer to longe abiden ne teache godchild ne þeos ant alle þulliche beoþ ilead to slawþe þet is þe feorþe moder of þe seove sunnen þe dronc drunch oþer ei þing dude hwerþurh na child ne schulde beon on hire i streonet oþer þet istreonede schulde forwurþen nis þis strong monslaht of galnesse awakenet alle sunnen sunderliche bi hare nomeliche nomen ne mahte namon rikenin ah i þeo þe ich habbe iseid alle oþre beoþ bilokene ant nis ich wene namon þe ne mei understonden him of his sunne nomeliche under sum of þe ilke imeane þe beoþ her iwritene of þeose seove beastes ant of hare streones i wildernesse of anlich lif is iseid herto þe alle þe forþfearinde fondiþ to fordonne þe liun of prude sleaþ alle þe prude alle þe beoþ hehe ant overhohe iheortet þe attri neddre þe ontfule ant te luþere iþonket wreaþfule þe unicorne alswa of þe oþre o rawe to godd ha beoþ isleine ah ha libbeþ to þe feond ant beoþ alle in his hond ant serviþ him in his curt euch of þe meoster þe him to falleþ þe prude beoþ his bemeres draheþ wind inward wiþ worltlich hereword ant eft wiþ idel ȝelp puffeþ hit utward as þe bemeres doþ makieþ noise ant lud dream to schawin hare orhel ah ȝef ha wel þohten of godes bemeres of þe englene bemen þe schulen o fowr half þe world bivore þe grurefule dom grisliche blawen ariseþ deade ariseþ cumeþ to drihtines dom forte beon idemet þear na prud bemere ne schal beon iborhen ȝef ha þohten þis wel ha walden inohreaþe i þe deofles servise dimluker bemin of þeose bemeres seiþ of þe wind drahinde in for luve of hereword seiþ as ich seide summe juglurs beoþ þe ne cunnen servin of nan oþer gleo bute makien cheres wrenche þe muþ mis schulen wiþ ehnen of þis meoster serviþ þe unseli ontfule i þe deofles curt to bringen o lahtre hare ondfule laverd ȝef ei seiþ wel oþer deþ wel ne mahen ha nanes weis lokin þider wiþ riht ehe of god heorte ah winkiþ o þet half ant bihaldeþ o luft ȝef þer is eawt to edwiten oþer ladliche þiderward schuleþ mid eiþer hwen ha ihereþ þet god skleatteþ þe earen adun ah þe lust aȝein þet uvel is eaver wid open þenne he wrencheþ þe muþ hwen he turneþ god to uvel ant ȝef hit is sumdel uvel þurh mare lastunge wrencheþ hit to wurse þeos beoþ forecwidderes hare ahne prophetes þeos bodieþ bivoren hu þe eateliche deoflen schulen ȝet ageasten ham wiþ hare grennunge ant hu ha schulen hamseolf grennin ant nivelin ant makien sur semblant for þe muchele angoise i þe pine of helle ah forþi ha beoþ þe leasse to meanen þet ha bivorenhond leorniþ hare meoster to makien grim chere þe wreaþfule bivore þe feond skirmeþ mid cnives ant is his cnif warpere ant pleieþ mid sweordes bereþ ham bi þe scharp ord upon his tunge sweord ant cnif eiþer beoþ scharpe ant keorvinde word þet he warpeþ from him ant skirmeþ toward oþre ant he bodeþ hu þe deoflen schulen pleien wiþ him mid hare scharpe eawles skirmi wiþ him abuten ant dusten ase pilcheclut euch to ward oþer ant wiþ helle sweordes asneasen him þurhut þet beoþ kene ant eateliche ant keorvinde pinen þe slawe liþ ant slepeþ o þe deofles bearm as his deore deorling ant te deovel leiþ his tutel dun to his eare ant tuteleþ him al þet he wule for swa hit is sikerliche to hwamse is idel of god meaþeleþ þe feond ȝeorne ant te idele underveþ luveliche his lare idel ant ȝemeles is þes deofles bearnes slep ah he schal o domesdei grimliche abreiden wiþ þe dredfule dream of þe englene bemen ant in helle wontreaþe echeliche wakien þe ȝiscere is his eskibah feareþ abuten esken ant bisiliche stureþ him to rukelin togederes muchele ant monie ruken blaweþ þe rin ant blent himseolf peaþereþ ant makeþ þe rin figures of augrim as þes rikeneres doþ þe habbeþ muche to rikenin þis is al þe canges blisse ant te feond bihalt tis gomen ant laheþ þet he bersteþ wel understont euch wis mon þet gold ba ant seolver ant euch eorþlich ahte nis bute eorþe ant esken þe ablendeþ euch mon þe ham in blaweþ þet is þe bolheþ him þurh ham in heorte prude ant al þet he rukeleþ ant gedereþ togederes ant eþalt of ei þing þet nis bute esken mare þen hit neodeþ schal in helle wurþen him tadden ant neddren ant ba as seiþ schulen beon of wurmes his cuvertur ant his hwitel þe nalde þer wiþ neodfule feden ne schruden þe ȝivere glutun is þe feondes manciple ah he stikeþ eaver i celer oþer i cuchene his heorte is i þe dissches his þoht al i þe neppes his lif i þe tunne his sawle i þe crohhe kimeþ bivoren his laverd bismuddet ant bismulret a disch in his an hond a scale in his oþer meaþeleþ mis wordes wigleþ as fordrunke mon þe haveþ imunt to fallen bihalt his greate wombe ant te deovel lahheþ þeose þreatiþ þus godd þurh mine men schulen eoten ant ow schal eaver hungrin ant ȝe schule beon feondes fode world buten ende ȝef þe kealchecuppe wallinde bres to drinken ȝeot in his wide þrote þet he swelte inwiþ aȝein an ȝef him twa þullich is godes dom aȝein ȝivere ant druncwile i þe apocalipse þe lecchurs i þe deofles curt habbeþ riht hare ahne nome for i þes muchele curz þeo me cleopeþ lecchurs þe habbeþ swa forlore scheome þet heom nis nawiht of scheome ah secheþ hu ha mahen meast vilainie wurchen þe lecchur i þe deofles curt bifuleþ himseolven fulliche ant his feolahes alle stinkeþ of þet fulþe ant paieþ wel his laverd wiþ þet stinkinde breaþ betere þen he schulde wiþ eani swote rechles hu he stinke to godd i þe engel hit schawde þe heold his nease þa þer com þe prude lecchur ridinde ant nawt for þet rotede lich þet he healp þe hali earmite to biburien of alle oþre þenne habbeþ þeos þe fuleste meoster i þe feondes curt þe swa bidoþ hamseolven ant he schal bidon ham pinin ham wiþ eche stench i þe put of helle nu ȝe habbeþ ane dale iherd mine leove sustren of þeo þe me cleopeþ þe seove modersunnen ant of hare teames ant of hwucche meosters þes ilke men serviþ i þe feondes curt þe habbeþ iwivet o þeose seoven haggen ant hwi ha beoþ swiþe to heatien ant to schunien ȝe beoþ ful feor from ham ure laverd beo iþoncket ah þet fule breaþ of þis leaste unþeaw þet is of leccherie stinkeþ se swiþe feor for þe feond hit saweþ ant toblaweþ over al þet ich am sumdel ofdred leste hit leape sumchearre into ower heortes nease stench stiheþ uppart ant ȝe beoþ hehe iclumben þer þe wind is muchel of stronge temptatiuns ure laverd ȝeove ow strengþe wel to wiþstonden sum weneþ þet ha schule stronglukest beon ifondet i þe forme tweofmoneþ þet ha bigon ancre lif ant i þe oþer þe refter ant hwen ha efter feole ȝer feleþ ham stronge wundreþ hire swiþe ant is ofdred leste godd habbe hire al forwarpen nai nawt nis hit swa i þe forme ȝeres nis bute balplohe to monie men of ordre ah neomeþ ȝeme hu hit feareþ bi a forbisne hwen a wis mon neowliche haveþ wif ilead ham he nimeþ ȝeme al softeliche of hire maneres þah he seo bi hire þet him mispaieþ he let ȝet iwurþen makeþ hire feire chere ant is umben euches weis þet ha him luvie inwardliche in hire heorte hwen he understont wel þet hire luve is treoweliche toward him ifestnet þenne mei he sikerliche chastien hire openliche of hire unþeawes þet he ear forber as he ham nawt nuste makeþ him swiþe sturne ant went te grimme toþ to forte fondin ȝetten ȝef he mahte hire luve toward him unfestnin alest hwen he understont þet ha is al wel ituht ne for þing þet he deþ hire ne luveþ him þe leasse ah mare ant mare ȝef ha mei from deie to deie þenne schaweþ he hire þet he hire luveþ sweteliche ant deþ al þet ha wule as þeo þet he wel i cnaweþ þenne is al þet wa iwurþe to wunne ȝef ower spus deþ alswa bi ow mine leove sustren ne þunche ow neaver wunder i þe frumþe nis þer buten olhnunge forte drahen in luve ah sone se he eaver understont þet he beo wel acointet he wule forbeoren ow leasse efter þe spreove on ende þenne is þe muchele joie al o þis ilke wise þa he walde his folc leaden ut of þeowdom ut of pharaones hond ut of egypte he dude for ham al þet ha walden miracles feole ant feire druhede þe reade sea ant makede ham freo wei þurh hire ant þer ha eoden drufot adrencte pharaon ant hare fan alle i þe desert forþre þa he hefde ilead ham feor i þe wildernesse he lette ham þolien wa inoh hunger þurst ant muche swinc ant weorren muchele ant monie on ende he ȝef ham reste ant alle weole ant wunne al hare heorte wil ant flesches eise ant este þus ure laverd speareþ on earst þe ȝunge ant te feble ant draheþ ham ut of þis world swoteliche ant wiþ liste sone se he siþ ham heardin he let weorre awakenin ant teacheþ ham to fehten ant weane to þolien on ende efter long swinc he ȝeveþ ham swote reste her ich segge i þis world ear ha cumen to heovene ant þuncheþ þenne swa god þe reste efter þe swinc þe muchele eise efter þe muchele meoseise þuncheþ se swote nu beoþ i þe sawter under þe twa temptatiuns þet ich ear seide þet beoþ þe uttre ant te inre þe temeþ alle þe oþre fowr dalen todealet þus fondunge liht ant dearne fondunge liht ant openlich fondunge strong ant dearne fondunge strong ant openlich as is þer understonden of fondunge liht ant dearne seiþ þeose wordes lutle dropen þurliþ þe flint þe ofte falleþ þe ron ant lihte dearne fondunges þe me nis war of falsiþ a treowe heorte of þe lihte openliche bi hwam he seiþ alswa nis nawt se muche dute of strong temptatiun þet is þah dearne is ec þet meaneþ þet is mine fan weitiþ me wiþ triccherie ant wiþ treisun ant ha strengden upo me ant nes hwa me hulpe wa schal cumen on þe ant tu ne schalt witen hweonne of þe feorþe fondunge þet is strong ant openlich he makeþ his man of his fan þe hali ant seiþ þet is ha þreasten in upo me as þah þe wal were tobroken ant te ȝeten opene þe forme ant te þridde fondunge of þeose fowre beoþ al meast under þe inre þe oþer ant te feorþe falleþ under þe uttre ant beoþ al meast fleschliche ant eþ forþi to felen þe oþre twa beoþ gasteliche of gasteliche unþeawes ant beoþ ihud ofte ant dearne hwen ha derveþ meast ant beoþ muche forþi þe mare to dreden moni þet ne weneþ nawt bret in hire breoste sum liunes hwelp sum neddre cundel þe forfret þe sawle of hwucche osee seiþ þet is unholde forfreten þe strengþe of his sawle ant he hit nawt nuste ȝet is meast dred of hwen þe sweoke of helle eggeþ to a þing þet þuncheþ swiþe god mid alle ant is þah sawle bone ant wei to deadlich sunne swa he deþ as ofte as he ne mei wiþ open uvel cuþen his strengþe na he seiþ ne mei ich nawt makien þeos to sungin þurh ȝivernesse ant ich chulle as þe wreastleare wrenchen hire þiderward as ha meast dreaieþ ant warpen hire o þet half ant breiden ferliche adun ear ha least wene ant eggeþ hire toward se muchel abstinence þet ha is þe unstrengre i godes servise ant to leaden se heard lif ant pinin swa þet licome þet te sawle asteorve he bihalt anoþer þet he ne mei nanesweis makien luþere iþoncket se luveful ant se reowþful is hire heorte ich chulle makien hire he seiþ to reowþful mid alle ich schal don hire se muchel þet ha schal luvien ahte þenchen leasse of godd ant leosen hire fame ant put þenne a þulli þonc in hire softe heorte seinte naveþ þe mon oþer þe wummon meoseise ant na mon nule don ham nawt me walde me ȝef ich bede ant swa ich mahte helpen ham ant don on ham ealmesse bringeþ hire on to gederin ant ȝeoven al earst to povre forþre to oþer freond aleast makien feaste ant wurþen al worldlich forschuppet of ancre to husewif of halle godd wat swuch feaste makeþ sum hore weneþ þet ha wel do as dusie ant adotede doþ hire to understonden flatriþ hire of freolec herieþ ant heoveþ up þe ealmesse þet ha deþ hu wide ha is icnawen ant heo let wel of ant leapeþ in orhel sum seiþ inohreaþe þet ha gedereþ hord swa þet hire hus mei ant heo ba beon irobbet reowþe over reowþe þus þe traitre of helle makeþ him treowe readesmon ne leve ȝe him neaver daviþ cleopeþ him briht schininde deovel ant seinte þet is engel of liht for swuch ofte he makeþ him ant schaweþ him to monie na sihþe þet ȝe seoþ ne i swefne ne waken ne telle ȝe bute dweole for nis hit bute his gile he haveþ wise men of hali ant of heh lif ofte swa bichearret as þe þet he com to i wummone liche i þe wildernesse seide ha wes igan o dweole ant weop as meoseise þing efter herbearhe ant te oþer hali mon þet he makede ileven þet he wes engel bi his feader þet he wes þe deovel ant makede him to slean his feader swa ofte þerbivoren he heafde iseid him eaver soþ forte biswiken him sariliche on ende alswa of þe hali mon þet he makede cumen ham forte dealen his feader feh to neodfule ant to povre se longe þet he deadliche sunegede o wummon ant swa feol into unhope ant deide in heaved sunne of mon þe spekeþ wiþ ow þulliche talen hereþ hu ȝe schulen witen ow wiþ þes deofles wiltes þet he ow ne bichearre sum of ow sumchearre he makede to leven þet hit were fikelunge ȝef ha speke feire ant ȝef ha eadmodliche meande hire neode ȝef ha þonckede mon of his goddede ant wes mare overhohe forte acwenchen chearite þen rihtwisnesse sum he is umben to makien se swiþe fleon monne frovre þet ha falleþ i deadlich sar þet is oþer into deop þoht swa þet ha dotie sum heateþ swa sunne þet ha haveþ overhohe of oþre þe falleþ þe schulde wepen for hire ant sare dreden for a swuch onont hireseolven ant seggen as þe hali mon þe seac ant weop ant seide þa me him talde þe fal of an of his breþren weilawei strongliche wes he itemptet ear he swa feolle as he feol todei ich mei quoþ he alswa fallen tomarhen nu mine leove sustren monie temptatiuns ich habbe ow inempnet under þe seove sunnen nawt þah þe þusentfald þet me is wiþ itemptet ne mahte ich wene ham namon nomeliche nempnin ah i þeo þe beoþ iseid alle beoþ bilokene lut beoþ i þis world oþer nan mid alle þet ne beo wiþ hare sum oþerhwile itemptet he haveþ se monie buistes ful of his letuaires þe luþere leche of helle þe forsakeþ an he beot anoþer forþ ananriht þe þridde þe feorþe ant swa eaver forþ aþet he cume o swuch þet me on ende undervo ant he þenne wiþ þet birleþ him ilome þencheþ her of þe tale of his ampoiles hereþ nu as ich bihet aȝein alle fondunges moni cunne frovre ant wiþ godes grace þe refter þe salve
