siker beo of fondunge hwase eaver stont in heh lif ant þis is þe earste frovre for eaver se herre tur se haveþ mare windes ȝe beoþ tur owseolven mine leove sustren ah ne drede ȝe nawt hwil ȝe beoþ se treoweliche ant se feste ilimet wiþ lim of anred luve euch of ow to oþer for na deofles puf ne þurve ȝe dreden bute þet lim falsi þet is to seggen bute luve bitweonen ow þurh þe feond wursi sone se ei unlimeþ hire ha biþ sone iswipt forþ bute ȝef þe oþre halden hire ha biþ sone ikeast adun as þe lowse stan is from þe tures cop into þe deope dich of sum suti sunne nu anoþer elne muchel ah to frovrin ow hwen ȝe beoþ itemptet þe tur nis nawt asailit ne castel ne cite hwen ha beoþ iwunnen alswa þe helle weorrur ne asaileþ nan wiþ fondunge þe he haveþ in his hond ah deþ þeo þe he naveþ nawt forþi leove sustren hwase nis nawt asailet ha mei sare beon ofdred leste ha beo biwunnen þe þridde cunfort is þet ure laverd seolf i þe teacheþ us to bidden þet is laverd feader ne suffre þu nawt þe feond þet he leade us allunge into fondunge lo neomeþ ȝeme he nule nawt þet we bidden þet we ne beon nawt ifondet for þet is ure purgatoire ure cleansing fur ah þet we ne beon nawt allunge ibroht þe rin wiþ consens of heorte wiþ skiles ȝettunge þe feorþe frovre is sikernesse of godes help i þe fehtunge aȝein as seinte witneþ godd he seiþ is treowe nule he neaver suffrin þet te deovel tempti us over þet he siþ wel þet we mahen þolien ah i þe temptatiun he haveþ iset to þe feond a mearke as þah he seide tempte hire swa feor ah ne schalt tu gan na forþre ant swa feor he ȝeveþ hire strengþe to wiþstonden þe feond ne mei nawt forþre gan a pricke ant þis is þe fifte frovre þet he ne mei na þing don us bute bi godes leave þet wes wel ischawet as þe godspel teleþ þa þe deoflen þet ure laverd weorp ut of a mon bisohten ant seiden ȝef þu heonne drivest us do us i þeos swin her þe eoden þer an heorde ant he ȝettede ham lo hu ha ne mahten nawt fule swin swenchen wiþuten his leave ant te swin ananriht urnen an urn to þe sea to adrenchen hamseolven seinte swa he stonc to þe swin þet ham wes leovre to adrenchen ham seolven þen forte beoren him ant an unseli sunful godes ilicnesse bereþ him in his breoste ant ne nimeþ neaver ȝeme al þet he dude eaver he nom leve þerof ed ure laverd þe tale i dyaloge lokiþ þet ȝe cunnen hu þe hali mon wes iwunet to seggen to þe deofles neddre ȝef þu havest leave do sting ȝef þu maht ant bead forþ his cheke ah he nefde þa nan bute to offearen him ȝef bileave him trukede ant hwen godd ȝeveþ him leave on his leove children hwi is hit bute for hare muchele biheve þah hit ham grevi sare þe seste confort is þet ure laverd hwen he þoleþ þet we beon itemptet he pleieþ wiþ us as þe moder wiþ hire ȝunge deorling fliþ from him ant hut hire ant let him sitten ane ant lokin ȝeorne abuten cleopien dame dame ant wepen ane hwile ant þenne wiþ spredde earmes leapeþ lahhinde forþ cluppeþ ant cusseþ ant wipeþ his ehnen swa ure laverd let us ane iwurþen oþerhwile ant wiþdraheþ his grace his cunfort ant his elne þet we ne findeþ swetnesse i na þing þet we wel doþ ne savur of heorte ant þah i þet ilke point ne luveþ us ure laverd neaver þe leasse ah deþ hit for muche luve ant þet understod wel daviþ þa he seide allunge quoþ he laverd ne leaf þu me nawt lo hu he walde þet he leafde him ah nawt allunge ant six acheisuns notiþ hwi godd for ure god wiþdraheþ him oþerhwiles an is þet we ne pruden anoþer þet we cnawen ure ahne feblesce ure muchele unstrengþe ant ure wacnesse ant þis is a swiþe muche god as seint seiþ þet is muche godnesse hit is to cnawen wel his wrecchehead ant his wacnesse hwet wat he seiþ þe þet is unfondet ant seint bereþ seint witnesse wiþ þeose wordes betere is þe þe truddeþ ant ofsecheþ wel ut his ahne feblesce þen þe þe meteþ hu heh is þe heovene ant hu deop þe eorþe hwen twa beoreþ a burþerne ant te oþer leaveþ hit þenne mei þe þe up haldeþ hit felen hu hit weieþ alswa leove suster hwil þet godd wiþ þe bereþ þi temptatiun nast tu neaver hu hevi hit is ant forþi ed sumchearre he leaveþ þe ane þet tu understonde þin ahne feblesce ant his help cleopie ant ȝeie lude efter him ȝef he is to longe hald hit wel þe hwile up ne derve hit te se sare hwase is siker of sucurs þet him schal cume sone ant ȝelt tah up his castel to his wiþeriwines swiþe he is to edwiten þencheþ her of þe tale hu þe hali mon in his fondunge seh bi west toȝeines him se muche ferd of deoflen ant forleas for muche dred þe strengþe of his bileave aþet te oþre seide him bihald quoþ he bi esten we habbeþ ma þen heo beoþ to help on ure halve for þe þridde þing is þet tu neaver ne beo al siker for sikernesse streoneþ ȝemeles ant overhohe ant ba þeose streoniþ inobedience þe feorþe acheisun is hwi ure laverd hut him þet tu seche him ȝeornluker ant cleopie ant wepe efter him as deþ þe lutel baban efter his moder þerefter is þe fifte þet tu his ȝeincume undervo þe gleadluker þe seste þet tu þe refter þe wisluker wite him hwen þu havest icaht him ant festluker halde ant segge wiþ his leofmon þeose six reisuns beoþ under þe seste frovre þe ȝe mahen habben mine leove sustren aȝeines fondunge þe seoveþe confort is þet alle þe hali halhen weren wodeliche itemptet nim of þe heste on alre earst to seinte seide ure laverd lo quoþ he is ȝeorne abuten forte ridli þe ut of mine icorene ah ich habbe for þe bisoht þet ti bileave allunge ne trukie seint hefde as he teleþ himseolf flesches pricunge ant bed ure laverd ȝeorne þet he dude hit from him ant he nalde ah seide þet is mi grace schal wite þe þet tu ne beo overcumen beo strong in unstrengþe þet is muche mihte alle þe oþre beoþ icrunet þurh feht of fondunge seinte sare nes ha fulle þreottene ȝer itemptet of hire flesch ah forþi þet ha wiste þet i þe muchele angoise aras þe muchele mede nalde ha neaver eanes bisechen ure laverd þet he allunge delivrede hire þe rof ah þis wes hire bone laverd ȝef me strengþe forte wiþstonden efter þreottene ȝer com þe acursede gast þe hefde hire itemptet blac ase blamon ant bigon to greden sare þu havest me overcumen ant heo him ondswerede þu lihest quoþ ha ful þing nawt ich ah haveþ mi laverd lo þe sweoke hu he walde makien hire aleast to leapen into prude ah ha wes wel war þe rof ant turnde al þe meistrie to godes strengþe sein seint ant te oþre wel ȝe witen hu ha weren itemptet ant þurh þe temptatiuns ipruvede to treowe champiuns ant swa wiþ rihte ofserveden kempene crune ant þis is þe eahtuþe elne þet alswa as þe goltsmiþ cleanseþ þet gold i þe fur alswa deþ godd te sawle i fur of fondunge þe niheþe confort is þet ȝef þe feond wiþ fondunge greveþ þe sare þu grevest him hwen þu edstondest hundret siþe sarre for þreo reisuns nomeliche þe an is þet he forleoseþ as origene seiþ his strengþe forte temptin eaver mare þeronuven of swuch manere sunne þe oþer is þet he forþluker echeþ his pine þe þridde fret his heorte of sar grome ant of teone þet he unþonc hise teþ i þe temptatiun þet tu stondest aȝein muchleþ þi mede ant for pine þet he wende forte drahe þe toward breideþ þe crune of blisse ant nawt ane an ne twa ah ase feole siþen as þu overkimest him ase feole crunen þet is to seggen ase feole mensken of misliche murhþen for swa sein seiþ þe tale i witneþ þis ilke of þe deciple þe set bivoren his meistre ant his meistre warþ o slepe hwil þet he learde him ant slepte aþet midniht þa he awakede art tu quoþ he ȝet her ga ant slep swiþe þe hali mon his meistre warþ eft o slep sone as þe þe hefde þerbivoren ibeon i muche wecche ant seh a swiþe feier stude ant iset forþ a trone ant þe ron seove crunen ant com a stevene ant seide þis sege ant þeose crunen haveþ þin deciple þis ilke niht ofsarvet ant te hali mon abreaid ant cleopede him to him sei quoþ he hu stod te hwil þu as ich slepte sete bivore me ich þohte quoþ he ofte þet ich walde awakenin þe ant for þu sleptest swote ne mahte ich for reowþe ant þenne þohte ich gan awei to slepen for me luste ant nalde bute leave hu ofte quoþ his meister over come þu þi þoht þus seove siþen seide he þa understond his meister wel hwet weren þe seove crunen seove cunne blissen þet his deciple hefde in euch a chearre ofservet þet he wiþseide þe feond ant overcom himseolven al þus leove sustren i wreastlunge of temptatiun ariseþ þe biȝete ne schal nan beon icrunet seiþ seinte bute hwase strongliche ant treoweliche fehteþ aȝein þe world aȝein himseolf aȝein þe feond of helle þeo fehteþ treoweliche þe hu se ha eaver beoþ iweorret wiþ þeos þreo wiþeriwines nomeliche of þe flesch hwuch se eaver þe lust beo se hit meadluker is wrinniþ aȝein festluker ant wiþseggeþ þe grant þe rof wiþ anewile heorte ne prokie hit se swiþe þeo þe þus doþ beoþ feolahes for ha doþ as he dude honginde o rode þet is he smahte þet bittre drunch ant wiþdroh him anan ant nalde hit nawt drinken þah he ofþurst were heo is þe swa deþ wiþ godd on his rode þah hire þurste i þe lust ant te deovel beot hire his healewi to drinken understonde ant þenche þah þet ter is galle under ant tah hit beo a pine betere is forte þolien þurst þen to beon iattret let lust overgan ant hit te wule eft likin hwil þe ȝicchunge least hit þuncheþ god to gnuddin ah þe refter me feleþ hit bitterliche smeorten weilawei ant moni an is for muchel heate se swiþe ofþurst mid alle þet hwil ha drinkeþ þet drunch ne beo hit ne se bitter ne feleþ ha hit neaver ah gluccheþ in ȝiverliche ne nimeþ neaver ȝeme hwen hit is al over spit ant schakeþ þet heaved feþ on forte nivelin ant makien grim chere ah to leate þenne nautforþi for efter uvel god is penitence þet is þe best þenne speowen hit anan ut wiþ schrift to þe preoste for leave hit inwiþ hit wule deaþ breden forþi mine leove sustren beoþ bivoren warre ant efter þe frovren þe beoþ her iwritene aȝein alle fondunges secheþ þeose salven aȝein alle temptatiuns ant nomeliche aȝein fleschliche salven beoþ ant bote under godes grace halie meditatiuns inwarde ant meadlese ant angoisuse bonen hardi bileave redunge veasten wecchen ant licomliche swinkes oþres frovre forte speoke toward i þe ilke stunde þet hire stont stronge eadmodnesse freolec of heorte ant alle gode þeawes beoþ armes i þis feht ant anrednesse of luve over alle þe oþre þe his wepnen warpeþ awei him luste beon iwundet hali meditatiuns beoþ bicluppet in a vers þet wes ȝare itaht ow mine leove sustren þet is þench ofte wiþ sar of þine sunnen þench of helle wa of heoveriches wunnen þench of þin ahne deaþ of godes deaþ o rode þe grimme dom of domesdei munneþ ofte i mode þench hu fals is þe worlt hwucche beoþ hire meden þench hwet hest godd for his god deden euchan of þeose word walde a long hwile forte beo wel iopenet ah ȝef ich hihi forþward demeori ȝe þe lengre a word ich segge efter ower sunnen hwense ȝe þencheþ of helle wa ant of heoveriches wunnen understondeþ þet godd walde o sum wise schawin ham to men i þis world bi worltliche pinen ant worltliche wunnen ant schaweþ ham forþ as schadewe for na lickre ne beoþ ha to þe wunne of heovene ne to þe wa of helle þen is schadewe to þet þing þet hit is of schadewe ȝe beoþ over þis worldes sea up þe brugge of heovene lokiþ þet ȝe ne beon nawt þe hors eschif iliche þe schuncheþ for a schadewe ant falleþ adun i þe weater of þe hehe brugge to childene ha beoþ þe fleoþ a peinture þe þuncheþ ham grislich ant grureful to bihalden wa ant wunne i þis world al nis bute peintunge al nis bute schadewe nawt ane hali meditatiuns as of ure laverd ant of alle his werkes ant of alle his wordes of þe deore leafdi ant of alle hali halhen ah oþre þohtes sum chearre i meadlese fondunges habbeþ iholpen fowr cunne nomeliche to þeo þe beoþ of flesches fondunges meadlese asailet dredfule wunderfule gleadfule ant sorhfule willes wiþute neod arearet i þe heorte as þenchen hwet tu waldest don ȝef þu sehe openliche stonde bivore þe ant ȝeoniende wide upo þe þen deovel of helle as he deþ dearnliche i þe fondunge ȝef me ȝeide fur fur þet te chirche bearnde ȝef þu herdest burgurs breoke þine wahes þeos ant oþre þulliche dredfule þohtes wunderfule ant gleadfule as ȝef þu sehe ant herdest him easki þe hwet te were leovest efter þi salvatiun ant þine leoveste freond of þing o þisse live ant beode þe cheosen wiþ þet tu wiþstode ȝef þu sehe al witerliche heovene ware ant helle ware i þe temptatiun bihalde þe ane ȝef me come ant talde þe þet mon þet te is leovest þurh sum miracle as þurh stevene of heovene were icoren to pape ant alle oþre swucche wunderfule ant sorhfule as ȝef þu herdest seggen þet mon þet te is leovest were ferliche adrenct islein oþer imurþret þet tine sustren weren in hare hus forbearnde þulliche þohtes ofte i fleschliche sawlen wrencheþ ut sonre fleschliche temptatiuns þen sum of þe oþre earre inwarde ant meadlese ant ancrefule bonen biwinneþ sone sucurs ant help ed ure laverd aȝeines flesches fondunges ne beon ha neaver se ancrefule ne se fulitohene þe deovel of helle duteþ ham swiþe for teke þet ha draheþ adun sucurs aȝein him ant godes hond of heovene ha doþ him twa hearmes bindeþ him ant bearneþ lo her preove of baþe an hali mon wes in his bonen ant com þe feond fleonninde bi þe lufte ant schulde al on toward te west half of þe worlt þurh heast þe empereur ant warþ ibunden heteveste wiþ þe hali monne bonen þe oftoken him as ha fluhen uppard toward heovene þet he ne mahte hider ne þider ten dahes fulle nabbe ȝe alswa of ruffin þe deovel broþer in ower englische boc of seinte of þet oþer me redeþ þet he gredde lude to sein þe muchel wes i benen wa me þine beoden forbearneþ me hwase mei þurh godes ȝeove i beoden habbe teares ha mei don wiþ godd al þet ha eaver wule for swa we redeþ eadi bone softeþ ant paieþ ure laverd ah teares doþ him strengþe beoden smirieþ him wiþ softe olhnunge ah teares prikieþ him ne ne ȝeoveþ him neaver pes ear þen he ȝetti ham al þet ha easkiþ hwen me asaileþ burhes oþer castel þeo wiþinnen healdeþ scaldinde weater ut ant werieþ swa þe walles ant ȝe don alswa as ofte as þe feond asaileþ ower castel ant te sawle burh wiþ in warde bonen warpeþ ut upon him scaldinde teares þet daviþ segge bi þe þu havest forscaldet te drake heaved wiþ wallinde weater þet is wiþ hate teares þear as þis weater is sikerliche þe feond fliþ leste he beo forscaldet eft anoþer castel þe haveþ dich abuten ant weater beo i þe dich þe castel is wel carles aȝeines his unwines castel is euch god mon þet te deovel weorreþ ah habbe ȝe deop dich of deop eadmodnesse ant wete teares þerto ȝe beoþ strong castel þe weorrur of helle mei longe asailin ow ant leosen his hwile eft me seiþ ant soþ hit is þet a muche wind aliþ wiþ a lute rein ant te sunne þe refter schineþ þe schenre alswa a muche temptatiun þet is þe feondes bleas afealleþ wiþ a softe rein of ane lut wordes teares ant te soþe sunne schineþ þe refter schenre to þe sawle þus beoþ teares gode wiþ inwarde bonen ant ȝef ȝe understondeþ ich habbe iseid of ham her fowr muchele efficaces forhwi ha beoþ to luvien in alle ower neoden sendeþ cwicliche anan þes sonde toward heovene for as seiþ þet is þe eadmodies bone þurleþ þe weolcne ant ter seiþ seint o muchel is þe mihte of schir ant cleane bone þe fliþ up ant kimeþ in bivoren almihti godd ant deþ þe ernde se wel þet godd haveþ o lives boc iwriten al þet ha seiþ as sein witneþ edhalt hire wiþ himseolf ant sent adun his engel to don al þet ha easkeþ nule ich her of bone segge na mare hardi bileave bringeþ þe deovel o fluht ananrihtes þet witneþ sein edstont ane þe feond ant he deþ him o fluhte edstond þurh hwet strengþe seinte teacheþ stondeþ aȝein him wiþ stronge bileave beoþ hardi of godes help ant witeþ hu he is wac þe na strengþe naveþ on us bute of usseolven ne mei he bute schawin forþ sumhwet of his eapeware ant olhnin oþer þreatin þet me bugge þe rof hweþer se he deþ scarniþ him lahheþ þe alde eape lude to bismere þurh treowe bileave ant he halt him ischent ant deþ him o fluht swiþe þet is þe hali halhen alle overcomen þurh bileave þe deofles rixlunge þet nis bute sunne for ne rixleþ he i nan bute þurh sunne ane neomeþ nu gode ȝeme hu alle þe seovene deadliche sunnen muhen beon afleiet þurh treowe bileave on earst nu of prude hwa halt him muchel as þe prude deþ hwen he bihalt hu lutel þe muchele laverd makede him inwiþ a povre meidenes breoste hwa is ontful þe bihalt wiþ ehnen of bileave hu godd nawt for his god ah for oþres god dude ant seide ant þolede al þet he þolede þe ontfule ne kepte nawt þet eani dealde of his god ant godd almihti ȝet efter al þet oþer lihte dun to helle for te sechen feolahes ant to deale wiþ ham þe god þet he hefde lo nu hu frommard beoþ ontfule ure laverd þe ancre þe wearnde anoþer a cwaer to lane feor ha hefde heoneward hire bileave ehe hwa halt wreaþþe þe bihalt þet god lihte on eorþe to makien þreofald sahte bitweone mon ant mon bitweone godd ant mon bitweone mon ant engel ant efter his ariste þa he com ant schawde him þis wes his gretunge to his deore deciples sahtnesse beo bitweonen ow neomeþ nu ȝeorne ȝeme hwen leof freond went from oþer þe leaste wordes þet he seiþ þeo schulen beo best edhalden ure laverdes leaste wordes þa he steah to heovene ant leafde his leove freond in uncuþe þeode weren of swote luve ant of sahtnesse þet is sahtnesse ich do imong ow sahtnesse ich leave wiþ ow þis wes his druerie þet he leafde ant ȝef ham in his departunge lokiþ nu ȝeorne for his deorewurþe luve hwuch a mearke he leide upon his icorene þa he steah to heovene bi þet ȝe schulen icnawen quoþ he þet ȝe beoþ mine deciples ȝef swete luve ant sahtnesse is eaver ow bitweonen godd hit wite ant he hit wat me were leovere þet ȝe weren alle o þe spiteluvel þen ȝe weren ontfule oþer feol iheortet for is al luve ant i luve he resteþ him ant haveþ his wununge þet is i sahtnesse is godes stude ant hwerse sahte is ant luve þear he bringeþ to nawt al þes deofles strengþe þer he brekeþ his bohe hit seiþ þet beoþ dearne fondunges þet he scheot of feor ant his sweord baþe þet beoþ temptatiuns keorvinde of neh ant kene neomeþ nu ȝeorne ȝeme bi moni forbisne hu god is anrednesse of luve ant annesse of heorte for nis þing under sunne þet me is leovere ne se leof þet ȝe habben nute ȝe þer men fehteþ i þes stronge ferdes þe ilke þe haldeþ ham feaste togederes ne muhe beo descumfit o neaver nane wise alswa hit is in gastelich feht aȝeines þe deovel al his entente is forte tweamen heorten forte bineomen luve þet halt men togederes for hwen luve aliþ þenne beoþ ha i sundret ant te deovel deþ him bitweonen ananriht ant sleaþ on euche halve dumbe beastes habbeþ þis ilke warschipe þet hwen ha beoþ asailet of wulf oþer of liun ha þrungeþ togederes al þe floc feste ant makieþ scheld of ham seolf euch of heom to oþer ant beoþ þe hwile sikere ȝef eani unseli went ut hit is sone awuriet þe þridde þer an geaþ him ane in a slubbri wei he slit ant falleþ sone þer monie gaþ togederes ant euch halt oþres hond ȝef eani feþ to sliden þe oþer hine breid up ear he ful falle ȝef ha wergiþ euchan halt him bi oþer fondunge is sliddrunge þurh wergunge beoþ bitacnet þe unþeawes un der slawþe þe beoþ inempnet þe ruppe þis is þet sein seiþ alswa i strong wind ant swifte weattres þe me mot overwaden of monie euch halt oþer þe isundrede is iswipt forþ ant forfeareþ eaver to wel we witen hu þe wei of þis world is slubbri hu þe wind ant te stream of fondunge aren stronge muche neod is þet euch halde wiþ bisie bonen ant wiþ luve oþres honden for as seiþ wa eaver þe ane for hwen he falleþ naveþ he hwa him areare nan nis ane þe haveþ godd to fere ant þet is euch þet soþ luve haveþ in his heorte þe seoveþe forbisne is þis ȝef ȝe riht telleþ dust ant greot as ȝe seoþ for hit is isundret ant nan ne halt to oþer a lutel windes puf todriveþ hit al to nawt þear hit is in a clot ilimet togederes hit liþ al stille an hondful of ȝerden beoþ earveþ to breoken hwil ha beoþ togederes euchan itweamet lihtliche bersteþ a treo þe wule fallen undersete hit wiþ anoþer ant hit stont feste tweam ham ant ba falleþ nu ȝe habbeþ nihene þus i þinges ute wiþ neomeþ forbisne hu god is annesse of luve ant sometreadnesse þet halt þe gode somet þet nan ne mei forwurþen ant þis wule iwiss habben þe rihte bileave bihald ȝeorne ant understont deorewurþe wordes ant werkes þe i luve weren alle ant i swetnesse over alle þing ich walde þet ancren leorneden wel þis lesceunes lare for monie mare hearm is beoþ foxes þe hefden þe neb euchan iwend frommard oþer ant weren bi þe teiles iteiet togederes as teleþ ant in euchanes teil a blease bearninde of þeose foxes ich spec feor þe ruppe ah nawt o þisse wise neomeþ gode ȝeme hwet þis beo to seggen me turneþ þe neb bliþeliche towart þing þet me luveþ ant frommard þing þet me heateþ þeo þenne habbeþ þe nebbes wrongwende euch frommard oþer hwen nan ne luveþ oþer ah bi þe teiles ha beoþ somet ant beoreþ þes deofles bleasen þe brune of galnesse on anoþer wise teil bitacneþ ende in hare ende ha schulen beon ibunden togederes as weren foxes bi þe teiles ant iset bleasen þe rin þet is þet fur of helle al þis is iseid mine leove sustren þet ower leove nebbes beon eaver iwent somet wiþ luveful semblant ant wiþ swote chere þet ȝe beon aa wiþ annesse of an heorte ant of a wil ilimet togederes as hit iwriten is bi ure laverdes deore deciples þis wes godes gretunge to his deore deciples griþ beo bimong ow ȝe beoþ þe ancren of englond swa feole togederes twenti nuþe oþer ma godd i god ow multi þet meast griþ is among meast annesse ant anrednesse ant somet readnesse of anred lif efter a riwle swa þet alle teoþ an alle iturnt anesweis ant nan frommard oþer efter þet word is forþi ȝe gaþ wel forþ ant spedeþ in ower wei for euch is wiþward oþer in an manere of liflade as þah ȝe weren an cuvent of lundene ant of oxnefort of schreobsburi oþer of chester þear as alle beoþ an wiþ an imeane manere ant wiþuten singularite þet is anful frommardschipe lah þing i religiun for hit towarpeþ annesse ant manere i meane þet ah to beon in ordre þis nu þenne þet ȝe beoþ alle as an cuvent is ower hehe fame þis is godd icweme þis is nunan wide cuþ swa þet ower cuvent biginneþ to spreaden toward englondes ende ȝe beoþ as þe moder hus þet heo beoþ of istreonet ȝe beoþ ase wealle ȝef þe wealle woreþ þe strunden woriþ alswa a wei la ȝef ȝe woriþ ne bide ich hit neaver ȝef ei is imong ow þe geaþ i singularite ant ne folheþ nawt þe cuvent ah went ut of þe floc þet is as in a cloistre þet is heh priur over went ut as a teowi schep ant meapeþ hire ane into breres teilac into wulves muþ toward te þrote of helle ȝef ei swuch is imong ow godd turne hire into floc wende hire into cuvent ant leve ow þe beoþ þe rin swa halden ow þe rin þet godd þe hehe priur neome ow on ende þeonne up into þe cloistre of heovene hwil ȝe haldeþ ow in an offearen ow mei þe feond ȝef he haveþ leave ah hearmin nawt mid alle þet he wat ful wel ant is forþi umben deies ant nihtes to unlimin ow wiþ wreaþþe oþer wiþ luþer onde ant sent mon oþer wummon þe telle þe an bi þe oþer sum suhinde sahe þet suster ne schulde nawt segge bi suster ower nan ich forbeode ow ne leve þe deofles sondesmon ah lokiþ þet euch of ow i cnawe wel hwen he spekeþ i þe uvele monnes tunge ant segge ananrihtes ure meistre haveþ iwriten us as in heast to halden þet we tellen him al þet euch of oþer hereþ ant forþi loke þe þet tu na þing ne telle me þet ich ne muhe him tellen þe mei don þe amendement ant con swaliches don hit þet ich ant tu baþe ȝef we beoþ i þe soþ schule beon unblamet euch noþeles warni oþer þurh ful siker sondesmon sweteliche ant luveliche as hire leove suster of þing þet ha misnimeþ ȝef ha hit wat to soþe ant makie hwase bereþ þet word recordin hit ofte bivoren hire ear ha ga hu ha wule seggen þet ha ne segge hit oþerweis ne cluti þerto mare for a lute clut mei ladlechin swiþe a muchel hal pece þeo þe ed hire suster þis luvesalve underveþ þoncki hire ȝeorne ant segge wiþ þe salmwruhte ant þe refter wiþ ȝef ha ne luvede me nalde ha nawt warni me i misericorde leovere me beoþ hire wunden þen fikiende cosses þus ondswerie eaver ant ȝef hit is oþerweis þen þe oþer understont sende hire word aȝein þe rof luveliche ant softe ant te oþer leve ananriht for þet ich chulle alswa þet euch of ow luvie oþer as hire seolven ȝef þe feond bitweonen ow toblaweþ eani wreaþþe oþer great heorte þet forbeode ear ha beo iset wel nawt ane to neomen godes flesch ant his blod ne wurþe nan se witles ah ȝet þet is leasse þet ha eanes ne bihalde þeron ne loki i ful wreaþþe toward him þe lihte to mon in eorþe of heovene to makien þreovald sahte as is iseid þe ruppe sende eiþer þenne oþer word þet ha haveþ imaket hire as þah ha were bivoren hire eadmodliche ant þeo þe ear ofdraheþ þus luve of hire suster ant ofgeaþ sahte ant nimeþ þe gult toward hire þah þe oþer hit habbe mare ha schal beo mi deorewurþe ant mi deore dohter for ha is godes dohter he himseolf hit seiþ þus prude ant onde ant wreaþþe beoþ ihwer afleiet hwerse soþ luve is ant treowe bileave to godes milde werkes ant luvefule wordes ga we nu forþre to þe oþre on a reawe hwa mei beo for scheome slummi sloggi ant slaw þe bihalt hu swiþe bisi ure laverd wes on eorþe efter al þet oþer bihaldeþ hu he i þe even of his lif swong o þe hearde rode oþre habbeþ reste fleoþ liht i chambre hudeþ ham hwen ha beoþ ilete blod on an earm eþre ant he o munt calvaire steah ȝet o rode herre ne ne swong neaver mon se swiþe ne se sare as he dude þet ilke dei þet he bledde o fif half brokes of ful brade wunden ant deope wiþuten þe eþren þe bledden on his heaved under þe kene þornene crune ant wiþuten þe ilke reowfule garces of þe luþere scurgunge ȝont al his leofliche lich nawt ane o þe schonken toȝeines slawe ant sleperes is swiþe openliche his earliche ariste from deaþe to live aȝeines ȝisceunge is his muchele poverte þe weox eaver upon him se lengre se mare for þa he wes iboren earst þe þet wrahte þe eorþe ne fond nawt on eorþe swa muche place as his lutle licome mahte beon ileid upon swa nearow wes þet stude þet unneaþe his moder ant josep seten þe rin ant swa ha leiden him on heh up in a crecche wiþ clutes biwrabbet as þet godspel seiþ þus feire he wes ischrud þe heovenliche schuppent þe schrudeþ þe sunne herefter þe povre meiden of heovene fostrede him ant fedde wiþ hire lutle milc as meiden deh to habben þis wes muche poverte ah mare com þerefter for lanhure þe ȝet he hefde fode as feol to him ant i stude of in his cradel herbearhede him seoþþen as he meande him nefde he hwer he mahte his heaved huden þus povre he wes of in of mete he wes se neodful þet þa he hefde i o palmsunnedei al dei ipreachet ant hit neolechede niht he lokede abuten hit seiþ i þe godspel ȝef ei walde cleopien him to mete oþer to herbearhe ah nes þer nan ant swa he wende ut of þe muchele burh into beþanie to hus ant to marþen þeras he eode mid his deciples sumchearre ha breken þe eares bi þe wei ant gnuddeden þe curnles ut bitweonen hare honden ant eten for hunger ant weren þervore swiþe icalenget ah alre meast poverte com ȝet herefter for steortnaket he wes despuilet o þe rode þa he meande him of þurst weater ne mahte he habben ȝet þet meast wunder is of al þe brade eorþe ne moste he habben a grot forte deien upon þe rode hefde a fot oþer lute mare ant þet wes to his pine hwen þe worldes wealdent walde beo þus povre unbilevet he is þe luveþ to muchel ant ȝisceþ worldes weole ant wunne aȝein glutunie is his povre pitance þet he hefde o rode twa manere men habbeþ neode to eote wel swinkinde ant blodletene þe dei þet he wes baþe i sar swinc ant ilete blod as ich nest seide nes his pitance o rode bute a spunge of galle loke nu hwa gruccheþ ȝef ha þencheþ wel heron mistrum mel of unsavuree metes of povre pitance of na mon ne of na wummon ne schule ȝe makie na man ne pleainin ow of na wone bute to sum treowe freond þet hit mei amendin ant godin ham oþer ow ant þet beo priveiliche iseid as under seel of schrift þet ȝe ne beon iblamet ȝef ȝe of ei þing habbeþ wone ant sum freond ȝeorne freini ow ȝef ȝe ei wone habbeþ ȝef ȝe hopieþ god of him ondswerieþ þis wise laverd godd forȝelde þe ich drede mare ich habbe þen ich were wurþe ant leasse wone ich þolie þen me neod were ȝef he easkeþ ȝeornluker þonkiþ him ȝeorne ant seggeþ ich ne dear nawt lihen o meseolven wone ich habbe ase riht is hwuch ancre kimeþ into ancrehus to habben hire eise ah nu þu wult hit alles witen ure laverd te forȝelde þis is nu an þing þet ich hefde neode to ant þus bid ure riwle þet we schawin to gode freond as oþre godes povre doþ hare meoseise wiþ milde eadmodnesse ne nawt ne schule we forsaken þe grace of godes sonde ah þonkin him ȝeorne leste he wreaþe him wiþ us ant wiþdrahe his large hond ant þe refter wiþ to muche wone abeate ure prude ant nis hit muchel hofles hwen godd beot his hond forþ puttinde hire aȝein segge ne kepe ich hit nawt have þeseolf ich wulle fondin ȝef ich mei libben herbuten þurh þis ich habbe iherd of swuch þet nom uvel ende aȝein leccherie is his iborenesse of þet cleane meiden ant al his cleane lif þet he leadde on eorþe ant alle þe hine fuleden þus lo þe articles þet beoþ as þah me seide þe liþes of ure bileave onont godes monhead hwase inwardliche bihalt ham fehteþ toȝein þe feond þe fondeþ us wiþ þeose deadliche sunnen forþi seiþ seinte armiþ ow he seiþ wiþ þoht upo þe in ure flesch wes ipinet ant seinte þencheþ þencheþ seiþ seinte hwen ȝe wergiþ i feht aȝeines þe deovel hu ure laverd seolf wiþseide his fleschliche wil ant wiþseggeþ ower ȝet nabbe ȝe nawt wiþstonden aþet te schedunge of ower blod as he dude of his for ow aȝeines himseolven anont he mon wes of ure cunde ȝet ȝe habbeþ þet ilke blod þet ilke blisfule bodi þet com of þe meiden ant deide o þe rode niht ant dei bi ow nis bute a wah bitweonen ant euche dei he kimeþ forþ ant schaweþ him to ow fleschliche ant licomliche inwiþ þe measse biwrixlet þah on oþres lite under breades furme for in his ahne ure ehnen ne mahten nawt þe brihte sihþe þolien ah swa he schaweþ him ow as þah he seide lowr ich her hwet wulle ȝe seggeþ me hwet were ow leof hwerto neodeþ ow meaneþ ower neode ȝef þe feondes ferd þet beoþ his temptatiuns asailiþ ow swiþe ondswerieþ him ant seggeþ ȝe laverd wunder is we beoþ iloget her bi þe þet art stan of help tur of treowe sucurs castel of strengþe ant te deofles ferd is woddre upon us þen upon eani oþre þis ich neome of for þer hit teleþ al þus þet israel godes folc com ant logede him bi þe stan of help ant te comen into afech beoþ unwihtes afech on ebreisch spealeþ neowe wodschipe swa hit is witerliche hwen mon logeþ him bi ure laverd þenne on earst biginneþ þe deovel to weden ah þer hit teleþ þet israel wende sone þe rug ant weren fowr þusent i þe fluht sariliche i sleine ne wende ȝe nawt te rug mine leove sustren ah wiþstondeþ þe feondes ferd amidde þe forheaved as is iseid þe ruppe wiþ stronge bileave ant wiþ þe gode sendeþ beode sondesmon sone efter sucurs to þe prince of heovene þis is þet englisch in us nis nawt deorewurþe laverd swa muchel strengþe þet we mahen wiþstonden þe deofles ferd þe is se strong upon us ah hwen we swa beoþ bisteaþet swa stronge bistonden þet we mid alle na read ne cunnen bi usseolven þis an we mahe don heoven ehnen up to þe mildfule laverd þu send us sucurs þu todreaf ure fan for to þe we lokiþ þus wiþ þe gode hwen godd kimeþ bivoren ow ant freineþ hwet ȝe wulleþ ant in euch time hwen ȝe neode habbeþ schawiþ hit swa sweteliche to his swote earen ȝef he sone ne hereþ ow ȝeieþ luddre ant meadlesluker ant þreatiþ þet ȝe wulleþ ȝelden up þe castel bute he sende ow sonre help ant hihi þe swiþere ah wite ȝe hu he ondswerede þe gode þus o þisse wise þus he onswereþ ow hwen ȝe help cleopieþ ne beo ȝe nawt offearede ne drede ȝe ham nawiht þah ha beon stronge ant monie þe feht is min nawt ower sulement stondeþ sikerliche ant ȝe schulen seon mi sucurs habbeþ ane to me trusti bileave ant ȝe beoþ al sikere lokiþ nu hwuch help is hardi bileave for al þet help þe godd bihat þe strengþe to stonde wel al is in hire ane hardi bileave makeþ stonden upriht ant te unwiht nis nawt laþre forþi þis is his word in buh þe he seiþ duneward þet ich mahe over þe þeo buheþ hire þe to hise fondunges buheþ hire heorte for hwil ha stont upriht ne mei he nowþer upon hire rukin ne riden lo þe treitre hu he seiþ buh þe let me leapen up nule ich þe nawt longe riden ah ich chulle wenden over he liheþ seiþ sein ne lef þu nawt þen traitre nule he nawt wenden over ah wule ful feaste sitten sum wes þet lefde him þohte he schulde sone adun as he bihat eaver do he seiþ þis enchearre ant schrif þe þe rof tomarhen buh þin heorte let me up schec me wiþ schrift adun ȝef ich alles walde ride þe longe sum as ich seide lefde him ant beah him ant he leop up ant rad hire baþe dei ant niht twenti ȝer fulle þet is ha dude a sunne i þe ilke niht þurh his procunge ant þohte þet ha walde hire schriven ine marhen ant dude hit eft ant eft ant fealh swa i uvel wune þet ha lei ant rotede þe rin swa longe as ich seide ant ȝef a miracle nere þe pufte adun þen deovel þe set on hire se feaste ha hefde iturplet wiþ him baþe hors ant lade dun into helle grunde forþi mine leove sustren haldeþ ow efne upriht i treowe bileave hardiliche ileveþ þet al þe deofles strengþe mealteþ þurh þe grace of þet hali sacrement hest over oþre þet ȝe seoþ as ofte as þe preost measseþ þe meidene bearn godd godes sune þe licomliche lihteþ oþerhwiles to ower in ant inwiþ ow eadmodliche nimeþ his herbearhe deuleset ha beoþ to wake ant to unwreaste iheortet þe wiþ swilli gest hardiliche ne fehteþ ȝe schulen bileave habben þet al hali chirche deþ red oþer singeþ ant alle hire sacremenz strengeþ ow gasteliche ah nan ase forþ ase þis for hit bringeþ to noht al þes deofles wiheles nawt ane his strengþes ant his stronge turnes ah deþ his wiltfule crokes his wrenchfule wicchecreftes ant alle his ȝulunges ase lease swefnes false schawunges dredfule offearunges fikele ant sweokele reades as þah hit were o godes half ant god for te donne for þet is his unwrench as ich ear seide þet hali men meast dredeþ þet haveþ moni hali mon grimliche biȝulet hwen he ne mei nawt bringen to nan open uvel he sput to a þing þet þuncheþ god þu schuldest he seiþ beo mildre ant leoten iwurþe þi chast nawt trubli þin heorte ant sturien into wreaþþe þis he seiþ forþi þet tu ne schuldest nawt chastien for hire gult ne tuhte wel þi meiden ant bringe þe into ȝemeles i stude of eadmodnesse eft riht þertoȝeines ne let tu hire na gult toȝeves he seiþ ȝef þu wult þet ha drede þe hald hire nearowe rihtwisnesse he seiþ mot beo nede sturne ant þus he liteþ cruelte wiþ heow of rihtwisnesse me mei beon al to rihtwis betere is wis liste þen luþer strengþe hwen þu havest longe iwaket ant schuldest gan to slepen nu is vertu he seiþ wakien hwen hit greveþ þe sei ȝet a nocturne forhwi deþ he swa for þet tu schuldest slepen eft hwen time were to wakien eft riht þertoȝeines ȝef þet tu maht wakien wel he leiþ on þe an hevinesse oþer deþ i þi þoht wisdom is þinge best ich chulle ga nu to slepen ant arise nunan ant don cwicluker þene nu þet ich don nuþe schulde ant swa ofte inohreaþe ne dest tu hit i nowþer time of þis ilke materie ich spec muchel þe ruppe i þulliche temptatiuns nis nan se wis ne se war bute godd him warni þet nis bigilet ofte ah þis hehe sacrement in hardi bileave over alle oþre þing unwriþ hise wrenches ant brekeþ hise strengþes iwis leove sustren hwen ȝe neh ow feleþ him forhwon þet ȝe habben hardi bileave nulle ȝe bute lahhen him lude to bismere þet he is se muchel ald cang þe kimeþ his pine to echen ant breiden ow crune sone se he siþ ow hardi ant bald i godes grace his mihte mealteþ ant he fliþ sone ah ȝef he mei underȝeoten þet ower bileave falsi swa þet ow þunche þet ȝe mahten beon allunge ilead forþ over ȝef ȝe weren swiþe i þe ilke stude itemptet þerwiþ ȝe unstrengeþ ant his mihte waxeþ we redeþ i þet ysboset lei ant slepte ant sette a wummon ȝeteward þe windwede hweate ant comen sunen remon ant banaa ant funden þe wummon istunt of hire windwunge ant ifolen o slepe ant wenden in ant slohen ysboset þe unseli þet lokede him se uvele þe bitacnunge herof is muche neod to understonden ysboset on ebrew is mon bimeaset on englisch ant nis he witerliche ameaset ant ut of his witte þe amidden his unwines leiþ him to slepen þe ȝeteward is wittes skile þet ah to windwin hweate schaden þe eilen ant te chef from þe cleane cornes þet is þurh bisi warschipe sundri god from uvel don þe hweate i gerner ant puffen eaver awei þe deofles chef þet nis noht bute to helle smorþre ah þe bimeasede ysboset lo hu measeliche he dude sette a wummon to ȝeteward þet is feble warde weila as feole doþ þus wummon is þe reisun þet is wittes skile hwen hit unstrengeþ þe schulde beo monlich stealewurþe ant kene in treowe bileave þis ȝete ward liþ to slepen sone se me biginneþ to sunne leoten lust gan in ward ant te delit waxen hwen sunen þet beoþ helle bearnes i findeþ swa unwaker ant swa nesche ȝeteward ha gaþ in ant sleaþ ysboset þet is þe bimeasede gast þe in a slepi ȝemeles forȝemeþ himseolven þet nis nawt to forȝeoten þet as hali writ seiþ ha þurhstichden him dun into þe schere her seiþ sein þe feond þurhsticheþ þe schere hwen delit of leccherie þurleþ þe heorte ant þis nis bute i slep of ȝemeles ant of slawþe as sein witneþ þis is þet englisch hwen þe alde unwine siþ slepi ure skile he draheþ him anan toward hire ant feleþ wiþ hire i speche þenchest tu he seiþ hu þe spec oþer þeo of flesches galnesse ant spekeþ þus þe alde sweoke toward hire heorte wordes þet ha ȝare herde fulliche iseide oþer sihþe þet ha seh oþer hire ahne fulþen þet ha sumhwile wrahte al þis he put forþ bivore þe heorte ehnen forte bifulen hire wiþ þoht of alde sunnen hwen he ne mei wiþ neowe ant swa he bringeþ ofte aȝein into þe adotede sawle þurh licunge þe ilke sunnen þe þurh reowþful sar weren ibet ȝare swa þet heo mei wepen ant meanen sari man wiþ þe salmwruhte weilawei mine wunden þe weren feire ihealet gederiþ neowe wursum ant foþ on eft to rotien ihealet wunde þenne biginneþ to rotien hwen sunne þe wes ibet kimeþ eft wiþ licunge into munegunge ant sleaþ þe unwarre sawle al þis unlimp iwarþ þurh þe ȝetewardes slep þet nes war ant waker ne nes nawt monlich ah wes wummonlich eþ to overkeasten beo hit wummon beo hit mon þenne is al þe strengþe efter þe bileave ant efter þet me haveþ trust to godes help þet is neh bute bileave trukie as ich ear buven seide heo unstrengeþ þe unwiht ant deþ him fleon ananriht forþi beoþ eaver aȝein him hardi ase liun i treowe bileave nomeliche i þe fondunge þet ysboset deide on þet is galnesse lo hu ȝe mahe cnawen þet he is earh ant unwreast hwen he smit þiderward nis he earh champiun þe skirmeþ to ward te vet þe secheþ se lahe on his kempeifere flesches lust is fotes wunde as wes feor iseid þe ruppe ant þis is þe reisun as ure fet beoreþ us alswa ure lustes beoreþ us ofte to þing þet us luste efter nu þenne þah þi va hurte þe o þe vet þet is to seggen fondeþ wiþ flesches lustes for se lah wunde ne dred tu nawt to sare bute hit to swiþe swelle þurh skiles ȝettunge wiþ to muchel delit up toward te heorte ah drinc þenne atterlaþe ant drif þet swealm aȝeinward frommard te heorte þet is to seggen þench o þe attri pine þet godd dronc o þe rode ant te swealm schal setten prude ant onde ant wreaþþe heorte sar for worltlich þing dreori oflongunge ant ȝisceunge of ahte þeose beoþ heorte wunden ant al þet of ham floweþ ant ȝeoveþ deaþes dunt anan buten ha beon isalvet hwen þe feond smit þiderward þenne is iwis to dreden ant nawt for fotwunden prude salve is eadmodnesse ondes feolahlich luve wreaþþes þolemodnesse redunge misliche werkes gastelich frovre ȝisceunges overhohe of eorþliche þinges festschipes freo heorte þet is to seggen nu of þe earste on alre earst ȝef þu wult beon eadmod þench eaver hwet te wonteþ of halinesse ant of gasteliche þeawes þench hwet tu havest of þeseolf þu art of twa dalen of licome ant of sawle in eiþer beoþ twa þinges þe mahen muchel meokin þe ȝef þu ham wel bihaldest i þe licome is fulþe ant unstrengþe ne kimeþ of þet vetles swuch þing as þer is in of þi flesches fetles kimeþ þer smeal of aromaz oþer of swote basme deale drue spritlen beoreþ winberien breres rose blostmen þi flesch hwet frut bereþ hit in all his openunges amid te menske of þi neb þet is þe fehereste deal bitweonen muþes smech ant neases smeal ne berest tu as twa prive þurles nart tu icumen of ful slim nart tu fulþe fette ne bist tu wurme fode nu a flehe mei eili þe makie þe to blenchen eaþe maht tu pruden bihald hali men þe weren sumhwile hu ha feasten hu ha wakeden i hwuch passiun i hwuch swinc ha weren ant swa þu maht icnawen þin ahne wake unstrengþe ah wast tu hwet awildgeþ monnes feble ehnen þet is hehe iclumben þet he bihalt duneward alswa hwase bihalt to þeo þe beoþ of lah lif þet makeþ him þunchen þet he is of heh lif ah bihald aa uppart toward heovenliche men þe clumben se hehe ant þenne schalt tu seon hu lahe þu stondest feasten a seoveniht to weater ant to breade þreo niht togederes wakien hu walde hit unstrengen þi fleschliche strenge þus þeos twa þinges bihald i þi licome fulþe ant unstrengþe i þi sawle oþer twa sunne ant ignorance þet is unwisdom ant unweotenesse for ofte þet tu wenest god is uvel ant sawle morþre bihald wiþ wet ehe þine scheome sunnen dred ȝet þi wake cunde þet is eþwarpe ant sei wiþ þe hali mon þe bigon to wepen ant seide þa me talde him þet an of his feren wes wiþ a wummon i flesches fulþe ifallen þet is he todei ant ich to marhen as þah he seide of as unstrong cunde ich am as he wes ant al swuch mei me ilimpen bute ȝef godd me halde þus lo þe hali mon nefde he of þe oþres fal na wunderlich overhohe ant biweop his unhap ant dredde þet him a swuch mahte bitiden o þis wise eadmodieþ ant meokiþ owseolven þet is alswa as prude is wilnunge of wurþschipe riht alswa þertoȝeines eadmodnesse is forkeastunge of wurþschipe ant luve of lutel hereword ant of lahnesse þis þeaw is alre þeawene moder ant streoneþ ham alle þe is umben wiþuten hire to gederin gode þeawes he bereþ dust i þe wind as sein seiþ þeos ane biþ iborhen þeos ane wiþbuheþ þe deofles grunen of helle as ure laverd schawde to seint þe seh al þe world ful of þe deofles tildunge a laverd quoþ he hwa mei wiþ þeose witen him þet he ne beo wiþ sum ilaht ane þe þolemode quoþ he ure laverd swa sutil þing is eadmodnesse ant swa gentilliche smeal ant se smuhel þet na grune ne mei hire edhalden ant lo muche wunder þah ha hire makie swa smeal ant se meoke ha is þinge strengest swa þet of hire is euch gastelich strengþe seint hit witneþ ah seiþ þe reisun hwi þeras eadmodnesse is þer he seiþ is þet is his feader wisdom ant his feader strengþe nis na wunder þenne þah strengþe beo þeras he is þurh his inwuniende grace þurh þe strengþe of eadmodnesse he weorp þe þurs of helle þe ȝape wreastlere nimeþ ȝeme hwet turn his fere ne kunne nawt þet he wiþ wreastleþ for wiþ þet turn he mei him unmundlunge warpen alswa dude ure laverd ant seh hu feole þe grimme wreastlere of helle breid upon his hupe ant weorp wiþ þe hancheturn into galnesse þe rixleþ i þe lenden hef on heh monie ant wende abuten wiþ ham ant swong ham þurh prude dun into helle grunde þohte ure laverd þe biheold al þis ich schal do þe a turn þet tu ne cuþest neaver ne ne maht neaver cunnen þe turn of eadmodnesse þet is þe fallinde turn ant feol from heovene to eorþe ant strahte him swa bi þe eorþe þet te feond wende þet he were al eorþlich ant wes bilurd wiþ þet turn ant is ȝet euche dei of eadmode men ant wummen þe hine wel cunnen on oþer half as seiþ he ne mei for prude ȝet bute bihalden hehe hali men þe haldeþ ham lutle ant of lah lif beoþ ut of his sihþe þe wilde bar ne mei nawt buhen him to smiten hwase falleþ adun ant þurh meoke eadmodnesse strecheþ him bi þer eorþe he is carles of his tuskes þis nis nawt toȝeines þet þet ich habbe i seid ear þet me schal stonden eaver toȝeines þe deovel for þet stondinge is treowe trust of hardi bileave upo godes strengþe þis fallunge is eadmod cnawunge of þin ahne wacnesse ant of þin unstrengþe ne nan ne mei stonde swa bute he þus falle þet is leote lutel tale ant unwurþ ant eþelich eaver of himseolven bihalde his blac ant nawt his hwit for hwit awilgeþ þe ehe eadmodnesse ne mei beon neaver ful preiset for þet wes þe lesceun þet ure laverd inwardlukest learde his icorene wiþ werc ba ant wiþ worde in hire he healdeþ nawt ane dropemel ah flowinde ȝeotteþ weallen of his graces as seiþ þe salmiste i þe dealen þu makest he seiþ weallen to springen heorte tobollen ant ihoven ase hul ne edhalt na wete of grace a bleddre ibollen of wind ne deveþ nawt into þeose halwende weattres ah a nelde prichunge warpeþ al þe wind ut an eþelich stiche oþer eche makeþ to understonden hu lutel prude is wurþ hu egede is orhel ondes salve ich seide wes feolahlich luve ant god unnunge ant god wil þer mihte of dede wonteþ swa muchel strengþe haveþ luve ant god wil þet hit makeþ oþres god ure god ase wel as his þet hit wurcheþ sulement luve his god beo wilcweme ant glead þe rof þus þu turnest hit to þe ant makest hit þin ahne sein hit witneþ ȝef þu havest onde of oþres god þu attrest te wiþ healewi ant wundest te wiþ salve þi salve hit is ȝef þu hit luvest aȝein sawle hurtes ant ti strengþe aȝein þe feond is al þe god þet oþer deþ ȝef þu hit wel unnest witerliche ich leve ne schulen flesches fondunges namare þen gasteliche meistrin þe neavere ȝef þu art swote iheortet eadmod ant milde ant luvest se inwardliche alle men ant wummen ant nomeliche ancres þine leove sustren þet tu art sari of hare uvel ant of hare god glead as of þin ahne unnen þet al þe luveþ þe luvede ham ase þe ant dude ham frovre as þe ȝef þu havest cnif oþer claþ oþer mete oþer drunch scrowe oþer cwaer hali monne frovre oþer ei oþer þing þet ham walde freamien unnen þet tu hefdest wonte þeseolf þe rof wiþ þon þet heo hit hefden ȝef eani is þe naveþ nawt þe heorte þus afeitet wiþ sorhfule sikes ba bi dei ant bi niht grede on ure laverd ne neaver griþ ne ȝeove him aþet he þurh his grace habbe hire swuch aturnet salve of wreaþþe ich seide is þolemodnesse þet haveþ þreo steiren heh ant herre ant alre hest ant nest te hehe heovene heh is þe steire ȝef þu þolest for þi gult herre ȝef þu navest gult alre hest ȝef þu þolest for þi goddede nai seiþ sum ameaset þing ȝef ich hefde gult þerto nalde ich neaver meanen art tu þet swa seist ut of þeseolven is þe leovere to beon feolahe þen fere ba weren ahonget ah for his gult wiþute gult for his muchele wes ahon o rode hweþeres fere wult tu beon wiþ hweþer wult tu þolien of þis is þe ruppe iwriten muchel hu he is þi file þe misseiþ oþer misdeþ þe lime is þe frensch of file nis hit or acurset þe iwurþeþ swartre ant ruhre se hit is ifilet mare ant rusteþ þe swiþere þet me hit scureþ hearde gold seolver stel irn al is or gold ant seolver cleansiþ ham of hare dros i þe fur ȝef þu gederest dros þe rin þet is aȝein cunde þe chaliz þe wes þerin imealt ant strongliche iweallet ant seoþþen þurh se moni dunt ant frotunge to godes nep se swiþe feire afeitet walde he ȝef he cuþe speoken awearien his cleansing fur ant his wruhte honden al þis world is godes smiþ to smeoþien his icorene wult tu þet godd nabbe na fur in his smiþþe ne bealies ne homeres fur is scheome ant pine þine bealies beoþ þe þe misseggeþ þine homeres þe þe hearmiþ þench of þis essample hwen dei of riht is iset ne deþ he scheome þe deme þe a þis half þe isette dei brekeþ þe triws ant wrekeþ him o þe oþer on himseolven ant hwa nat þet domesdei nis þe dei iset to don riht alle men hald þe triws þe hwiles hwet woh se me deþ þe þe richtwise deme haveþ iset te dei to loki richt bitwenen ow ne do þu nawt him scheome forhohie wrake of his dom ant neomen to þin ahne twa þinges beoþ þet godd haveþ edhalden to himseolven þet beoþ wurþschipe ant wrake as hali writ witneþ hwase eaver on himseolf takeþ owþer of þeos twa he robbeþ godd ant reaveþ deale art tu se wraþ wiþ mon oþer wiþ wummon þet tu wult forte wreoke þe reavin godd mid strengþe salve is gastelich gleadschipe ant frovre of gleadful hope þurh redunge þurh hali þoht oþer of monnes muþe ofte leove sustren ȝe schulen uri leasse forte reden mare redunge is god bone redunge teacheþ hu ant hwet me bidde ant beode biȝet hit efter amidde þe redunge hwen þe heorte likeþ kimeþ up a devotiun þet is wurþ monie benen forþi seiþ sein hali redunge beo eaver i þine honden slep ga upo þe as þu lokest þe ron ant te hali pagne ikepe þi fallinde neb swa þu schalt reden ȝeornliche ant longe euch þing þah me mei overdon best is eaver mete aȝeines ȝisceunge ich walde þet oþre schuneden as ȝe doþ gederunge to muche freolec cundleþ hire ofte freo iheortet ȝe schule beon ancre of oþer freolec haveþ ibeon oþerhwiles to freo of hireseolven galnesse kimeþ of ȝivernesse ant of flesches eise for as sein seiþ mete ant drunch over riht temeþ þreo teames lihte wordes lihte werkes ant leccheries lustes ure laverd beo iþonket þe haveþ of ȝivernesse ihealet ow mid alle ah galnesse ne biþ neaver allunge cleane acwenct of flesches fondunge ah þet understondeþ wel þet þreo degrez beoþ þe rin as seint witneþ þe forme is cogitatiun þe oþer is affectiun þe þridde is cunsence cogitatiuns beoþ fleonninde þohtes þe ne leasteþ nawt ant teo as sein seiþ ne hurteþ nawt te sawle ah þah ha bispottiþ hire wiþ hare blake speckes swa þet nis ha nawt wurþe þet hire leofmon þet is al feier bicluppe hire ne cusse hire ear ha beo iwesschen swuch fulþe as hit kimeþ lihtliche lihtliche geaþ awei wiþ wiþ wiþ alle goddeden affectiun is hwen þe þoht geaþ inward ant delit kimeþ up ant te lust waxeþ þenne as wes spot ear upo þe hwite hude þer waxeþ wunde ant deopeþ in toward te sawle efter þet te lust geaþ ant te delit þe rin forþre ant forþre þenne is neod to ȝeiȝen a laverd heal me for ich am iwundet þu reade þoht þu blodi delit ne waxe þu neaver cunsense þet is skiles ȝettunge hwen þe delit i þe lust is igan se overforþ þet ter nere nan wiþseggunge ȝef þer were eise to fulle þe dede þis is hwen þe heorte draheþ to hire unlust as þing þe were amainet ant feþ on as to winkin to leote þe feond iwurþen ant leiþ hireseolf duneward buheþ him as he bit ant ȝeieþ cravant cravant ase softe swohninde þenne is he kene þe wes ear curre þenne leapeþ he to þe stod ear feorren to ant bit deaþes bite godes deore spuse iwiss deaþes bite for his teþ beoþ attrie as of a wed dogge daviþ i þe sawter cleopeþ hine dogge forþi mi leove suster sone se þu eaver underȝetest þet tes dogge of helle cume snakerinde wiþ his blodi flehen of stinkinde þohtes ne li þu nawt stille ne ne site nowþer to lokin hwet he wule don ne hu feor he wule gan ne sei þu nawt slepinde ame dogge ga her ut hwet wult tu nu her inne þis tolleþ him inward ah nim anan þe rodesteaf mid nempnunge i þi muþ mid te mearke i þin hond mid þoht i þin heorte ant hat him ut heterliche þe fule curdogge ant liþere to him luþerliche mid te hali rodesteaf stronge bacduntes þet is rung up sture þe hald up ehnen on heh ant honden toward heovene gred efter sucurs ȝef þe ne kimeþ sone help gred luddre wiþ hat heorte ant swa al þe salm over wiþ halsinde bonen o þin ahne ledene smit smeortliche adun þe cneon to þer eorþe ant breid up þe rode steaf ant sweng him o fowr half aȝein helle dogge þet nis nawt elles bute blesce þe al abuten wiþ þe eadi rodetaken spite him amid te beard to hoker ant to scarne þe flikereþ swa wiþ þe ant fikeþ dogge fahenunge hwen he for se liht wurþ for þe licunge of a lust ane hwile stucche chapeþ þi sawle godes deore bune þet he bohte mid his blod ant mid his deorewurþe deaþ o þe deore rode aa bihald hire wurþ þet he paide for hire ant dem þe refter hire pris ant beo on hire þe deorre ne sule þu neaver se eþeliche his ant þin eiþer his deorewurþe spuse þet costnede him se deore makie deofles hore of hire is reowþe over reowþe to unwreast mid alle ha is þe mei wiþ toheoven up hire þreo fingres overcumen hire ant ne luste for slawþe hef forþi wiþ treowe ant hardi bileave up þine þreo fingres ant wiþ þe hali rodesteaf þet him is laþest cuggel lei o þe doggedeovel nempne ofte cleope his passiunes help halse bi his pine bi his deorewurþe blod bi his deaþ o rode flih to his wunden muchel he luvede us þe lette makien swucche þurles in him forte huden us in creop in ham wiþ þi þoht ne beoþ ha al opene ant wiþ his deore wurþe blod biblodge þin heorte ga into þe stan seiþ þe prophete ant hud te i þe dolven eorþe þet is i þe wunden of ure laverdes flesch þe wes as idolven wiþ þe dulle neiles as he i þe sawter longe vore seide þet is ha dulven me baþe þe vet ant te honden ne seide he nawt þurleden for efter þis leattre as ure meistres seggeþ swa weren þe neiles dulle þet ha dulven his flesch ant tobreken þe ban mare þen þurleden to pinin him sarre he himseolf cleopeþ þe toward teose wunden mi culvre he seiþ cum hud te i mine limen þurles i þe hole of mi side muche luve he cudde to his leove culvre þet he swuch hudles makede loke nu þet tu þe he cleopeþ culvre habbe culvre cunde þet is wiþute galle ant cum to him baldeliche ant make scheld of his passiun ant sei wiþ þet is þu schalt ȝeove me laverd heorte scheld aȝein þe feond þi swincfule pine þet hit swincful wes he schawde hit witerliche inoh þa he sweatte ase blodes swat dropen þe runnen to þer eorþe me schal halden scheld i feht up abuven heaved oþer aȝein þe breoste nawt ne drahen hit bihinden al riht swa ȝef þu wult þet te rodescheld ant godes stronge passiun falsi þe deofles wepnen ne dragse þu hit nawt efter þe ah hef hit on heh buve þin heorte heaved i þine breoste ehnen hald hit up toȝein þe feond schaw hit him witerliche þe sihþe þe rof ane bringeþ him o fluhte for ba him scheomeþ þerwiþ ant griseþ ut of witte efter þe ilke time þet ure laverd þerwiþ brohte swa to grunde his cointe coverschipe ant his prude strengþe ȝef þu þurh þi ȝemeles werest te earst wacliche ant ȝevest to þe feond inȝong to forþ i þe frumþe swa þet tu ne mahe nawt reculin him aȝeinward for þi muchele unstrengþe ah art ibroht se overforþ þet tu ne maht þis scheld halden o þin heorte ne wrenchen hire þerunder frommard te deofles earowen nim þe aleast forþ sein salve þah ne þearf hit nawt beon se overstrong as his wes þe of þe walewunge rug ant side ant wombe ron al o gureblode ah lanhure ȝef þeseolf hwen þe strongest stont a smeort discepline ant drif as he dude þet swete licunge into smeortunge ȝef þu þus ne dest nawt ah slepinde werest te he wule gan to feor on þe ear þu least wene ant bringe þe of ful þoht into delit of ful lust ant swa he bringeþ þe al over to skiles ȝettunge þet is deadlich sunne wiþuten þe dede ant swa is ec þe delit of þet stinkinde lust wiþute grant of þe werc se longe hit mei leasten þenne hit least to longe hwen þe skile ne fehteþ na lengre þer toȝeines forþi leove suster as ure laverd leareþ totred te neddre heaved þet is þe biginnung of his fondunge eadi is seiþ daviþ þe wiþhalt hire on earst ant tobrekeþ to þe stan þe earste sturunges hwen þe flesch ariseþ hwil þet ha beoþ ȝunge ure laverd is icleopet stan for his treownesse nim ant keche us leofmon anan þe ȝunge foxes he seiþ ure laverd þe strueþ þe winȝardes þet beoþ þe earste procunges þe strueþ ure sawlen þe mot muche tilunge to to beoren winberien þe deovel is beore cunnes ant haveþ asse cunde for he is bihinden strong ant i þe heaved feble swa is beore ant asse þet is i þe frumþe ne ȝef þu him neaver inȝong ah tep him o þe sculle for he is earh as beore þe ron ant hihe him swa þeoneward ant askur him se scheomeliche sone se þu underȝetest him þet him grise wiþ þe stude þet tu wunest inne for he is þinge prudest ant him is scheome laþest alswa leove suster sone se þu eaver felest þet tin heorte wiþ luve falle to eani þing eawt over mete ananrihtes beo war of þe neddre atter ant totred his heaved þe cwene seide ful soþ þe wiþ a strea ontende alle hire wanes þet muchel kimeþ of lutel ant nim nu ȝeme hu hit feareþ þe sperke þe wint up ne bringeþ nawt ananriht þe hus al o leie ah liþ ant kecheþ mare fur ant fostreþ forþ ant waxeþ from leasse to mare aþet al þe hus bleasie forþ ear me least wene ant te deovel blaweþ to from þet hit earst cundleþ ant mutleþ his beali bleas eaver as hit waxeþ understond tis bi þeseolf a sihþe þet tu sist oþer anlepi word þet tu misherest ȝef hit eawt stureþ þe cwench hit wiþ teares weater ant mid blod hwil hit nis bute a sperke ear þen hit waxe ant ontende þe swa þet tu hit ne mahe cwenchen for swa hit timeþ ofte ant hit is riht godes dom þet hwa ne deþ hwen ha mei ne schal ha hwen ha walde moni cunnes fondunge is i þis feorþe dale misliche frovren ant monifalde salven ure laverd ȝeove ow grace þet ha ow moten helpen of alle þe oþre þenne is schrift þe biheveste of hit schal beon þe fifte dale as ich bihet þe ruppe ant neomeþ ȝeme hu euchan dale falleþ into oþer as ich þear seide twa þinges neomeþ ȝeme of schrift i þe biginnunge þe earre of hwuch mihte hit beo þe oþer hwuch hit schule beon þis beoþ nu as twa limen ant eiþer is todealet þe earre o sixe þe oþer o sixtene stucchen nu is þis of þe earre schrift haveþ monie mihtes ah nulle ich of alle seggen bute sixe þreo aȝein þe deovel ant þreo on usseolven schrift schent þen deovel hackeþ of his heaved ant todreaveþ his ferd schrift wescheþ us of alle ure fulþen ȝelt us alle ure luren makeþ us godes children eiþer haveþ hise þreo pruvie we nu alle þe earste þreo beoþ alle ischawde i deden þet is schrift as wes ȝare iseid sloh þet is þe feond of helle turn þe ruppe þer we speken of fuhelene cunde þe beoþ ievenet to ancre ha hackede of his heaved ant seoþþen com ant schawde hit to þe burhpreostes þenne is þe feond ischend hwen me schaweþ alle hise cweadschipes his heaved is ihacket of ant he islein i þe mon sone se he eaver is riht sari for his sunnen ant haveþ schrift on heorte ah he nis nawt þe ȝet ischend hwil his heaved is ihulet as dude on earst ear hit beo i schawet þet is ear þe muþ i schrift do ut þe heaved sunne nawt te sunne ane ah al þe biginnunge þe rof ant te foreridles þe brohten in þe sunne þet is þe deofles heaved þet me schal totreoden anan as ich ear seide þenne fliþ his ferd anan as dude his wiheles ant his wrenches þet he us wiþ asaileþ doþ ham alle o fluhte ant te burh is arud þet ha hefden biset þet is to seggen þe sunfule is delifret hwa stod aȝein him alswa i þet folc þa hit easkede efter deaþ hwa schulde beon hare dug ant leaden ham i ferde ure laverd ham ondswerede schal gan bivoren ow ant ich chulle ower faes lond biteachen in his honden lokiþ nu ful ȝeorne hwet tis beo to seggen spealeþ heale ant schrift as þenne is dead hwen sawle heale is forloren þurh eani deadlich sunne þe sunfule seolf is þe unwihtes lond þe is ure deadliche ah þis lond ure laverd bihat to biteachen i honden forhwon þet he ga bivoren schrift lo is gunfanuner ant bereþ þe banere bivoren al godes ferd þet beoþ gode þeawes schrift reaveþ þe feond his lond þet is þe sunfule mon ant al todriveþ chanaan þe feondes ferd of helle hit dude licomliche ant schrift þet hit bitacneþ deþ gasteliche þet ilke þis beoþ nuþe þreo þing þet schrift deþ o þe deovel þe oþer þreo þing þet hit deþ usseolven þet beoþ þeose herefter schrift wescheþ us of alle ure fulþen for swa hit is iwriten ant þet wes bitacnet þa wesch hire ant despulede hire of widewene schrud þet wes merke of sorhe ant sorhe nis bute of sunne schrift eft al þet god þet we hefden forloren þurh heavedsunne bringeþ al aȝein ant ȝelt al togederes þis wes bitacnet þurh þet schrudde hire mid hali dahne weden ant feahede hire utewiþ as schrift deþ us inwiþ wiþ alle þe feire urnemenz þe blisse bitacniþ ant ure laverd seiþ þurh þet is schrift schal makie þe mon alswuch as he wes bivore þet he sunegede ase cleane ant ase feier ant ase riche of alle god þe limpeþ to sawle þe þridde þing is þet schrift deþ usseolven þe frut of þes oþre twa ant endeþ ham baþe þet is makeþ us godes children þis is bitacnet þerbi þet i biwon of seiþ ase muchel ase sune of riht half þet is schrift alswa as is for ba ha spealieþ an on ebreische ledene þes gasteliche biȝet of his feader þet is ure laverd to beon his rihþondes sune ant bruken buten ende þe eritage of heovene nu we habbeþ iseid of hwuch mihte schrift is hwucch efficaces hit haveþ ant inempnet sixe loki we nu ȝeornliche hwuch schrift schule beon þe beo of swuch strengþe ant forte schawin hit bet deale we nu þis lim o sixtene stucchen schrift schal beo wreiful bitter mid sorhe ihal naket ofte imaket hihful eadmod scheomeful dredful hopeful wis soþ ant willes ahne ant studevest biþoht bivore longe her beoþ nu as þah hit weren sixtene stuchen þe beoþ ifeiet to schrift ant we schulen of euchan sum word sunderliche seggen schrift schal beo wreiful mon schal wreien him i schrift nawt werien him ne seggen ich hit dude þurh oþre ich wes ined þerto þe feond hit makede me don þus eve ant adam wereden ham adam þurh eve ant eve þurh þe neddre þe feond ne mei neden namon to na sunne þah he eggi þerto ah ful wel he let of hwen ei seiþ þet he makede him to sunegin as þah he hefde strengþe þe naveþ nan mid alle bute of usseolven ah me ah to seggen min ahne unwrestlec hit dude ant willes ant waldes ich beah to þe deovel ȝef þu witest ei þing þi sunne bute þe seolven þu ne schrivest te nawt ȝef þu seist þet tin unstrengþe ne mahte nawt elles þu wrenchest þi sunne upo godd þe makede þe swuch þet tu bi þin tale wiþstonde ne mahtest wreie we þenne usseolven for lo hwet seinte seiþ þet is ȝef we wreieþ wel her ant demeþ her usseolven we schule beo cwite of wreiunge ed te muchele dome þear as seint seiþ þeos dredfule wordes o þe an half o domesdei schulen ure swarte sunnen strongliche bicleopien us of ure sawle morþre o þe oþer half stont rihtwisnesse þet na reowþe nis wiþ dredful ant grislich ant grureful to bihalden buven us þe eorre deme for ase softe as he is her ase heard he biþ þer ase milde as he is nu ase sturne þenne lomb her liun þer as þe prophete witneþ þe liun schal greden he seiþ hwa ne mei beon offearet her we cleopieþ him lomb as ofte as we singeþ nu as ich seide schule we seon buven us þe ilke eorre deme þet is ec witnesse ant wat alle ure gultes bineoþen us ȝeoniende þe wide þrote of helle inwiþ usseolven ure ahne conscience þet is ure inwit forculiende hireseolven wiþ þe fur of sunne wiþuten us al þe world leitinde o swart lei up into þe skiwes þe sari sunfule þus biset hu schal him stonde þenne to hwuch of þes fowre mei he him biwenden nis þer buten heren þet hearde word þet wa word þet grisliche word grureful over alle gaþ ȝe aweariede ut of min ehsihþe into þet eche fur þet wes igreiþet to þe feond ant to his engles ȝe forbuhe monne dom þet ich demde mon to þet wes to libben i swinc ant i sar on eorþe ant ȝe schulen nu forþi habben deofles dom bearne wiþ him echeliche i þe fur of helle wiþ þis schulen þe forlorene warpen a swuch ȝur þet heovene ant eorþe mahen ba grimliche agrisen forþi seint leofliche us leareþ þet is þenche mon o domesdei ant deme her him seolven þus o þisse wise skile sitte as domesmon upo þe domseotel cume þe refter forþ his þohtes munegunge wreie him ant bicleopie him of misliche sunnen beal ami þis þu dudest þear ant tis þear ant tis þear ant o þisse wise his inwit beo icnawes þe rof ant beore witnesse soþ hit is soþ hit is þis ant muchele mare cume forþ þe refter fearlac þurh þe deme heast þe heterliche hate tac bind him heteveste for he is deaþes wurþe bind him swa euch lim þet he haveþ wiþ i suneget þet he ne mahe wiþ ham sunegi na mare fearlac haveþ ibunden him hwen he ne dear for fearlac sturie toward sunne ȝet nis nawt þe deme þet is skile ipaiet þah he beo ibunden ant halde him wiþ sunne bute ȝef he abugge þe sunne þet he wrahte ant cleopeþ forþ pine ant sorhe ant hat þet sorhe þersche inwiþ þe heorte wiþ sar bireowsunge swa þet hire suhie ant pini þe flesch utewiþ mid feasten ant wiþ oþre fleschliche sares hwase o þisse wise bivoren þe muchele dom demeþ her himseolven eadi he is ant seli for as þe prophete seiþ nule nawt ure laverd þet a mon for a þing beo twien i demet hit nis nawt i godes curt as i þe schire þeras þe þet nickeþ wel mei beon iborhen ant te ful þe is icnawen bivore godd is oþerweis ȝef þu wreiest te her godd wule werie þe þear ant skerin mid alle ed te nearewe dome forhwon þet tu deme þe as ich itaht habbe schrift schal beo bitter aȝein þet te sunne þuhte sumchearre swete þe spealeþ schrift as ich ofte habbe iseid wes merarihtes dohter ant þet is ec schrift wivede o þamar merariht ant þamar ba ha spealieþ an on ebreische ledene neomeþ nu ȝeorne ȝeme of þe bitacnunge ich hit segge scheortliche bitter sar ant schrift þet an mot cumen of þe oþer as dude of merariht ant ba beon somet ifeiet as ant þamar for nowþer wiþuten oþer nis noht wurþ oþer lutel phares ant ne temiþ ha neavre streonede of þamar phares ant þe gasteliche bitacniþ tweamunge from sunne ant i þe heorte þe refter arisinde grace fowr þinges ȝef mon þencheþ þet heaved sunne dude him mahen makien him to sorhin ant bittrin his heorte lo þis þe forme ȝef a mon hefde ilosed in a time of þe dei his feader ant his moder his sustren ant his breþren ant al his cun ant alle his freond þet he eaver hefde weren astorven ferliche nalde he over alle men sorhful beon ant sari as he eaþe mahte godd wat he mei beon muche deale sorhfulre þet haveþ wiþ deadlich sunne gasteliche islein godd inwiþ his sawle nawt ane forloren þe swete feader of heovene ant seinte his deorewurþe moder oþer hali chirche hwen he of hire naveþ ne leasse ne mare ant te engles of heovene ant alle hali halhen þe weren him ear for freond for breþren ant for sustren as to him ha beoþ deade as onont him is he haveþ islein ham alle ant haveþ þear as ha livieþ aa leaþþe of ham alle as witneþ þet is al þet him luvede ȝeieþ spi him on ant heatieþ him alle ȝet mare his children sone se he sunegede deadliche deiden alle clane þet beoþ his gode werkes þe beoþ forloren alle ȝet upon al þis ilke he is himseolf biwrixlet ant bicumen of godes child þe deofles bearn of helle eatelich to seonne as godd seolf i þe godspel seiþ þenche euch of his estat þet he is oþer wes in ant he mei seon hwervore he ah to siken sare forþi seiþ make bitter man as wif deþ for hire child þe nefde bute him ane ant siþ hit bivoren hire fearliche asteorven nu þe oþer þet ich bihet a mon þe were idemet for a luþer morþre to beo forbearnd al cwic oþer scheomeliche ahonget hu walde his heorte stonden me þu unseli sunful þa þu þurh deadlich sunne murþredest godes spuse þet is þi sawle þa þu were idemet forte beon ahonget o bearninde wearitre i þe eche lei of helle þer þu makedest foreward mid te deovel of þi deaþ ant seidest in wiþ þe forlorene þet is we habbeþ treowþe ipliht deaþ foreward ifeast mid helle for þis is þe feondes chaffere he ȝeove þe sunne ant tu him þi sawle ant ti bodi mid al to weane ant to wontreaþe world abuten ende nu þe þridde scheortliche þench a mon þe hefde al þe world o walde ant hefde for his cweadschipe forloren al on a stunde hu he walde murnin ant sari iwurþen þenne ahest tu to beon hundret siþe sarure þe þurh an heaved sunne forlure þe riche of heovene forlure ure laverd þet is hundret siþen ȝe þusent þusent siþen betere þen is al þe world eorþe ba ant heovene nu ȝet þe feorþe ȝef þe king hefde bitaht his deore sune to his an cniht to lokin ant unþeode leadde forþ þis child in his warde swa þet tet child seolf weorrede upon his feader wiþ þet unþeode nalde þe cniht beo sari ant scheomien ful sare we beoþ alle godes sunen þe kinges of heovene þe haveþ bitaht ure euch an engel i warde sari is he on his wise hwen unþeode leat us forþ hwen we ure gode feader wreaþeþ wiþ sunne beo we sari þet we eaver schulen wreaþen swuch feader ant sweamen swuch wardein þe wit ant wereþ us eaver wiþ þe unseli gastes for elles uvele us stode ah we schuhteþ him awei hwen we doþ deadlich sunne ant heo leapeþ þenne to sone se he us firseþ halde we him neh us wiþ smeal of gode werkes ant us in his warde wat ure euchan to se gentil wardein bereþ to lutel menske ant kunnen him to lutel þonc of his servise þeos ant monie reisuns beoþ hwi mon mei beo bitterliche sari for his sunnen ant wepen ful sare ant wel is him þe swa mei for wop is sawle heale ure laverd deþ toward us as me deþ to uvel deattur nimeþ leasse þen we ahen him ant is þah wel ipaiet we ahen him blod for blod ant ure blod þah aȝein his blod þet he schedde for us were ful unefne change ah wast tu hu me ȝeddeþ me nimeþ ed uvel dettur aten for hweate ant ure laverd nimeþ ed us teares aȝein his blod ant is wilcweme he weop o þe rode o o for oþer monne sunnen ȝef we wepeþ for ure ahne nis na muche wunder wepe we quoþ þe hali mon i þa me hefde longe on him iȝeiet efter sarmun leote we quoþ he teares leste ure ahne teares forseoþen us in helle schrift schal beon ihal þet is iseid al to a mon ut of childhade þe povre widewe hwen ha wule hire hus cleansin ha gedereþ al þe greaste on an heap on alre earst ant schuveþ hit ut þenne þe refter kimeþ eft aȝein ant heapeþ eft togederes þet wes ear ileavet ant schuveþ hit ut efter þe refter o þe smeale dust ȝef hit dusteþ swiþe ha flaskeþ weater ant swopeþ ut efter al þet oþer alswa schal þe schriveþ him efter þe greate schuven ut þe smealre ȝef dust of lihte þohtes windeþ to swiþe up flaski teares on ham ne schulen ha nawt þenne ablende þe heorte ehnen hwase heleþ eawiht he naveþ iseid nawiht forhwon he beo þe skerre ah is ilich þe mon þe haveþ on him monie deadliche wunden ant schaweþ þe leche alle ant let healen buten an þet he deieþ upon as he schulde on alle he is ase men in a schip þe haveþ monie þurles þer þe weater þreasteþ in ant heo dutteþ alle buten an þurh hwam ha druncniþ alle clane me teleþ of þe hali mon þe lei on his deaþ uvel ant wes laþ to seggen a sunne of his childhad ant his abbat bed him allegate seggen ant he ondswerede þet hit nere na neod forþi þet he wes lute child þa he hit wrahte o least þah unneaþe þurh þe abbates ropunge þet he hit seide ant deide þerefter sone efter his deaþ com a niht ant schawde him to his abbat i snawhwite schrudes as þe þet was iborhen ant seide þet sikerliche ȝef he nefde þet ilke þing þet he dude i childhad i schrift utterliche iseid he were idemet bimong þe forlorene alswa of anoþer þet wes for neh fordemet forþi þet he hefde enchearre ined a mon to drinken ant deide þe rof unschriven alswa of þe leafdi forþi þet ha hefde i leanet to a wake a wummon an of hire weden ah hwase haveþ ȝeorne isoht alle þe hurnen of his heorte ne ne con rungi mare ut ȝef þer eawiht edluteþ hit is ich hopie i þe schrift ischuven ut mid tet oþer hwen þer ne liþ na ȝemeles ant he walde fein mare ȝef he cuþe seggen schrift schal beo naket þet is naketliche imaket nawt bisamplet feire ne hendeliche ismaket ah schulen þe wordes beon ischawet efter þe werkes þet is tacne of heatunge þet me tukeþ to wundre þing þet me heateþ swiþe ȝef þu heatest ti sunne hwi spekest tu menskeliche þe rof hwi hudest tu his fulþe spec hit scheome schendfulliche ant tuk hit al to wundre alswa as þu wel wult schende þen schucke sire ha seiþ þe wummon ich habbe ihaved leofmon oþer ich habbe ibeon ha seiþ fol of meseolven þis nis nawt naket schrift biclute þu hit nawt do awei þe totagges unwrih þe ant sei sire godes are ich am a ful stod meare a stinkinde hore ȝef þi a ful nome ant cleope þi sunne fule make hit i schrift steortnaket þet is ne hel þu nawiht of al þet liþ þerabuten þah to fule me mei seggen me ne þearf nawt nempnin þet fule dede bi his ahne fule nome ne þe schendfule limes bi hare ahne nome inoh is to seggen swa þet te hali schriftfeader witerliche understonde hweat tu wulle meanen abute sunne liggeþ six þing þet hit hulieþ o latin circumstances on englisch totagges mahe beon icleopede persone stude time manere tale cause persone þe dude þe sunne oþer wiþ hwam me hit dude unwreo ant segge sire ich am a wummon ant schulde bi rihte beo mare scheomeful to habben ispeken as ich spec oþer idon as ich dude forþi mi sunne is mare þen of a wepmon for hit bicom me wurse ich am an ancre a nunne a wif iweddet a meiden a wummon þet me lefde se wel a wummon þe habbe ear ibeon ibearnd wiþ swuch þing ant ahte þe betere forte beon iwarnet sire hit wes wiþ swuch mon ant nempni þenne munek preost oþer clearc ant of þet ordre a weddet mon a ladles þing a wummon as ich am þis is nu of persone alswa of þe stude sire þus ich pleide oþer spec i chirche eode o ring i chirchȝard biheold hit oþer wreastlunge ant oþre fol gomenes spec þus oþer pleide bivoren worltliche men bivoren recluse in ancrehus ed oþer þurl þen ich schulde neh hali þing ich custe him þer hondlede him i swuch stude oþer meseolven i chirche ich þohte þus biheold him ed te weovede of þe time alswa sire ich wes of swuch ealde þet ich ahte wel to habben wisluker iwite me sire ich hit dude in lenten i feasten dahes in hali dahes hwen oþre weren ed chirche sire ich wes sone overcumen ant is þe sunne mare þen ȝef ich hefde ibeon akeast wiþ strengþe ant feole swenges sire ich wes þe biginnunge hwi swuch þing hefde forþgong þurh þet ich com i swuch stude ant i swuch time ich biþohte me ful wel ear þen ich hit eaver dude hu uvele hit were idon ant dude hit noþeleatere þe manere alswa seggen þet is þe feorþe totagge sire þis sunne ich dude þus ant o þisse wise þus ich leornede hit earst þus ich com earst þe rin þus ich dude hit forþward o þus feole wisen þus fulliche þus scheomeliche þus ich sohte delit hu ich meast mahte paien mi lustes brune ant seggen al þe wise tale is þe fifte totagge hu ofte hit is idon tellen al sire ich habbe þis þus ofte idon iwonet for to speoke þus hercni þullich speche þenchen hwiche þochtes forȝeme þing ant forȝeoten lachyen eoten drinken lasse oþer mare þenne neode askeþ ich habbe ibeon þus ofte wraþ seoþþen ich wes ischriven nest ant for þulli þing ant þus longe hit leste þus ofte iseid les þus ofte þis ant þis ich habbe i don þis to þus feole ant þus feole siþen cause is þe seste totagge cause is hwi þu hit dudest oþer hulpe oþre þerto oþer þurh hwet hit bigon sire ich hit dude for delit for uvel luve for biȝete for fearlac for flatrunge sire ich hit dude for uvel þah þer ne come nan of sire mi lihte ondswere oþer mine lihte lates tulden him earst upo me sire of þis word com oþer of þis dede wreaþþe ant uvele wordes sire þe acheisun is þis hwi þet uvel leasteþ ȝet þus wac wes min heorte euch efter þet he is segge his totagges mon as limpeþ to him wummon þet hire rineþ for her nabbe ich nan iseid bute forte munegin mon oþer wummon of þeo þe to ham falleþ þurh þeo þe beoþ her iseide as on urn þus of þeose six wriheles despoile þi sunne ant make hit naket i þi schrift as leareþ sched ut ase weater þin heorte ȝef eoile schet of a feat ȝet ter wule leaven in sumhwet of þe licur ȝef milc schet þe heow leaveþ ȝef win sched þe smeal leaveþ ah weater geaþ al somet ut alswa sched þin heorte þet is al þet uvel þet is i þin heorte ȝef þu ne dest nawt lo hu grurefulliche godd seolf þreateþ þe þurh naum þe prophete þu naldest nawt unwreo þe to þe preost i schrifte ant ich schal schawin al naket to al folc þi cweadschipe ant to alle kinedomes þine scheome sunnen to þe kinedom of eorþe to þe kinedom of helle to þe kinedom of heovene ant trussin al þi schendfulnesse o þin ahne necke as me deþ o þe þeof þe me leat to demen ant swa wiþ al þe schendlac þu schalt trusse ant al torplin into helle seiþ sein o seiþ sein hwuch schendlac ant hwuch sorhe biþ þer ed te dome hwen alle þe leaves schule beon towarplet ant al þet fulþe schaweþ him ant wringeþ ut þet wursum bivoren al þe wide worlt eorþ ware ant heovenes nawt ane of werkes ah of idelnesses of wordes ant of þohtes þe ne beoþ ibet her as seint witneþ euc tide ant time schal beo þer i rikenet hu hit wes her ispenet hwen alle þe leaves he seiþ sein schulen beo towarplet he biheold hu adam ant eve þa ha hefden i þe frumþe isuneget gedereden leaves ant makeden wriheles of ham to hare schentfule limen þus doþ monie efter ham schrift schal beon ofte imaket forþi is i þe sawter ant ure laverd seolf seiþ to his deciples ga we eft seide he into judee judee spealeþ schrift ant swa we ifindeþ þet he wende ofte ut of galilee into judee galilee spealeþ hweol forte learen us þet we of þe worldes turpelnesse ant of sunne hweol ofte gan to schrifte for þis is þe sacrement efter þe weofdes sacrement ant efter fulluht þet te feond is laþest as he haveþ to hali men himseolf sare his unþonckes ibeon hit icnawen wule a web beon ed enchearre wiþ a weater wel ibleachet a sol claþ wel iweschen þu weschest þine honden in anlepi dei twien oþer þrien ant nult nawt þe sawle spuse þe eaver se ha is hwittre se fulþe is senre upon hire bute ha beo i wesschen nult nawt to godes cluppunge ofte umbe seoveniht wesschen hire eanes hali weater beoden hali þohtes blesceunges cneolunges euch god word euch god werc wesscheþ smeale sunnen þe me ne mei alle seggen ah eaver is schrift þe heaved schrift schal beon on hihþe imaket ȝef sunne timeþ bi niht anan oþer ine marhen ȝef hit timeþ bi dei ear þen me slepe hwa durste slepen hwil his deadliche heolde an itohe sweord upon his heaved þe neappiþ upon helle breord ha torpliþ ofte al in ear ha least wenen hwase is ifallen amid te bearninde fur nis he mare þen amead ȝef he liþ biþencheþ him hwenne he wule arisen a wummon þe haveþ i losed hire nelde oþer a sutere his eal secheþ hit ananriht ant towent euch strea aþet hit beo ifunden ant godd þurh sunne forloren schal liggen unsoht seove dahes fulle nihe þinges beoþ þet ahten hihin to schrift þe pine þet okereþ for sunne is þe deofles feh þet he ȝeveþ to okere ant to gavel of pine ant eaver se mon liþ lengre in his sunne se þe gavel waxeþ of pine i purgatoire oþer her oþer in helle þe oþer þing is þe muchele ant te reowþfule lure þet he leoseþ þet na þing þet he deþ nis gode licwurþe þe þridde is deaþ þet he nat hweþer he schule þet ilke dei ferliche asteorven þe feorþe is secnesse þet he ne mei þenche wel bute ane of his uvel ne speoken as he schulde bute granin for his eche ant grunte mare for his stiche þen for his sunne þe fifte þing is muche scheome þet hit is efter val to liggen se longe ant hure under þe schucke þe seste is þe wunde þet eaver wurseþ on hond ant strengre is to healen þe seoveþe þing is uvel wune þet bitacneþ þe stonc se longe he hefde ilein i þer eorþe o hwam ure laverd weop as þe godspel teleþ ant risede ant mengde himseolven ant ȝeide lude upon him ear he him arearde forte schawin hu strong hit is to arisen of uvel wune þe roteþ in his sunne seinte stonc of fowr dahes hu stinkeþ þe sunfule of fowr ȝer oþer of five o seiþ seint hu earmliche he ariseþ þe under wune of sunne haveþ ilein longe monie hundes seiþ daviþ habbeþ biset me hwen gredi hundes stondeþ bivore þe bord nis hit neod ȝerde as ofte as eani lecheþ toward te ant reaveþ þe of þi mete nult tu as ofte smiten elles ha walden kecchen of þe al þet tu hefdest ant tu alswa þenne nim þe ȝerde of þi tunge ant as ofte as þe dogge of helle kecheþ ei god from þe smit him ananriht mid te ȝerde of þi tunge i schrift ant smit him se luþerliche þet him laþi ant drede to snecchen eft toward te þet dunt of alle duntes is him dunte laþest þe hund þe fret leþer oþer awurieþ ahte me hit beat ananriht þet he understonde forhwi he is ibeaten þenne ne dear he nawt eft do þet ilke beat alswa mid ti tunge i schrift þe hund of helle ananriht ant he wule beon ofdred to do þe eft swuch þucke hwa is se fol þet he seiþ bi þe hund þet fret leþer abid aþet tomarhen ne beat tu him nawt ȝetten ah ananriht beat beat beat ananriht nis þing i þe world þet smeorteþ him sarre þen deþ swuch beatunge se me deoppre wadeþ i þe feondes leiven se me kimeþ up leatere þe eahtuþe þing is þet seint seiþ þet is sunne þet nis sone ibet draheþ anan anoþer ant þet eft þe þridde ant swa euchan cundleþ mare ant wurse cundel þen þe seolve moder þe niheþe reisun is se he ear biginneþ her to don his penitence se he haveþ to beten leasse i pine of purgatoire þis beoþ nu nihe reisuns ant monie ma þer beoþ hwi schrift ah to beon imaket aa on hihþe schrift ah to beon eadmod as þe puplicanes wes nawt as þe phariseus wes þe talde his goddeden ant schawde þet hale forþ þa he schulde habben unwrihen hise wunden forþi he wende unhealet as ure laverd seolf teleþ ut of þe temple eadmodnesse is
