ilich þeose cointe hearloz hare gutefeastre hare flowinde cweise þet ha putteþ eaver forþ ant ȝef hit is eatelich ha schawiþ hit ȝet eateluker i riche monnes ehnen þet ha habben reowþe of ham ant ȝeoven ham god þe reaþere hudeþ hare hale claþ ant doþ on alre uvemest fiterokes al totorene o þis ilke wise eadmodnesse eadmodliche bigileþ ure laverd ant biȝet of his god wiþ seli truandise hudeþ eaver hire god schaweþ forþ hire poverte put forþ hire cancre wepinde ant graninde bivore godes ehnen halseþ meadlesliche on his derve passiun on his deore wurþe blod on his fif wunden on his moder teares o þe ilke tittes þet he seac þe milc þet hine fedde on alle his halhene luve o þe deore druerie þet he haveþ to his deore spuse þet is to cleane sawle oþer to hali chirche on his deaþ o rode for hire to biȝeotene wiþ þus anewil ropunge halseþ efter sum help to þe wrecche meoseise to lechni wiþ þe seke to healen hire cancre ant ure laverd ihalset swa ne mei for reowþe wearnen hire ne sweamen hire wiþ warne nomeliche swa as he is se unimete large þet him nis na þing leovere þen þet he mahe ifinden acheisun forte ȝeovene ah hwase ȝelpeþ of his god as doþ i schrift þeos prude hwet neod is ham to helpe moni haveþ a swuch manere to seggen hire sunnen þet hit is wurþ a dearne ȝelp ant hunteþ efter hereword of mare halinesse schrift ah to beon scheomeful bi þet te folc of israel wende ut þurh þe reade sea þet wes read ant bitter is bitacnet þet we moten þurh rudi scheome þet is i soþ schrift ant þurh bitter penitence passin to heovene god riht is wat þet us scheomie bivore mon þe forȝeten scheome þa we duden þe sunne bivore godes sihþe for al þet is al is naket seiþ seinte ant open to his ehnen wiþ hwam we schulen rikenin alle ure deden scheome is þe measte deal as seint seiþ of ure penitence ant sein seiþ þet na deorewurþe ȝimstan ne deliteþ swa muchel mon to bihalden as deþ godes ehe þe rude of monnes neb þe riht seiþ hise sunnen understond wel þis word schrift is a sacrement ant euch sacrament haveþ an ilicnesse utewiþ of þet hit wurcheþ in wiþ as hit is i fulluht þe wesschunge wiþuten bitacneþ þe wesschunge of sawle wiþinnen alswa i schrift þe cwike rude of þe neb deþ to understonden þet te sawle þe wes bla ant nefde bute dead heow haveþ icaht cwic heow ant is irudet feire schrift schal beo dredful þet tu segge wiþ as ofte as ich am ischriven eaver me þuncheþ me unschriven for eaver is sum forȝeten of þe totagges forþi seiþ seint þet is þe beste mon of al þe world ȝef ure laverd demde him al efter rihtwisnesse ant nawt efter mearci wa schulde him iwurþen ah his mearci toward us weieþ eaver mare þen þe rihte nearewe schrift schal beon hopeful hwase seiþ as he con ant deþ al þet he mei godd ne bit na mare ah hope ant dred schulen aa beon imengt togederes þis forte bitacnin wes i þe alde lahe ihaten þet te twa grindelstanes ne schulde namon twinnin þe neoþere þe liþ stille ant bereþ hevi charge bitacneþ fearlac þe teieþ mon from sunne ant is iheveget her wiþ heard forte beo quite of heardre þe uvere stan bitacneþ hope þe eorneþ ant stureþ hire i gode werkes eaver wiþ trust of muche mede þeos twa namon ne parti from oþer for as sein seiþ dred wiþuten hope makeþ mon untrusten ant hope wiþute dred makeþ over trusten þeos twa unþeawes untrust ant overtrust beoþ þe deofles tristen þer þet wrecche beast seldene edstearteþ triste is þer me sit mid te greahunz forte kepe þe heare oþer tildeþ þe nettes aȝein him toward an of þeos twa is al þet he sleateþ for þer beoþ his greahunz þer beoþ his nettes untrust ant overtrust beoþ of alle sunnen nest te ȝete of helle wiþ dred wiþuten hope þet is wiþ untrust wes schrift ant forhwi ha forferden wiþ hope wiþute dred þet is wiþ overtrust is þe unselies sahe þe seiþ i þe sawter nis nawt godd quoþ ha se grim as ȝe him fore makieþ na he seiþ daviþ ȝeoi he ant seiþ þenne on alre earst he cleopeþ þe overtrusti unbilevet þe unbilevet wiþ hwon gremeþ he godd almihti wiþ þon þet he seiþ nule he nawt se nearowliche demen as ȝe seggeþ ȝeoi siker ah he wule þus þeos twa unþeawes beoþ to grimme robberes ievenet for þe an þet is overtrust reaveþ godd his rihte dom ant his rihtwisnesse þe oþer þet is untrust reaveþ him his milce ant swa ha beoþ umben to fordon godd seolf for godd ne muhte nawt beon wiþuten rihtwisnesse ne wiþuten milce nu þenne hwucche unþeawes beoþ evening to þeose þe wulleþ godd acwellen on hare fule wise ȝef þu art to trusti ant haldest godd to nessche forte wreoke sunne sunne likeþ him bi þin tale ah bihald hu he wrec in his heh engel þe þohte of a prude hu he wrec in adam þe bite of an eappel hu he bisencte sodome ant gommorre were ant wif ant wenchel þe nomecuþe burhes al a muche schire dun into helle grunde þeras is nu þe deade sea þet nawiht cwikes nis inne hu he i noes flod al þe world adrencte bute eahte i þe arche hu he in his ahne folc israel his deorling grimliche awrec him ase ofte as ha gulten daþan ant abyron chore ant his feren þe oþre alswa þe he sloh bi feole þusendes ofte for hare gruchunge ane on oþer half loke ȝef þu havest untrust of his unimete milce hu lihtliche ant hu sone seinte efter þet he hefde forsaken him ant þet for a cwene word wes wiþ him isahtnet hu þe þeof o rode þe hefde aa ilived uvele in a sterþwile hefde ed him milce wiþ a feier speche forþi bitweone þeos twa untrust ant overtrust hope ant dred beon aa ifeiet togederes schrift ȝet schal beo wis ant to wis mon imaket of uncuþe sunnen nawt to ȝunge preostes ȝunge ich segge of wit ne to sotte alde bigin earst ed prude ant sech alle þe bohes þe rof as ha beoþ þe ruppe iwritene hwuch falle to þe þe refter alswa of onde ant ga we swa duneward rawe bi rawe aþet to þe leaste ant drah togedere al þe team under þe moder schrift ah to beo soþ ne lih þu nawt o þeseolf for as seint seiþ þe seiþ leas on himseolf þurh to muchel eadmodnesse he is imaket sunful þah he ear nere sein seiþ þah cunde of god heorte is to beon offearet of sunne þeras nan nis ofte oþer weie swiþre his sunne sumchearre þen he þurfte weien hit to lutel is ase uvel oþer wurse þe middel wei of meosure is eaver guldene drede we us eavre for ofte we weneþ forte don a lutel uvel ant doþ a great sunne ofte wel to donne ant doþ al to cweade segge we eaver þenne wiþ seinte na god in us nis of us ure god is godes ah sunne is of us ant ure ahne godes god hwen ich hit do quoþ he seint swa o summe wise min uvel hit forgneaieþ oþer ich hit do ungleadliche oþer to ear oþer to leate oþer leote wel þe rof þah namon hit nute oþer walde þet ei hit wiste oþer ȝemelesliche do hit oþer to unwisliche to muchel oþer to lutel þus eaver sum uvel mongleþ him wiþ mi god þet godes grace ȝeveþ me þet hit mei lutel likin godd ant mislikin ofte seinte hwen þe hali mon seide þus bi himseolf hu mahe we hit witerliche seggen bi us wrecches schrift ah to beon willes þet is willeliche unfreinet nawt idrahen of þe as þin unþonkes hwil þu const seggen eawt sei al uneasket me ne schal easki nan but for neode ane for of þe easkunge mei uvel fallen bute hit beo þe wisre on oþer half moni mon abit forte schriven him aþet te nede tippe ah ofte him liheþ þe wrench þet he ne mei hwen he wule þe nalde þa he mahte na mare cangschipe nis þen setten godd tearme as þah grace were his as he bere hire in his purs to neomen upo grace þe rin i þe tearme as he himseolf sette nai beal ami nai þe tearme is i godes hond nawt i þi bandun hwen godd beot hit te reach to ba þe honden for wiþdrahe he his hond þu maht þe refter lokin ȝef uvel oþer oþerhwet ned te to schrifte lo hwet seiþ seint servises inedde ne cwemeþ nawt ure laverd þah noþeleatere betere is o þene no nis neaver to leate penitence þet is soþliche imaket he seiþ eft himseolven ah betere is as daviþ seiþ þet is mi flesch is ifluret bicumen al neowe for ich chulle schrive me ant herie godd willes wel seiþ he ifluret to bitacnin wilschrift for þe eorþe al unnet ant te treon alswa openiþ ham ant bringeþ forþ misliche flures eadmodnesse abstinence culvres unlaþnesse ant oþre swucche vertuz beoþ feire i godes ehnen ant swote i godes nease smeallinde flures of ham make his herbearhe inwiþ þeseolven for his delices he seiþ beoþ þer forte wunien schrift ah to beon ahne namon ne schal i schrift wreien bute himseolven ase forþ as he mei þis ich segge forþi þet swuch aventure bitimeþ to sum mon oþer to sum wummon þet ha ne mei nawt fulleliche wreien hireseolven bute ha wreie oþre ah bi nome noþeleatere ne nempni ha nawt þe ilke þah þe schriftfeader wite wel toward hwam hit turne ah a munk oþer a preost nawt wilyam ne water þah þer ne beo nan oþer schrift schal beo studevest to halde þe penitence ant leave þe sunne þet tu segge to þe preost ich habbe studefestliche i þonc ant in heorte þis sunne to forleten ant do þe penitence þe preost ne schal nawt easki þe ȝef þu wult þeonnevorþ forhate þi sunne inoh is þet tu segge þet tu hit havest on heorte treoweliche to donne þurh godes grace ant ȝef þu fallest eft þe rin þet tu wult ananriht arisen þurh godes help ant cumen aȝein to schrifte ga quoþ ure laverd to a sunful wummon ant have wil þet tu nult sungi na mare þus ne easkede he nan oþer sikernesse schrift ah to beon biþoht bivore longe of fif þinges wiþ þi wit gedere þine sunnen of alle þine ealdes of childhad of ȝuheþehad gedere al togederes þe refter gedere þe studen þet tu in wunedest ant þench ȝeorne hwet tu dudest in euch stude sunderliche ant in euch ealde þe refter sech al ut ant trude þine sunnen bi þine fif wittes þe refter bi alle þine limen i hwuch þu havest isuneget meast oþer oftest aleast sunderliche bi dahes ant bi tiden nu ȝe habbeþ alle ihaved as ich understonde þe sixtene stucchen þe ich bihet to dealen ant alle ich habbe tobroken ham ow mine leove sustren as me deþ to children þe mahten wiþ unbroke bread deien on hunger ah me is þet wite ȝe moni crome edfallen secheþ ham ant gederiþ for ha beoþ sawle fode þulli schrift þet haveþ þus þes sixtene stucchen haveþ þe ilke muchele mihten þet ich earst seide þreo aȝein þe deovel þreo on usseolven ant þreo aȝeines þe world deorewurþe over gold or ant ȝimmes of ynde mine leove sustren þis fifte dale þe is of schrift limpeþ to alle men iliche forþi ne wundri ȝe ow nawt þet ich toward ow nomeliche nabbe nawt ispeken i þis dale habbeþ þah to ower bihove þis lutle leaste ende of alle cuþe sunnen as of prude of great oþer of heh heorte of onde of wreaþþe of slawþe of ȝemeles of idel word of untohene þohtes of sum idel herunge of sum fals gleadunge oþer of hevi murnunge of ypocresie of mete of drunch to muchel oþer to lutel of gruchunge of grim chere of silences ibrokene of sitten longe ed þurl of ures mis iseide wiþute ȝeme of heorte oþer in untime of sum fals word of sware of plohe of ischake lahtre of schede cromen oþer ale of leote þinges muhelin rustin oþer rotien claþes unseowet bireinet unwesschen breoke nep oþer disch oþer biseo ȝemelesliche ei þing þet me wiþ feareþ oþer ahte to ȝemen of keorfunge of hurtunge þurh unbisehenesse of alle þe þinges þe beoþ i þis riwle þe beoþ misnumene of alle þulliche þing schrive hire euche wike eanes ed te leaste for nan se lutel nis of þeos þet te deovel naveþ enbrevet on his rolle ah schrift hit schrapeþ of ant makeþ him to leosen muchel of his hwile ah al þet schrift ne schrapeþ of al he wule o domesdei rede ful witerliche forte bicleopie þe wiþ a word ne schal þer wontin nu þenne ich reade ȝeoveþ him to writen þet leaste þet ȝe eaver mahen for na meoster nis him leovere ant hwetse he writ beoþ umben to schrapien hit of cleanliche wiþ na þing ne mahe ȝe matin him betere to euch preost mei ancre schriven hire of swucche utterliche sunnen þe to alle bifalleþ ah ful trusti ha schal beon o þe preostes þet ha allunge schaweþ to hu hire stonde abute flesches temptatiuns ȝef ha is swa ifondet bute i deaþes dute þus þah me þuncheþ þet ha mei seggen sire flesches fondunge þet ich habbe oþer habbe ihaved geaþ to vorþ upo me þurh mi þeafunge ich am ofdred leste ich ga drivinde oþerhwiles to swiþe forþward mine fol þohtes ant fule umbestunde as þah ich huntede efter licunge ich mihte þurh godes strengþe schaken ham ofte of me ȝef ich were cwicliche ant stealewurþliche umben ich am offearet sare þet te delit i þe þoht leaste to longe ofte swa þet hit cume neh skiles ȝettunge ne dear ich þet ha deopluker ne witerluker schrive hire to ȝung preost herabuten ant ȝet of þis inohreaþe him walde þunche wunder ah to hire ahne schriftfeader oþer to sum lifhali mon ȝef ha mei him habben culle al þe pot ut þer speowe ut al þet wunder þer wiþ fule wordes þet fulþe efter þet hit is tuki al to wundre swa þet ha drede þet ha hurte his earen þet hercneþ hire sunnen ȝef ei ancre nat nawt of þulliche þinges þonki ȝeorne ant halde hire i drede þe deovel nis nawt dead þet wite ha þah he slepe lihte gultes beteþ þus anan bi owseolven ant þah seggeþ ham i schrift hwen ȝe þencheþ ham on as ȝe speokeþ mid preoste for þe leaste of alle sone se ȝe underȝeoteþ hit falleþ bivoren ower weoved o cros to þer eorþe ant seggeþ ich gulte mearci laverd þe preost ne þearf for na gult bute hit beo þe greattre leggen oþer schrift on ow þen þet lif þet ȝe leadeþ efter þeos riwle ah efter þe absolutiun he schal þus seggen al þet god þet tu eaver dest ant al þet uvel þet tu eaver þolest for þe luve of inwiþ þine ancrewahes al ich engoini þe al ich legge upo þe i remissiun of þeose ant forȝevenesse of alle þine sunnen ant þenne sum lutles ihweat he mei leggen upon ow as a salm oþer twa tene oþer tweolve disceplines echi to ȝef him swa þuncheþ efter þe totagges þe beoþ iwriten þe ruppe he schal þe sunne demen mare oþer leasse a sunne ful forȝevelich mei wurþe ful deadlich þurh sum uvel totagge þe liþ þerbisiden efter schrift falleþ to speoken of penitence þet is deadbote ant swa we habbeþ inȝong ut of þis fifte dale into þe seste al is penitence ant strong penitence þet ȝe eaver dreheþ mine leove sustren al þet ȝe eaver doþ of god al þet ȝe þolieþ is ow martirdom i se derf ordre for ȝe beoþ niht ant dei upo godes rode bliþe mahe ȝe beon þe rof for as seinte seiþ as ȝe scottiþ wiþ him of his pine on eorþe ȝe schule scotti wiþ him of his blisse in heovene forþi seiþ seinte ant hali chirche singeþ al ure blisse mot beon i rode þis word nomeliche limpeþ to recluses hwas blisse ah to beon allunge i godes rode ich chulle biginnen herre ant lihten swa herto neomeþ nu gode ȝeme for al meast is sein sentence þreo manere men of godes icorene livieþ on eorþe þe ane mahe beon to gode pilegrimes ievenet þe oþre to deade þe þridde to ihongede wiþ hare gode wil o rode þe forme beoþ gode þe oþre beoþ betere þe þridde best of alle to þe forme gredeþ seinte inwardliche ich halsi ow he seiþ as elþeodie ant pilegrimes þet ȝe wiþhalden ow from fleschliche lustes þe weorriþ aȝein þe sawle þe gode pilegrim halt eaver his rihte wei forþward þah he seo oþer here idele gomenes ant wundres bi þe weie he ne edstont nawt as foles doþ ah halt forþ his rute ant hiheþ toward his giste he ne bereþ na gersum bute his speonse gnedeliche ne claþes bute ane þeo þet him to neodeþ þis beoþ hali men þe þah ha beon i þe world ha beoþ þe rin as pilegrimes ant gaþ wiþ god liflade toward te riche of heovene ant seggeþ wiþ þe apostle þet is nabbe we na wununge her ah we secheþ oþer beoþ bi þe leaste þet ha mahen ne ne haldeþ na tale of na worltlich frovre þah ha beon i worltlich wei as ich seide of pilegrim ah habbeþ hare heorte eaver toward heovene ant ahen wel to habben for oþer pilegrimes gaþ i muche swinc to sechen ane sontes banes as sein oþer sein giles ah þeo pilegrimes þe gaþ toward heovene ha gaþ to beon isontet ant to finden godd seolf ant alle his hali halhen liviende i blisse ant schulen livien wiþ him i wunne buten ende ha ifindeþ iwis sein in þe weifearinde men ȝeornliche bisecheþ nu beoþ þeose gode ah ȝet beoþ þe oþre betere for allegate pilegrimes as ich ear seide al gan ha eaver forþward ne bicumen burhmen i þe worldes burh ham þuncheþ sumchearre god of þet ha seoþ bi weie ant edstuteþ sum deal þah ha ne don mid alle ant moni þing ham falleþ to hwerþurh ha beoþ i lette swa þet mare hearm is sum kimeþ leate ham sum neaver mare hwa is þenne skerre ant mare ut of þe world þen pilegrimes þet is to seggen þen þeo men þe habbeþ worltlich þing ant ne luvieþ hit nawt ah ȝeoveþ hit as hit kimeþ ham ant gaþ untrusset lihte as pilegrimes doþ toward heovene hwa beoþ betere þene þeos godd wat þeo beoþ betere þe þe apostle spekeþ to ant seiþ in his epistle ȝe beoþ deade ant ower lif is ihud mid hwen he þet is ower lif eadeaweþ ant springeþ as þe dahunge efter nihtes þeosternesse ant ȝe schulen wiþ him springen schenre þen þe sunne into eche blisse þe nu beoþ þus deade hare liflade is herre for pilegrim eileþ monihwet þe deade nis noht of þah he ligge unburiet ant rotie buven eorþe preise him laste him do him scheome sei him scheome al him is iliche leof þis is a seli deaþ þet makeþ cwic mon þus oþer cwic wummon ut of þe worlde ah sikerliche hwase is þus dead in hireseolven godd liveþ in hire heorte for þis is þet te apostle seiþ ich livie nawt ich ah liveþ in me þurh his inwuniende grace ant is as þah he seide worltlich speche worltlich sihþe ant euch worltlich þing ifindeþ me deade ah þet te limpeþ to þet ich seo ant here ant wurche i cwicnesse þus riht is euch religius dead to þe worlde ant cwic þah to þis is an heh steire ah ȝet is þah an herre ant hwa stod eaver þe rin godd wat þe þe seide þis is þet ich seide þe ruppe me schilde forte habben eani blisse i þis world bute i rode mi laverd þurh hwam þe world is me unwurþ ant ich am unwurþ hire as weari þe is ahonget a laverd hehe stod he þe spec o þisse wise ant þis is ancre steire þet ha þus segge i na þing ne blissi ich me bute i godes rode þet ich þolie nu wa ant am itald unwurþ as godd wes o rode lokiþ leove sustren hu þis steire is herre þen eani beo of þe oþre þe pilegrim i þe worldes wei þah he ga forþward toward te ham of heovene he siþ ant hereþ unnet ant spekeþ umbehwile wreaþeþ him for weohes ant moni þing mei letten him of his jurnee þe deade nis na mare of scheome þen of menske of heard þen of nesche for he ne feleþ nowþer ant forþi ne ofearneþ he nowþer wa ne wunne ah þe þe is o rode ant haveþ blisse þe rof he wendeþ scheome to menske ant wa into wunne ant ofearneþ forþi hure over hure þis beoþ þeo þe neaver ne beoþ gleade iheortet bute hwen ha þolieþ sum wa oþer sum scheome wiþ on his rode for þis is þe selhþe on eorþe hwase mei for godes luve habben scheome ant teone þus lo rihte ancres ne beoþ nawt ane pilegrimes ne ȝet nawt ane deade ah beoþ of þeos þridde for al hare blisse is forte beon ahonget sariliche ant scheomeliche wiþ on his rode þeos mahe bliþe wiþ hali chirche singen þet is as ich seide ear hwetse beo of oþre þe habbeþ hare blisse summe i flesches licunge summe i worldes dweole summe in oþres uvel we mote nede blissin us i rode þet is i scheome ant i wa þet he droh o rode moni walde summes weis þolien flesches heardschipe ah beon itald unwurþ ne scheome ne mahte he þolien ah he nis bute halflunge upo godes rode ȝef he nis igreiþet to þolien ham baþe vilte ant asprete þeos twa scheome ant pine as sein seiþ beoþ þe twa leaddresteolen þe beoþ up iriht to heovene ant bitweone þeose steolen beoþ of alle gode þeawes þe tindes ifestnet bi hwucche me climbeþ to þe blisse of heovene forþi þet daviþ hefde þe twa steolen of þis leaddre þah he king were he clomb uppard ant seide baldeliche to ure laverd bihald quoþ he ant sih min eadmodnesse ant mi swinc ant forȝef me mine sunnen alle togederes notiþ wel þes twa word þe daviþ feieþ somet swinc ant eadmodnesse swinc i pine ant i wa i sar ant i sorhe eadmodnesse aȝein woh of scheome þet mon dreheþ þe is itald unwurþ ba þeos bihald in me quoþ daviþ godes deorling ich habbe þeos twa leaddresteolen leaf quoþ he bihinde me ant warp awei from me alle mine gultes þet ich ilihtet of hare hevinesse lihtliche stihe up to heovene bi þeos leaddre þeose twa þinges þet is wa ant scheome ifeiet togederes beoþ helyes hweoles þe weren furene hit teleþ ant beren him up to parais þer he liveþ ȝetten fur is hat ant read i þe heate is understonden euch wa þet eileþ flesch scheome bi þe reade ah wel mei duhen ha beoþ her hweolinde ase hweoles overturneþ sone ne leasteþ nane hwile þis ilke is ec bitacnet bi cherubines sweord bivore paraise ȝeten þe wes of lei ant hweolinde ant turninde abuten ne kimeþ nan into parais bute þurh þis leitinde sweord þe wes hat ant read ant in helyes furene hweoles þet is þurh sar ant þurh scheome þe overturneþ tidliche ant agaþ sone ant nes godes rode wiþ his deorewurþe blod irudet ant ireadet forte schawin on himseolf þet pine ant sorhe ant sar schulden wiþ scheome beon iheowet nis hit iwriten bi him þet is he wes buhsum his feader nawt ane to deaþ ah to deaþ o rode þurh þet he seide earst deaþ is pine understonden þurh þet he þe refter seiþ deaþ o þe rode is schendlac bitacnet for swuch wes godes deaþ o þe deore rode pinful ant schentful over alle oþre hwase eaver deieþ ine godd ant o godes rode þeos twa ha mot þolien scheome for him ant pine scheome ich cleopie eaver her beon itald unwurþ ant beggin as an hearlot ȝef neod is hire liveneþ ant beon oþres beodesmon as ȝe beoþ leove sustren ant þolieþ ofte danger of swuch oþerhwile þe mahte beon ower þreal þis is þet eadi scheome þet ich of talie pine ne trukeþ ow nawt i þeos ilke twa þing þet al penitence is in blissiþ ow ant gleadieþ for aȝein þeos twa ow beoþ twafald blissen iȝarket aȝein scheome menske aȝein pine delit ant reste buten ende ha schulen seiþ in hare ahne lond wealden twavald blisse aȝein twavald wa þet ha her dreheþ in hare ahne lond seiþ for alswa as þe uvele nabbeþ na lot in heovene ne þe gode nabbeþ na lot in eorþe in hare ahne lond ha schulen wealden blisse twafald cunne mede aȝein twavald sorhe as þah he seide ne þunche ham na feorlich þah ha her þolien as in uncuþ lond ant in uncuþ eard bituhhen unþeode scheome ba ant sorhe for swa deþ moni gentil mon þe is uncuþ in uncuþþe me mot ute swinken ed hame me schal resten ant nis he a cang cniht þe secheþ reste i þe feht ant eise i þe place al þis lif is a feht as witneþ ah efter þis feht her ȝef we wel fehteþ menske ant reste abit us ed hame in ure ahne lond þet is heoveriche lokiþ nu hu witerliche ure laverd seolf hit witneþ hwen ich sitte forte demen seiþ ure laverd ȝe schulen sitten wiþ me ant deme wiþ me al þe world þet schal beon idemet kinges ant keisers cnihtes ant clearkes i þe sete is reste ant eise bitacnet aȝein þe swinc þet her is i þe menske of þe dom þet ha schulen demen is hehschipe menskeful over alle understonden aȝein scheome ant lahschipe þet ha her for godes luve mildeliche þoleden nis þer nu þenne bute þolien gleadliche for bi godd seolf is iwriten þet is þurh schentful pine he com to gloire of blisful ariste nis na selcuþ þenne ȝef we wrecche sunfule þolien her pine ȝef we wulleþ o domesdei blisfule arisen ant þet we mahen þurh his grace ȝef we usseolf wulleþ seinte sahe þe seiþ se wel eaver ȝef we beoþ to þe i licnesse of godes deaþ we schulen of his ariste þet is to seggen ȝef we libbeþ i scheome ant i pine for his luve i hwucche twa he deide we schulen beon iliche his blisful ariste ure bodi briht as his is world buten ende as seinte witneþ let oþre acemin hare bodi þe eorneþ bivorenhond abide we ure healent þe schal acemin ure efter his ahne ȝef we þolieþ wiþ him we schule blissin wiþ him nis þis god foreward wat nis he nawt god feolahe ne treowe þe nule scottin i þe lure as eft i þe biȝete godd schedde his blod for alle ah heom ane hit is wurþ þe fleoþ flesches licunge ant piniþ hamseolven ant is þet eani wunder nis godd ure heaved ant we his limen alle ah nis euch lim sar wiþ sorhe of þe heaved his lim þenne nis he nawt þe naveþ eche under se sar akinde heaved hwen þe heaved sweat wel þet lim þe ne swet nawt nis hit uvel tacne he þe is ure heaved sweatte blodes swat for ure secnesse to turnen us of þet londuvel þet alle londes leien on ant liggeþ ȝette monie þe lim þe ne sweat nawt i swincful pine for his luve deuleset hit leaveþ in his secnesse ant nis þer bute forkeorven hit þah hit þunche sar godd for betere is finger offe þen he ake eaver cwemeþ he nu wel godd þe þus bilimeþ him of himseolf þurh þet he nule sweaten seinte mearci hit moste swa beon hit seiþ þolie pine ant passiun ant swa habben inȝong into his riche lo deale hwet he seiþ swa habben inȝong into his riche swa ant nan oþerweis ant we wrecches sunfule wulleþ wiþ eise stihen to heovene þet is se hehe buven us ant se swiþe muchel wurþ ant me ne mei nawt wiþuten swinc a lutel cote arearen ne twa þwongede scheos habbe wiþute bune oþer þeo beoþ canges þe weneþ wiþ liht leapes buggen eche blisse oþer þe hali halhen þe bohten hit se deore nes seinte ant seinte þerevore istraht o rode sein o þe gridil ant laþlese meidnes þe tittes itoren of tohwiþeret o hweoles heafdes bicorven ah ure sotschipe is sutel ant heo weren ilich þeose ȝape children þe habbeþ riche feaderes þe willes ant waldes toteoreþ hare claþes forte habbe neowe ure alde curtel is þe flesch þet we of adam ure alde feader habbeþ þe neowe we schulen undervon of godd ure riche feader i þe ariste of domesdei hwen ure flesch schal blikien schenre þen þe sunne ȝef hit is totoren her wiþ wontreaþe ant wiþ weane of þeo þe hare curtles toteoreþ o þisse wise seiþ a folc tolaimet ant totoren a folc he seiþ fearlich schal makien to ure laverd present of himseolven folc tolaimet ant totoren wiþ strong liflade ant wiþ heard he cleopeþ folc fearlich for þe feond is of swucche offruht ant offearet forþi þet wes þullich he meande him ant seide þet is he wulle ȝeoven fel for fel þe alde for þe neowe as þah he seide ne geineþ me nawt to asailin him he is of þet totore folc he tereþ his alde curtel ant torendeþ þe alde pilche of his deadliche fel for þe fel is undeadlich þet i þe neowe ariste schal schine seovevald brihtre þen þe sunne eise ant flesches este beoþ þes deofles mearken hwen he siþ þeos mearken i mon oþer i wummon he wat þe castel is his ant geaþ baldeliche in þer he siþ iriht up swucche baneres as me deþ i castel i þet totore folc he misseþ his merken ant siþ in ham iriht up godes banere þet is heardschipe of lif ant haveþ muche dred þe rof as witneþ me leove sire seiþ sum ant is hit nu wisdom to don se wa himseolven ant tu ȝeld me ondswere of tweie men hweþer is wisre ha beoþ ba seke þe an forgeaþ al þet he luveþ of metes ant of drunches ant drinkeþ bitter sabraz forte acovrin heale þe oþer folheþ al his wil ant forþeþ his lustes aȝein his secnesse ant leoseþ his lif sone hweþer is wisre of þes twa hweþer is betere his ahne freond hweþer luveþ himseolf mare ant hwa nis sec of sunne godd for ure secnesse dronc attri drunch o rode ant we nulleþ nawt bittres biten for us seolven nis þer nawiht þe rof sikerliche his folhere mot wiþ pine of his flesch folhin his pine ne wene nan wiþ este stihen to heovene me sire seiþ sum eft wule godd se wracfulliche wreoken upo sunne ȝe mon for loke nu hu he hit heateþ swiþe hu walde nu þe mon beate þet þing seolf hwerse he hit ifunde þe for muchel heatunge beote þe rof þe schadewe ant al þet hefde þerto eani licnesse godd feader almihti hu beot he bitterliche his deorewurþe sune ure laverd þet neaver nefde sunne bute ane þet he ber flesch ilich ure þet is ful of sunne ant we schulden beon i spearet þe beoreþ on us his sune deaþ þe wepne þet sloh him þet wes ure sunne ant he þe nefde nawt of sunne bute schadewe ane wes i þe ilke schadewe se scheomeliche ituket se sorhfulliche ipinet þet ear hit come þerto for þe þreatunge ane þe rof swa him agras þeraȝein þet he bed his feader are sare quoþ he me grulleþ aȝein mi muchele pine mi feader ȝef hit mei beon speare me ed tis time þi wil þah ant nawt min eaver beo i vorþet his deorewurþe feader forþi ne forber him nawt ah leide on him se luþerliche þet he bigon to greden wiþ reowþfule stevene mi godd mi godd mi deorewurþe feader havest tu al forwarpe me þin anlepi sune þe beatest me se hearde for al þis ne lette he nawt ah beot se swiþe longe ant se swiþe grimliche þet he stearf o rode seiþ þus ure beatunge feol on him for he dude himseolven bitweonen us ant his feader þe þreatte us forte smiten ase moder þet is reowþful deþ hire bitweonen hire child ant te wraþe sturne feader hwen he hit wule beaten þus dude ure laverd ikepte on him deaþes dunt forte schilden us þerwiþ igracet beo his milce hwerse muchel dunt is hit bulteþ aȝein upo þeo þe þer neh stondeþ soþliche hwase is neh him þe i kepte se hevi dunt hit wule bulten on him ne nule he him neaver meanen for þet is þe preove þet he stont neh him ant liht is þe bultunge to þolien for his luve þe underveng se hevi dunt us forte burhen from þe deofles botte i þe pine of helle ȝet seiþ moni mon hweat is godd þe betere þah ich pini me for his luve leove mon ant wummon godd þuncheþ god of ure god ure god is ȝef we doþ þet tet we ahen nim ȝeme of þis essample a mon þe were feor ifearen ant me come ant talde him þet his deore spuse se swiþe murnede efter him þet heo wiþuten him delit nefde i na þing ah were for þoht of his luve leane ant el heowet nalde him betere likin þen þet me seide him þet ha gleowde ant gomnede ant wedde wiþ oþre men ant livede i delices alswa ure laverd þet is þe sawle spus þet siþ al þet ha deþ þah he hehe sitte he is ful wel ipaiet þet ha murneþ efter him ant wule hihin toward hire mucheles þe swiþere wiþ ȝeove of his grace oþer fecchen hire allunge to him to gloire ant to blisse þurh wuniende ne grapi hire nan to softeliche hireseolven to bichearren ne schal ha for hire lif witen hire al cleane ne halden riht hire chastete wiþuten twa þinges as seint þe abbat wrat to his suster þet an is pinsunge i flesch wiþ feasten wiþ wecchen wiþ disceplines wiþ heard werunge heard leohe wiþ uvel wiþ muchele swinkes þe oþer is heorte þeawes devotiun reowfulnesse riht luve eadmodnesse ant vertuz oþre swucche me sire þu ondswerest me suleþ godd his grace nis grace wilȝeove mine leove sustren þah cleannesse of chastete ne beo nawt bune ed godd ah beo ȝeove of grace ungraciuse stondeþ þertoȝeines ant makieþ ham unwurþe to halden se heh þing þe nulleþ swinc þervore bliþeliche þolien bitweonen delices ant eise ant flesches este hwa wes eaver chaste hwa bredde eaver inwiþ hire fur þet ha ne bearnde pot þe walleþ swiþe nule he beon overleden oþer cald weater iwarpe þe rin ant brondes wiþdrahene þe wombepot þe walleþ of metes ant of drunches is se neh nehbur to þet fulitohe lim þet ha dealeþ þerwiþ þe brune of hire heate ah monie mare hearm is beoþ se fleschwise ant swa overswiþe ofdred leste hare heaved ake leste hare licome febli to swiþe ant witeþ swa hare heale þet te gast unstrengeþ ant secleþ i sunne ant þeo þe schulden ane lechnin hare sawle wiþ heorte bireowsunge ant flesches pinsunge forwurþeþ fisitiens ant licomes leche dude swa seinte agace þe ondswerede ant seide to ure laverdes sonde þe brohte salve o godes half to healen hire tittes þet is fleschlich medecine ne dude ich me neavre nabbe ȝe iherd tellen of þe þreo hali men bute þe an wes iwunet for his calde mahe to nutten hate speces ant wes ornre of mete ant of drunch þen þe tweien oþre þe þah ha weren seke ne nomen neaver ȝeme hweat wes hal hwet unhal to eoten ne to drinken ah nomen eaver forþriht hwetse godd ham sende ne makeden neaver strengþe of gingivre ne of zedual ne of clowes de gilofre a dei as ha þreo weren ifolen o slepe ant lei bitweone þes twa þe þridde þet ich seide com þe cwen of heovene ant twa meidnes wiþ hire þe an as þah hit were ber a letuaire þe oþer of gold a sticcke ure leafdi wiþ þe sticke nom ant dude i þe anes muþ of þe letuaire ant te meidnes eoden forþre to þe midleste nai quoþ ure leafdi he is his ahne leche ga over to þe þridde stod an hali mon of feor biheold al þis ilke hwen sec mon haveþ ed hond þing þet wule don him god he hit mei wel notien ah beon þe refter se ancreful nomeliche religius nis nawt godd icweme godd ant his desciples speken of sawle lechecreft ypocras ant galien of licomes heale þe an þe wes best i learet of lechecreft seiþ flesches wisdom is deaþ to þe sawle as seiþ swa we dredeþ flesches uvel ofte ear þen hit cume þet sawle uvel kimeþ up ant we þolieþ sawle uvel forte edstearten flesches uvel as þah hit were betere to þolien galnesses brune þen heavedeche oþer grucchunge of a mistohe wombe ant hweþer is betere i secnesse to beo godes freo child þen i flesches heale to beo þreal under sunne ant þis ne segge ich nawt swa þet wisdom ant meosure ne beon overal iloket þe moder is ant nurrice of alle gode þeawes ah we cleopieþ ofte wisdom þet nis nan for soþ wisdom is don eaver sawle heale bivore flesches heale ant hwen he ne mei nawt ba somet halden cheose ear licomes hurt þen þurh to strong fondunge sawle þrowunge brohte to smirien ure laverd an hundret weies hit seiþ of mirre ant of aloes þet beoþ bittre speces ant bitacniþ bittre swinkes ant flesches pinsunges hundret is ful tale ant noteþ perfectiun þet is ful dede forte schawin þet me schal ful do flesches pine ase forþ as eaver evene mei þolien i þe weie is bitacnet meosure ant wis dom þet euch mon wiþ wisdom weie hwet he mahe don ne beo nawt se over swiþe i gast þet he forȝeme þe bodi ne eft se tendre of his flesch þet hit i wurþe untohen ant makie þe gast þeowe nu is al þis meast iseid of bitternesse utewiþ of bitternesse inwiþ segge we nu sumhweat for of þes twa bitternesses awakeneþ swetnesse her ȝet i þis world nawt ane in heovene as ich seide riht nu þet brohte smirles to ure laverd alswa þe þreo bohten deorewurþe aromaz his bodi forte smirien neomeþ nu gode ȝeme mine leove sustren þeos þreo bitacniþ þreo bitternesses for þis nome as meraht ant merariht þet ich spec þe ruppe of spealeþ bitternesse þe earste bitternesse is i sunne bireowsunge ant i deadbote hwen þe sunfule is iturnd earst to ure laverd ant þeos is understonden bi þe earste ant bi god rihte for ha wiþ muche bireowsunge ant bitternesse of heorte leafde hire sunnen ant turnde to ure laverd ah forþi þet sum mahte þurh to muche bitternesse fallen into unhope þe spealeþ tures hehnesse is to ifeiet þurh hwet is bitacnet hope of heh mearci ant of heovene blisse þe oþer bitternesse is i wreastlunge ant i wragelunge aȝeines fondunges ant þeos is bitacnet bi þe oþer for spealeþ wreastlere þis wreastlunge is ful bitter to monie þe beoþ ful forþ i þe wei toward heovene for þeo ȝet i fondunges þet beoþ þe deofles swenges waggiþ oþerhwiles ant moten wreastlin aȝein wiþ strong wraglunge for as seint seiþ hwil eaver israeles folc wes in egypte under pharones hond ne leadde he neaver ferd þe ron ah þa hit fleah from him þa wiþ al his strengþe wende he þe refter forþi is eaver bitter feht neod aȝein pharaon þet is aȝein þe deovel for ase seiþ flih sunne ant sunne wule folhin eaver efter inoh is iseid þe ruppe hwi þe gode nis neaver sker of alle fondunges sone se he haveþ þe an overcumen ikepe anan anoþer þe þridde bitternesse is i longunge toward heovene ant i þe ennu of þis world hwen ei is se hehe þet he haveþ heorte reste onont unþeawes weorre ant is as in heovene ȝeten ant þuncheþ bitter alle worltliche þinges ant tis þridde bitternesse is understonden bi þe þridde for spealeþ pes ant þeo ȝet þe habbeþ pes ant reste of cleane inwit habbeþ in hare heorte bitternesse of þis lif þet edhalt ham from blisse þet ham longeþ to from godd þet ha luvieþ þus lo in euch stat rixleþ bitternesse earst i þe biginnunge hwen me sahtneþ wiþ godd i þe forþȝong of god lif ant i þe leaste ende hwa is þenne o godes half þe wilneþ i þis world eise oþer este ah neomeþ nu ȝeme mine leove sustren hu efter bitternesse kimeþ swetnesse bitternesse buþ hit for as þet godspel teleþ þeose þreo bohten swote smeallinde aromaz to smirien ure laverd þurh aromaz þe beoþ swote is understonden swotnesse of devot heorte þeos hit buggeþ þet is þurh bitternesse me kimeþ to swotnesse bi þis nome nim eaver bitternesse þurh bone wes ed te neoces weater iwent to wine þet is to understonden þurh bone of bitternesse þet me dreheþ for godd þe heorte þe wes weattri smechles ne ne felde na savur of godd namare þen i weater schal beon iwent to wine þet is ifinden smech in him swete over alle wines forþi seiþ þe wise þe þolemode þolie bitter ane hwile he schal sone þe refter habben ȝeld of blisse ant anna i seiþ bi ure laverd þet is iblescet beo þu laverd þe makest stille efter storm ant efter wopi weattres ȝeldest bliþe murhþes ȝef þu art ofhungret efter þet swete þu most earst witerliche biten o þe bittre ich chulle ha seiþ godes deore spuse gan to rechleses hul bi þe dun of myrre lo hwuch is þe wei to rechleses swotnesse bi myrre of bitternesse ant eft i þet ilke luveboc aromaz me makeþ of myrre ant of rechles ah myrre he set bivoren ant rechles kimeþ efter nu meaneþ hire sum þet ha ne mei habben na swotnesse of godd ne swetnesse wiþinnen ne wundri ha hire nawiht ȝef ha nis for ha hit mot buggen wiþ bitternesse wiþuten nawt wiþ euch bitternesse for sum geaþ frommard godd as euch worltlich sar þet nis for sawle heale forþi i þe godspel of þe þreo is iwriten þisses weis þeos hit seiþ þeose biternesses weren cuminde to smirien ure laverd þeo beoþ cuminde to smirien ure laverd þe me þoleþ for his luve þe strecheþ him toward us as þing þet ismired is ant makeþ him nesche ant softe to hondlin ant nes he himseolf reclus i wombe þeos twa þing limpeþ to ancre nearowþe ant bitternesse for wombe is nearow wununge þer ure laverd wes reclus ant tis word as ich ofte habbe i seid spealeþ bitternesse ȝef ȝe þenne i nearow stude þolieþ bitternesse ȝe beoþ his feolahes reclus as he wes i wombe beo ȝe ibunden inwiþ fowr large wahes ant he in a nearow ineilet o rode i stanene þruh bicluset hetefeste wombe ant þis þruh weren his ancrehuses i nowþer nes he worltlich mon ah wes as ut of þe world forte schawin ancren þet ha ne schulen wiþ þe world na þing habben imeane ȝe þu ondswerest me ah he wende ut of ba ȝe went tu alswa of ba þine ancrehuses as he dude wiþute bruche ant leaf ham ba ihale þet schal beon hwen þe gast went ut on ende wiþuten bruche ant wem of his twa huses þet an is þe licome þet oþer is þe uttre hus þet is as þe uttre wah abute þe castel al þet ich habbe iseid of flesches pinsunge nis nawt for ow mine leove sustren þe oþerhwile þolieþ mare þen ich walde ah is for sum þet schal rede þis inohreaþe þe grapeþ hire to softe noþeles ȝunge impen me bigurd wiþ þornes leste beastes freoten ham hwil ha beoþ mearewe ȝe beoþ ȝunge impen iset i godes orchard þornes beoþ þe heardschipes þet ich habbe ispeken of ant ow is neod þet ȝe beon biset wiþ ham abuten þet te beast of helle hwen he snakereþ toward ow forte biten on ow hurte him o þe scharpschipe ant schunche aȝeinwardes wiþ alle þeose heardschipes beoþ gleade ant wel i paiet ȝef lutel word is of ow ȝef ȝe beoþ unwurþe for þorn is scharp ant unwurþ wiþ þeose twa beoþ bigurde ȝe ne ahen nawt to unnen þet uvel word beo of ow scandle is heavedsunne þet is þing swa iseid oþer idon þet me mei rihtliche turnen hit to uvele ant sunegin þe refter þerþurh wiþ misþoht wiþ uvel word on hire on oþre ant sungin ec wiþ dede ah ȝe ahen unnen þet na word ne beo of ow na mare þen of deade ant beon bliþe iheortet ȝef ȝe þolieþ danger of sluri þe cokes cneave þe wescheþ ant wipeþ disches i cuchene þenne beo ȝe dunes ihehet toward heovene for lo hu spekeþ þe leafdi i þet swete luveboc mi leof kimeþ leapinde ha seiþ o þe dunes overleapinde hulles dunes bitacneþ þeo þe leadeþ hechhest lif hulles beoþ þe lachhere nu seiþ ha þet hire leof leapeþ o þe dunes þet is totret ham tofuleþ ham þoleþ þet me totreode ham tuki ham al to wundre schaweþ in ham his ahne troden þet me trudde him in ham ifinde hu he wes totreden as his trode schaweþ þis beoþ þe hehe dunes as munt of muntgiw dunes of armenie þe hulles þe beoþ lahre þeo as þe leafdi seiþ hireseolf he overleapeþ ne trust nawt se wel on ham for hare feblesce ne mahte nawt þolien swuch totreodunge ant he leapeþ over ham forbereþ ham ant forbuheþ aþet ha waxen herre from hulles to dunes his schadewe lanhure overgeaþ ant wriþ ham hwil he leapeþ over ham þat is sum ilicnesse he leiþ on ham of his lif on eorþe as þah hit were his schadewe ah þe dunes undervoþ þe troden of himseolven ant schaweþ in hare lif hwuch his liflade wes hu ant hwer he eode i hwuch vilte i hwuch wa he leadde his lif on eorþe þulliche dunes þe gode spek of ant eadmodliche seide alle wa quoþ he ant alle scheome we þolieþ ah þet is ure selhþe þet we beoren on ure bodi deadlicnesse þet hit suteli in us hwuch wes his lif on eorþe godd hit wat þe þus doþ ha pruvieþ us hare luve toward ure laverd luvest tu me cuþ hit for luve wule schawin him wiþ uttre werkes ne beo neaver þing se heard soþ luve lihteþ hit ant softeþ ant sweteþ hweat þolieþ men ant wummen for fals luve ant for ful luve ant mare walden þolien ant hweat is mare wunder þet siker luve ant treowe ant over alle oþre swete ne mei meistrin us se forþ as deþ þe luve of sunne nawt forþi ich wat swuch þet bereþ ba togederes hevi brunie ant here ibunden hearde wiþ irn middel þeh ant earmes mid brade þicke bondes swa þet tet swat þe rof is passiun to þolien feasteþ wakeþ swinkeþ ant hit wat meaneþ him þet hit ne greveþ him nawt ant bit me ofte teachen him sumhwet wiþ hwet he mahte his licome derven al þet is bitter for ure laverdes luve al him þuncheþ swete deuleset ȝet he wepeþ to me as wivene sarest ant seiþ godd forȝet him forþi þet he ne sent him na muchel secnesse godd hit wat þet makeþ luve for as he seiþ me ofte for na þing þet godd mahte don uvele bi him þah he wiþ þe forlorene wurpe him into helle ne mahte he neaver him þuncheþ luvien him þe leasse ȝef ei mon eani swuch þing ortrowi bi him he is mare mat þen þeof inume wiþ þeofþe ich wat ec swuch wummon þet þoleþ lutel leasse ah nis þer bute þoncki godd i strengþe þet he ȝeveþ ham ant icnawen eadmodliche ure wacnesse luvie we hare god ant swa hit is ure ahne for as sein seiþ of swa muchel strengþe is luve þet hit makeþ oþres god wiþute swinc ure ahne as is iseid þe ruppe nu me þuncheþ we beoþ icumen into þe seoveþe dale þet is al of luve þe makeþ schir heorte seinte witneþ þet alle uttre heardschipes alle flesches pinsunges ant licomliche swinkes al is ase nawt aȝeines luve þe schireþ ant brihteþ þe heorte þet is licomlich bisischipe is to lutel wurþ ah swote ant schir heorte is god to alle þinges þah ich cuþe he seiþ monne ledene ant englene þah ich dude o mi bodi alle pine ant passiun þet bodi mahte þolien þah ich ȝeve povre al þet ich hefde ȝef ich nefde luve þerwiþ to godd ant to alle men in him ant for him al were ispillet for as þe hali abbat seide al þet wa ant al þet heard þet we þolieþ o flesch ant al þet god þet we eaver doþ alle swucche þinges ne beoþ nawt bute as lomen to tilie wiþ þe heorte ȝef þe axe ne kurve ne spitelsteaf ne dulve ne þe sulh ne erede hwa kepte ham to halden alswa as na mon ne luveþ lomen for hamseolf ah deþ for þe þinges þet me wurcheþ wiþ ham alswa na flesches derf nis to luvien bute forþi þet godd te reaþere þider ward loki mid his grace ant makie þe heorte schir ant of briht sihþe þet nan ne mei habben wiþ monglunge of unþeawes ne wiþ eorþlich luve of worltliche þinges for þis mong woreþ swa þe ehnen of þe heorte þet ha ne mei cnawen godd ne gleadien of his sihþe schir heorte as seint seiþ makieþ twa þinges þet tu al þet tu dest do hit oþer for luve ane of godd oþer for oþres god ant for his biheve have in al þet tu dest an of þes twa ententes oþer ba togederes for þe leatere falleþ into þe earre have eaver schir heorte þus ant do al þet tu wult have wori heorte al þe sit uvele forþi mine leove sustren over alle þing beoþ bisie to habben schir heorte hwet is schir heorte ich hit habbe iseid ear þet is þet ȝe na þing ne wilnin ne ne luvien bute godd ane ant te ilke þinges for godd þe helpeþ ow toward him for godd ich segge luvien ham ant nawt for hamseolven as is mete oþer claþ mon oþer wummon þe ȝe beoþ of igodet for ase seiþ seint ant spekeþ þus to ure laverd þet is laverd leasse ha luvieþ þe þe luvieþ eawt bute þe bute ha luvien hit for þe schirnesse of heorte is godes luve ane i þis is al þe strengþe of alle religiuns þe ende of alle ordres luve fulleþ þe lahe seiþ seinte alle godes heastes as sein seiþ beoþ i luve irotet luve ane schal beon ileid i seinte mihales weie þeo þe meast luvieþ schulen beo meast iblisset nawt þeo þe leadeþ heardest lif for luve hit overweieþ luve is heovene stiward for hire muchele freolec for heo ne edhalt na þing ah ȝeveþ al þet ha haveþ ant ec hireseolven elles ne kepte godd nawt of þet hiren were godd haveþ ofgan ure luve on alle cunne wise he haveþ muchel idon us ant mare bihaten muchel ȝeove ofdraheþ luve me al þe world he ȝef us in adam ure alde feader ant al þet is i þe world he weorp under ure fet beastes ant fuheles ear we weren forgulte ant ȝet al þet is as is þe ruppe iseid serveþ þe gode to sawle biheve ȝet te uvele serviþ eorþe sea ant sunne he dude ȝet mare ȝef us nawt ane of his ah dude al himseolven se heh ȝeove nes neaver i ȝeven to se lahe wrecches seiþ seinte luvede swa his leofmon þet he ȝef for hire þe pris of himseolven neomeþ nu gode ȝeme mine leove sustren for hwi me ah him to luvien earst as a mon þe woheþ as a king þet luvede a gentil povre leafdi of feorrene londe he sende his sonden bivoren þet weren þe patriarches ant te prophetes of þe alde testament wiþ leattres isealet on ende he com himseolven ant brohte þe godspel as leattres iopenet ant wrat wiþ his ahne blod saluz to his leofmon luvegretunge forte wohin hire wiþ ant hire luve wealden herto falleþ a tale a wrihe forbisne a leafdi wes mid hire fan biset al abuten hire lond al destruet ant heo al povre inwiþ an eorþene castel a mihti kinges luve wes þah biturnd upon hire swa unimete swiþe þet he for wohlech sende hire his sonden an efter oþer ofte somet monie sende hire beawbelez baþe feole ant feire sucurs of liveneþ help of his hehe hird to halden hire castel heo underfeng al as on unrecheles ant swa wes heard iheortet þet hire luve ne mahte he neaver beo þe neorre hwet wult tu mare he com himseolf on ende schawde hire his feire neb as þe þe wes of alle men feherest to bihalden spec se swiþe swoteliche ant wordes se murie þet ha mahten deade arearen to live wrahte feole wundres ant dude muchele meistries bivoren hire ehsihþe schawde hire his mihte talde hire of his kinedom bead to makien hire cwen of al þet he ahte al þis ne heold nawt nes þis hoker wunder for heo nes neaver wurþe forte beon his þuften ah swa þurh his deboneirte luve hefde overcumen him þet he seide on ende dame þu art i weorret ant þine van beoþ se stronge þet tu ne maht nanesweis wiþute mi sucurs edfleon hare honden þet ha ne don þe to scheome deaþ efter al þi weane ich chulle for þe luve of þe neome þet feht upo me ant arudde þe of ham þe þi deaþ secheþ ich wat þah to soþe þet ich schal bituhen ham neomen deaþes wunde ant ich hit wulle heorteliche forte ofgan þin heorte nu þenne biseche ich þe for þe luve þet ich cuþe þe þet tu luvie me lanhure efter þe ilke dede dead hwen þu naldest lives þes king dude al þus arudde hire of alle hire van ant wes himseolf to wundre ituket ant islein on ende þurh miracle aras þah from deaþe to live nere þeos ilke leafdi of uveles cunnes cunde ȝef ha over alle þing ne luvede him herefter þes king is godes sune þet al o þisse wise wohede ure sawle þe deoflen hefden biset ant he as noble wohere efter monie messagers ant feole goddeden com to pruvien his luve ant schawde þurh cnihtschipe þet he wes luvewurþe as weren sumhwile cnihtes iwunet to donne dude him i turneiment ant hefde for his leoves luve his scheld i feht as kene cniht on euche half iþurlet his scheld þe wreah his goddhead wes his leove licome þet wes ispread o rode brad as scheld buven in his istrahte earmes nearow bineoþen as þe an fot efter mon ies wene set upo þe oþer þet þis scheld naveþ siden is for bitacnunge þet his deciples þe schulden stonden bi him ant habben ibeon his siden fluhen alle from him ant leafden him as fremede as þe godspel seiþ þis scheld is iȝeven us aȝein alle temptatiuns as witneþ nawt ane þis scheld ne schilt us from alle uveles ah deþ ȝet mare cruneþ us in heovene laverd he seiþ daviþ wiþ þe scheld of þi gode wil þu havest us icrunet scheld he seiþ of god wil for willes he þolede al þet he þolede me laverd þu seist hwerto ne mahte he wiþ leasse gref habben arud us ȝeoi iwiss ful lihtliche ah he nalde forhwi forte bineomen us euch bitellunge aȝein him of ure luve þet he se deore bohte me buþ lihtliche þing þet me luveþ lutel he bohte us wiþ his heorte blod deorre pris nes neaver forte ofdrahen of us ure luve toward him þet costnede him se sare i scheld beoþ þreo þinges þe treo ant te leþer ant te litunge alswa wes i þis scheld þe treo of þe rode þet leþer of godes licome þe litunge of þe reade blod þet heowede hire se feire eft þe þridde reisun efter kene cnihtes deaþ me hongeþ hehe i chirche his scheld on his mungunge alswa is þis scheld þet is þe crucifix i chirche iset i swuch stude þer me hit sonest seo forte þenchen þerbi o cnihtschipe þet he dude o rode his leofmon bihalde þe ron hu he bohte hire luve lette þurlin his scheld openin his side to schawin hire his heorte to schawin hire openliche hu inwardliche he luvede hire ant to ofdrahen hire heorte fowr heaved luven me ifind i þis world bitweone gode iferen bitweone mon ant wummon bitweone wif ant hire child bitweone licome ant sawle þe luve þet haveþ to his deore leofmon overgeaþ þeos fowre passeþ ham alle ne teleþ me him god fere þe leiþ his wed i giwerie to acwitin ut his fere godd almihti leide himseolf for us i giwerie ant dude his deorewurþe bodi to acwitin ut his leofmon of giwene honden neaver fere ne dude swuch fordede for his fere muche luve is ofte bitweone mon ant wummon ah þah ha were iweddet him ha mahte iwurþen se unwreast ant swa longe ha mahte forhorin hire wiþ oþre men þet þah ha walde aȝein cumen he ne kepte hire nawt forþi luveþ mare for þah þe sawle his spuse forhori hire wiþ þe feond under heavedsunne feole ȝeres ant dahes his mearci is hire eaver ȝarow hwen ha wule cumen ham ant leten þen deovel al þis he seiþ himseolf þurh ȝet he ȝeiȝeþ al dei þu þet havest se unwreaste idon biturn þe ant cum aȝein welcume schalt tu beo me ȝet he eorneþ hit seiþ aȝein hire ȝeincume ant warpeþ earmes anan abuten hire swire hweat is mare milce ȝet her gleadfulre wunder ne beo neaver his leof forhoret mid se monie deadliche sunnen sone se ha kimeþ to him aȝein he makeþ hire neowe meiden for as seint seiþ swa muchel is bitweonen godes neoleachunge ant monnes to wummon þet monnes neoleachunge makeþ of meiden wif ant godd makeþ of wif meiden gode werkes ant treowe bileave þeose twa þinges beoþ meiþhad i sawle nu of þe þridde luve child þet hefde swuch uvel þet him bihofde beaþ of blod ear hit were ihealet muchel þe moder luvede hit þe walde þis beaþ him makien þis dude ure laverd us þe weren se seke of sunne ant swa isulet þer wiþ þet na þing ne mahte healen us ne cleansin us bute his blod ane for swa he hit walde his luve makeþ us beaþ þe rof iblescet beo he eavre þreo beaþes he greiþede to his deore leofmon forte weschen hire in ham se hwit ant se feier þet ha were wurþe to his cleane cluppunges þe earste beaþ is fulluht þe oþer beoþ teares inre oþer uttre efter þe forme beaþ ȝef ha hire suleþ þe þridde is blod þet halheþ ba þe oþre as sein seiþ i þe apocalipse þet he luveþ us mare þen eani moder hire child he hit seiþ himseolven þurh mei moder he seiþ forȝeoten hire child ant þah heo do ich ne mei þe forȝeoten neaver ant seiþ þe resun efter ich habbe he seiþ depeint te i mine honden swa he dude mid read blod upo þe rode me cnut his gurdel to habben þoht of a þing ah ure laverd for he nalde neaver forȝeoten us dude mearke of þurlunge in ure munegunge i ba twa his honden nu þe feorþe luve þe sawle luveþ þe licome swiþe mid alle ant þet is etscene i þe twinnunge for leove freond beoþ sari hwen ha schulen twinnin ah ure laverd willeliche totweamde his sawle from his bodi forte veien ure baþe togederes world buten ende i þe blisse of heovene þus lo luve toward his deore spuse þet is hali chirche oþer cleane sawle passeþ alle ant overkimeþ þe fowr measte luven þet me ifind on eorþe wiþ al þis luve ȝetten he woheþ hire o þis wise þi luve he seiþ oþer hit is forte ȝeoven allunge oþer hit is to sullen oþer hit is to reavin ant to neomen wiþ strengþe ȝef hit is forte ȝeoven hwer maht tu biteon hit betere þen upo me nam ich þinge feherest nam ich kinge richest nam ich hest icunnet nam ich weolie wisest nam ich monne hendest nam ich þinge freoest for swa me seiþ bi large mon þe ne con nawt edhalden þet he haveþ þe honden as mine beoþ iþurlet nam ich alre þinge swotest ant swetest þus alle þe reisuns hwi me ah to ȝeove luve þu maht ifinden in me nomeliche ȝef þu luvest chaste cleannesse for nan ne mei luvie me bute ha hire halde ah ha is þreovald i widewehad i spushad i meidenhad þe heste ȝef þi luve nis nawt to ȝeovene ah wult þet me bugge hire buggen hire hu oþer wiþ oþer luve oþer wiþ sumhweat elles me suleþ wel luve for luve ant swa me ah to sulle luve ant for na þing elles ȝef þin is swa to sullen ich habbe iboht hire wiþ luve over alle oþre for of þe fowr measte luven ich habbe icud toward te þe measte of ham alle ȝef þu seist þu nult nawt leote þeron se liht chap ah wult ȝette mare nempne hweat hit schule beon sete feor o þi luve þu ne schalt seggen se muchel þet ich nule ȝeove mare wult tu castles kinedomes wult tu wealden al þe world ich chulle do þe betere makie þe wiþ al þis cwen of heoveriche þu schalt teseolf beo seovevald brihtre þen þe sunne nan uvel ne schal nahhi þe na wunne ne schal wonti þe al þi wil schal beon iwraht in heovene ant ec in eorþe ȝe ant ȝet in helle ne schal neaver heorte þenchen hwuch selhþe þet ich nule ȝeoven for þi luve unmeteliche unevenliche unendeliche mare al creasuse weole þe wes kinge richest schene wlite þe as ofte as me evesede him salde his evesunge þe her þet he kearf of for twa hundret sicles of seolver iweiet asaeles swiftschipe þe straf wiþ heortes of urn strengþe þe sloh a þusent of his fan al ed a time ant ane bute fere cesares freolec hereword heale nalde a mon for an of þeos ȝeoven al þet he ahte ant alle somet aȝein mi bodi ne beoþ nawt wurþ a nelde ȝef þu art se swiþe anewil ant swa ut of þi wit þet tu þurh nawt to leosen forsakest swuch biȝete wiþ alles cunnes selhþe lo ich halde her heatel sweord upo þin heaved to dealen lif ant sawle ant bisenchen ham ba into þe fur of helle to beon deofles hore schentfulliche ant sorhfulliche world abuten ende ondswere nu ant were þe ȝef þu const aȝein me oþer ȝette me þi luve þe ich ȝirne se swiþe nawt for min ah for þin ahne muchele biheve lo þus ure laverd woheþ nis ha to heard iheortet þet a þulli wohere ne mei to his luve turnen ȝef ha wel þencheþ þeose þreo þinges hwet he is ant hwet heo is ant hu muchel is þe luve of se heh as he is toward se lah as heo is forþi seiþ þe salmwruhte nis nan þet mahe edlutien þet ha ne mot him luvien þe soþe sunne i þe undertid wes forþi istihen on heh o þe hehe rode forte spreaden overal hate luvegleames þus neodful he wes ant is aþet tes dei to ontenden his luve i his leoves heorte ant seiþ i þe godspel ich com to bringen he seiþ fur into eorþe þet is bearninde luve into eorþlich heorte ant hwet ȝirne ich elles bute þet hit bleasie wlech luve is him laþ as he seiþ þurh sein i þe apocalipse ich walde he seiþ to his leofmon þet tu were i mi luve oþer allunge cald oþer hat mid alle ah forþi þet tu art ase wlech bitweone twa nowþer hat ne cald þu makest me to wleatien ant ich wulle speowe þe ut bute þu wurþe hattre nu ȝe habbeþ iherd mine leove sustren hu ant forhwi godd is swiþe to luvien forte ontenden ow wel gederiþ wude þerto wiþ þe povre wummon of þe burh þe spealeþ ontendunge laverd quoþ ha to helye þe hali prophete lo ich gederi twa treon þeos twa treon bitacniþ þet a treo þet stod upriht ant þet oþer þe eode þwertover o þe deore rode of þeos twa treon ȝe schulen ontende fur of luve inwiþ ower heorte biseoþ ofte towart ham þencheþ ȝef ȝe ne ahen eaþe to luvien þe king of blisse þe tospreat swa his earmes toward ow ant buheþ as to beoden cos duneward his heaved sikerliche ich segge hit ȝef þe soþe helye þet is godd almihti ifint ow þeose twa treon bisiliche gederin he wule gestnin wiþ ow ant monifalden in ow his deorewurþe grace as helie dude hire liveneþ ant gestnede wiþ hire þet he ifond þe twa treon gederin i grickisch fur is imaket of reades monnes blod ant þet ne mei na þing bute migge ant sond ant eisil as me seiþ acwenchen þis grickisch fur is þe luve of ure laverd ant ȝe hit schule makien of reade monnes blod þet is ireadet wiþ his ahne blod o þe deore rode ant wes inread cundeliche alswa as me weneþ þis blod for ow isched upo þe earre twa treon schal makien ow þet is ontende mid tis grickisch fur þet as seiþ nane weattres þet beoþ worldliche tribulatiuns nane temptatiuns nowþer inre ne uttre ne mahen þis luve acwenchen nu nis þenne on ende bute witen ow warliche wiþ al þet hit acwencheþ þet beoþ migge ant sond ant eisil as ich ear seide migge is stench of sunne o sond ne groweþ na god ant bitacneþ idel idel akeldeþ ant acwencheþ þis fur sturieþ ow cwicliche aa i gode werkes ant þet schal heaten ow ant ontenden þis fur aȝein þe brune of sunne for alswa as þe an neil driveþ ut þen oþer alswa þe brune of godes luve driveþ brune of ful luve ut of þe heorte þe þridde þing is eisil þet is sur heorte of niþ oþer of onde understondeþ þis word þa þe niþfule giws offreden ure laverd þis sure present upo þe rode þa seide he þet reowþfule word neaver quoþ he ear nu nes ich ful pinet nawt þurh þet eisil ah þurh hare ondfule niþ þet tet eisil bitacnede þet heo him duden drinken ant is ilich as þah a mon þet hefde longe iswunken ant failede efter long swinc on ende of his hure alswa ure laverd mare þen twa ant þritti ȝer tilede efter hare luve ant for al his sare swinc ne wilnede na þing bute luve to hure ah i þe ende of his lif þet wes as i þe eventid hwen me ȝelt wercmen hare deies hure loke hu ha ȝulden him for piment of huni luve eisil of sur niþ ant galle of bitter onde o quoþ ure laverd þa al mi swinc on eorþe al mi pine o rode ne sweameþ ne ne derveþ me nawiht aȝein þis þet ich þus biteo al þet ich idon habbe þis eisil þet ȝe beodeþ me þis sure hure þurhfulleþ mi pine þis eisil of sur heorte ant of bitter þonc over alle oþre þing acwencheþ grickisch fur þet is þe luve of ure laverd ant hwase hit bereþ i breoste toward wummon oþer mon ha is giwes make ha offreþ godd þis eisil ant þurhfulleþ onont hire pine o rode me warpeþ grickisch fur upon his famen ant swa me overkimeþ ham ȝe schule don alswa hwen godd areareþ ow of ei va eani weorre hu ȝe hit schule warpen teacheþ þet is ȝef þi hungreþ fed him to his þurst ȝef him drunch þet is to understonden ȝef he efter þin hearm haveþ hunger oþer þurst ȝef him fode of þine beoden þet godd do him are ȝef him drunch of teares wep for his sunnen þus þu schalt seiþ rukelin on his heaved bearninde gleden þet is to seggen þus þu schalt ontenden his heorte forte luvie þe for heorte is in hali writ bi heaved understonden o þulli wise wule godd seggen ed te dome hwi luvedest tu þe mon oþer þe wummon sire ha luveden me ȝe he wule seggen þu ȝulde þet tu ahtest her nabbe ich þe nawt muches to ȝelden ȝef þu maht ondswerien alle wa ha duden me ne na luve ne ahte ich ham ah sire ich luvede ham for þi luve þet luve he ah þe for hit wes iȝeven him ant he hit wule þe ȝelden migge as ich seide þet acwencheþ grickisch fur is stinkinde flesches luve þe acwencheþ gastelich luve þet grickisch fur bitacneþ hweat flesch wes on eorþe se swete ant se hali as wes flesch ant þah he seide himseolf to his deore deciples þet is bute ich parti from ow þe hali gast þet is min ant mines feaderes luve ne mei nawt cumen to ow ah hwen ich beo from ow ich chulle senden him ow hwen ahne deciples hwil þet ha fleschliche luveden him neh ham foreoden þe swetnesse of þe hali gast ne ne mahte nawt habben baþe togederes demeþ owseolven nis he wod oþer heo þe luveþ to swiþe hire ahne flesch oþer eani mon fleschliche swa þet ha ȝirne to swiþe his sihþe oþer his speche ne þunche hire neaver wunder ȝef hire wonti þe hali gastes frovre cheose nu euchan of þes twa eorþlich elne ant heovenlich to hweþer ha wule halden for þet oþer ha mot leten for i þe tweire monglunge ne mei ha habben neaver mare schirnesse of heorte þet is as we seiden ear þet god ant te strengþe of alle religiuns ant in euch ordre luve makeþ hire schir griþful ant cleane luve haveþ a meistrie bivoren alle oþre for al þet ha rineþ al ha turneþ to hire ant makeþ al hire ahne deore walde moni mon buggen a swuch þing þet al þet he rine to al were his ahne ant ne seide hit þe ruppe feor ane þurh þet tu luvest þet god þet is in anoþer wiþ þe rinunge of þi luve þu makest wiþuten oþer swinc his god þin ahne god as sein witneþ lokiþ nu hu muchel god þe ontfule leoseþ streche þi luve to þu havest him i wunnen rin him wiþ ase muche luve as þu havest sum mon sumchearre he is þin to don wiþ al þet tu wilnest ah hwa luveþ þing þet leaveþ hit for leasse þen hit is wurþ nis godd betere unevenlich þen al þet is i þe world chearite is cherte of leof þing ant of deore undeore he makeþ godd ant to unwurþ mid alle þet for ei worltlich þing of his luve leaskeþ for na þing ne con luvien riht bute he ane swa overswiþe he luveþ luve þet he makeþ hire his evening ȝet ich dear segge mare he makeþ hire his meistre ant deþ al þet ha hat as þah he moste nede mei ich pruvien þis ȝe witerliche ich bi his ahne wordes for þus he spekeþ to þe monne meast him luvede ich hefde quoþ he imunt to wreoke mine wreaþþe i þis folc ah þu seist i ne schal nawt þi word beo iforþet me seiþ þet luve bindeþ witerliche luve bint swa ure laverd þet he ne mei na þing don bute þurh luves leave nu preove herof for hit þuncheþ wunder laverd þu wult smiten seiþ weilawei þu maht wel nis nan þet te halde as þah he seide ȝef ei luvede þe riht he mahte halden þe ant wearnen þe to smiten þet is þa ure laverd walde bisenchen sodome þer lot his freond wes inne hihe þe quoþ he utward for hwil þu art bimong ham ne mei ich nawt don ham nes þes wiþ luve ibunden hwet wult tu mare luve is his chamberleng his conseiler his spuse þet he ne mei nawt heole wiþ ah teleþ al þet he þencheþ mei ich quoþ ure laverd heolen þing þet ich þenche to donne nai o nane wise nu con þes luvien þe þus spekeþ ant þus deþ to alle þe him inwardliche leveþ ant luvieþ þe blisse þet he ȝarkeþ ham as ha is unevenlich to alle worldes blissen alswa ha is untalelich to worldliche tungen ȝe habbeþ of þeos blissen iwriten elleshwer mine leove sustren þis luve is þe riwle þe riwleþ þe heorte þis is þe leafdi riwle alle þe oþre serviþ hire ant ane for hire sake me hat ham to luvien lutel strengþe ich do of ham forhwon þet þeos beo deorewurþliche ihalden habbeþ ham þah scheortliche i þe eahtuþe dale bivoren on earst ich seide þet ȝe ne schulden nawiht as i vu bihaten for te halden nan of þe uttre riwlen þet ilke ich segge ȝetten ne nane ne write ich ham buten ow ane ich segge þis forþi þet oþre ancren ne seggen nawt þet ich þurh mi meistrie makie ham neowe riwle ne bidde ich nawt þet ha halden ham ah ȝe ȝet moten changin hwense ȝe eaver wulleþ þeose for betere aȝein þinges þe beoþ bivoren of ham is lutel strengþe of sihþe ant of speche ant of þe oþre wittes is inoh iseid nu is þis leaste dale as ich bihet on earst todealet ant isundret o lutle seove stucchen me let leasse of þe þing þet me haveþ ofte forþi ne schule ȝe beon bute as ure breþren beoþ ihuslet inwiþ tweolfmoneþ fiftene siþen i mid winter dei tweofte dei condelmeasse dei a sunnedei midwei bitweonen þet ant easter oþer ure leafdi dei ȝef he is neh þe sunnedei for þe hehnesse easter dei þe þridde sunnedei þe refter hali þursdei viii witsunne dei midsumer dei seinte dei þe assumptiun þe nativite seinte mihales dei alle halhene dei seint dei aȝein alle þeose beoþ cleanliche ischrivene ant neomeþ disceplines neaver þah of namon bute of owseolven ant forgaþ an dei ower pitance ȝef ewt ilimpeþ misliche þet ȝe ne beon nawt ihuslet i þeose sette tearmes beoþ hit þe neste sunnedei oþer ȝef þe oþer terme is neh abideþ aþet tenne ȝe schulen eoten from easter aþet te hali rode dei þe leatere þe is in hervest euche dei twien bute þe fridahes oþer umbridaȝes ȝongdaȝes vigilies i þeose daȝes ne i þe advent ne schule ȝe nawt eoten hwit bute neode hit makie þe oþer half ȝer feasten al bute sunnedahes ane hwen ȝe beoþ in heale ant i ful strengþe ah riwle ne tweast nawt seke ne blodletene ȝe ne schulen nawt eoten flesch ne seim bute for muche secnesse oþer hwa se is overfeble potage eoteþ bliþeliche ant wunieþ ow to lutel drunch no þeles leove sustren ower mete ant ower drunch haveþ iþuht me ofte leasse þen ich walde ne feaste ȝe na dei to bread ne to weattre bute ȝe habben leave sum ancre makeþ hire bord wiþ hire gest utewiþ þet is to muche freondschipe for of alle ordres þenne is hit uncundelukest ant meast aȝein ancre ordre þe is al dead to þe world me haveþ iherd ofte þet deade speken wiþ cwike ah þet ha eten wiþ cwike ne fond ich ȝet neaver ne makie ȝe nane gestnunges ne ne tulle ȝe to þe ȝete nane uncuþe hearloz þah þer nere nw uvel bute hare meadlese nurþ hit walde letten oþerhwile heovenliche þohtes ne limpeþ nawt to ancre of oþer monnes ealmesse to makien hire large nalde me lahhen a beggere lude to bismere þe leaþede men to feaste ant marþe ba weren sustren ah hare lif sundrede ȝe ancren beoþ inumen ow to dale þe ure laverd seolf herede marþe marþe quoþ he þu art in muche baret haveþ icore bet ant ne schal hire na þing reavin hire dale husewifschipe is marþe dale dale is stilnesse ant reste of alle worldes noise þet na þing ne lette hire to heren godes stevene ant lokiþ hwet godd seiþ þet na þing ne schal ow reavin þis dale marþe haveþ hire meoster leoteþ hire iwurþen ȝe sitten wiþ stanstille ed godes fet ant hercniþ him ane marþe meoster is to feden povre ant schruden as husleafdi ne ah nawt to entremeatin þe rof ȝef ei blameþ hire godd seolf ihwer wereþ hire as hali writ witneþ on oþer half nan ancre ne ah to neomen bute meaþfulliche þet hire to neodeþ hwerof þenne mei ha makien hire large ha schal libben bi ealmesse ase meaþfulliche as ha eaver mei ant nawt gederin forte ȝeoven ha nis nawt husewif ah is a chirchancre ȝef ha mei spearien eani povre schraden sende ham al dearnliche ut of hire wanes under semblant of god is ofte ihulet sunne ant hu schulen þeose riche ancres þe tilieþ oþer habbeþ rentes isette don to povre nehburs dearnliche hare ealmesse ne wilni ha nawt to habbe word of a large ancre ne forte ȝeoven muchel ne beo nan þe grediure forte habben mare forhwon þet gredinesse beo rote of þet gederunge of hire bitternesse al beoþ þe bohes bittre þe of hire spruteþ bidden hit forte ȝeoven hit nis nawt ancre rihte of ancre curteisie of ancre largesce is icumen ofte sunne ant scheome on ende wummen ant children ant nomeliche ancre meidnes þe cumeþ iswenchet for ow þah ȝe spearien hit on ow oþer borhin oþer bidden hit makieþ ham to eotene wiþ chearitable chere ant leaþieþ to herbarhin na mon ne eote bivoren ow bute bi ower meistres leave general oþer spetial general as of freres preachurs ant meonurs spetial of alle oþre ne leaþie ȝe nane oþre to eoten ne to drinken bute alswa þurh his leave liht is me seiþ leave nawiht ne ȝirne ich þet me for swucche boden telle ow hende ancren i hwear þah ant eaver ȝemeþ ow þet nan from ow þurh ower untuhtle ne parti wiþ scandle ed gode men neomeþ al þet ow to nedeþ ah þet lokiþ ow wel þet ȝe ne kecchen þe nome of gederinde ancren of mon þet ȝe misleveþ þurh his fol semblant oþer bi his wake wordes nowþer ne neome ȝe ne leasse ne mare neode schal driven ow forte bidden ei þing þah eadmodliche schawiþ to gode men ant wummen ower meoseise ȝe mine leove sustren bute ȝef neod ow drive ant ower meistre hit reade ne schulen habbe na beast bute cat ane ancre þe haveþ ahte þuncheþ bet huse wif ase marþe wes ne lihtliche ne mei ha nawt beo marþe suster wiþ griþfullnesse of heorte for þenne mot ha þenchen of þe kues foddre of heorde monne hure olhnin þe heiward wearien hwen he punt hire ant ȝelden þah þe hearmes ladlich þing is hit wat hwen me makeþ i tune man of ancre ahte nu þenne ȝef eani mot nedlunge habben hit loki þet hit namon ne eili ne ne hearmi ne þet hire þoht ne beo nawiht þe ron ifestnet ancre ne ah to habben na þing þet utward drahe hire heorte na chaffere ne drive ȝe ancre þet is chepilt þet is buþ forte sullen efter biȝete ha chepeþ hire sawle þe chapmon of helle þing þah þet ha wurcheþ ha mei þurh hire meistres read for hire neode sullen hali men sumhwile liveden bi hare honden nawt deore dehtren ne wite ȝe in ower hus of oþer monne þinges ne ahte ne claþes ne boistes ne chartres scoren ne cyrograffes ne þe chirch vestemenz ne þe calices bute neode oþer strengþe hit makie oþer muchel eie of swuch witunge is muchel uvel ilumpen ofte siþen inwiþ ower wanes ne leote ȝe namon slepen ȝef muchel neod mid alle makeþ breoken ower hus hwil hit eaver is ibroken habbeþ þe rinne wiþ ow a wummon of cleane lif deies ant nihtes forþi þet wepmen ne seoþ ow ne ȝe ham wel mei don of ower claþ beo hit hwit beo hit blac bute hit beo unorne warm ant wel iwraht felles wel itawet ant habbeþ ase monie as ow to neodeþ to bedde ant to rugge nest flesch ne schal nan werien linnene claþ bute hit beo of hearde ant of greate heorden stamin habbe hwase wule hwase wule beo buten ȝe schulen in an hetter ant igurd liggen swa leoþeliche þah þet ȝe mahen honden putten þerunder nest lich nan ne gurde hire wiþ na cunne gurdles bute þurh schriftes leave ne beore nan irn ne here ne ilespiles felles ne ne beate hire þerwiþ ne wiþ scurge ileadet wiþ holin ne wiþ breres ne biblodgi hire seolf wiþute schriftes leave nohwer ne binetli hire ne ne beate bivoren ne na keorvunge ne keorve ne ne neome ed eanes to luþere disceplines temptatiuns forte acwenchen ne for na bote aȝein cundeliche secnesses nan uncundelich lechecreft ne leve ȝe ne ne fondin wiþuten ower meistres read leste ow stonde wurse ower schon i winter beon meoke greate ant warme i sumer ȝe habbeþ leave bearvot gan ant sitten ant lihte scheos werien hosen wiþute vampez ligge in hwase likeþ ischeoed ne slepe ȝe nawt ne nohwer bute i bedde sum wummon inohreaþe wereþ þe brech of here ful wel icnottet þe streapeles dun to þe vet ilacet ful feaste ah eaver is best þe swete ant te swote heorte me is leovere þet ȝe þolien wel an heard word þen an heard here ȝef ȝe muhen beo wimpelles ant ȝe wel wullen beoþ bi warme cappen ant þeruppon hwite oþer blake veiles ancren summe sungiþ in hare wimplunge na leasse þen leafdis ah þah seiþ sum þet hit limpeþ to euch wummon cundeliche forte werien wimpel nai wimpel ne heavedclaþ nowþer ne nempneþ hali writ ah wriheles ane wummon seiþ þe apostle schal wreon hire heaved wrihen he seiþ nawt wimplin wrihen ha schal hire scheome as eve sunfule dohter i mungunge of þe sunne þet schende us on earst alle ant nawt drahe þe wriheles to tiffunge ant to prude eft wule þe apostle þet wummon wreo i chirche hire neb ȝetten leste uvel þoht arise þurh hire onsihþe hwi þenne þu chirchancre iwimplet openest þi neb to wepmonnes ehe toȝeines þe þe sist men spekeþ þe apostle ȝef þu þe ne hudest ah ȝef þet ei þing wriheþ þi neb from monnes ehe beo hit wah beo hit claþ i wel itund windowe wel mei duhen ancre of oþer wimplunge toȝeines þe þe þus ne dest spekeþ þe apostle nawt toȝeines oþre þet hare ahne wah wriheþ wiþ euch monnes sihþe þer awakeniþ ofte wake þohtes of ant werkes oþerhwiles hwase wule beon i sehen þah ha atiffi hire nis nawt muche wunder ah to godes ehnen ha is lufsumre þe is for þe luve of him untiffet wiþuten ring ne broche ne habbe ȝe ne gurdel imembret ne gloven ne nan swuch þing þet ow ne deh to habben a meoke surpliz ȝe mahen in hat sumer werien eaver me is leovere se ȝe doþ greattre werkes ne makie ȝe nane purses forte freondin ow wiþ bute to þeo þet ower meistre ȝeveþ ow his leave ne huve ne blodbinde of seolc ne laz buten leave ah schapieþ ant seowiþ ant mendiþ chirche claþes ant povre monne hettren na swuch þing ne schule ȝe ȝeoven wiþuten schriftes leave namare þen neomen þet ȝe ne seggen him fore as of oþre þinges kun oþer cuþþe hu ofte ȝe undervengen hu longe ȝe edheolden tendre of cun ne limpeþ nawt ancre beonne a mon wes of religiun ant com to him efter help his fleschliche broþer ant he tahte him to his þridde breþer þe wes dead biburiet þe ondswerede wundrinde nai quoþ he nis he dead ant ich quoþ þe hali mon am dead gasteliche na fleschlich freond ne easki me fleschlich frovre amites ant parures worldliche leafdis mahen inoh wurchen ant ȝef ȝe ham makieþ ne makie ȝe þe rof na mustreisun veinegloire attreþ alle gode þeawes ant alle gode werkes criblin ne schal nan of ow for luve ne for hure taveles ne forbeode ich nawt ȝef sum riveþ surpliz oþer meassekemese oþre rivunges ne rive ha nawt nomeliche overegede bute for muche neode helpeþ ow wiþ ower ahne swinc se forþ se ȝe eaver mahen to schruden ow seolven ant feden ȝef neod is ant þeo þe ow serviþ as sein leareþ ne beo ȝe neaver longe ne lihtliche of sum þing allunges idel for ananrihtes þe feond beot hire his werc þe i godes werc ne swinkeþ ant tuteleþ anan toward hire for hwil he siþ hire bisi he þencheþ þus for nawt ich schulde nu cume neh hire ne mei ha nawt iȝemen to lustni mi lare of idelnesse awakeneþ muchel flesches fondunge þet is sodomes cwedschipe com of idelnesse ant of ful wombe irn þet liþ stille gedereþ sone rust weater þe ne stureþ nawt readliche stinkeþ ancre ne schal nawt forwurþe scolmeistre ne turnen ancrehus to childrene scole hire meiden mei learen sum oþer meiden þet were pliht of to leornin among wepmen oþer bimong gromes ah ancre ne ah to ȝemen bute godd ane þah bi hire meistres read ha mei sum rihten ant helpen to learen ȝe ne schulen senden leattres ne undervon leattres ne writen bute leave ȝe schulen beon idoddet oþer ȝef ȝe wulleþ ischaven fowr siþen i þe ȝer to lihtin ower heaved beo bi þe her ieveset hwase swa is leovere ant as ofte ileten blod ant ȝef neod is oftre þe mei beo þerbuten ich hit mei wel þolien hwen ȝe beoþ al greiþe ilete blod ȝe ne schule don na þing þe þreo dahes þet ow greveþ ah talkiþ to ower meidnes ant wiþ þeawfule talen schurteþ ow togederes ȝe mahen swa don ofte hwen ow þuncheþ hevie oþer beoþ for sum worltlich þing sare oþer seke þah euch worltlich frovre is unwurþe to ancre swa wisliche witeþ ow in ower blodletunge ant haldeþ ow i swuch reste þet ȝe longe þe refter mahen i godes servise þe monluker swinken ant alswa hwen ȝe feleþ eani secnesse muchel sotschipe hit is leosen for an dei tene oþer tweolve wesscheþ ow hwerse neod is as ofte as ȝe wulleþ ant ower oþre þinges nes neaver fulþe godd leof þah poverte ant unorneschipe beon him licwurþe understondeþ eaver of alle þeose þinges þet nan nis heast ne forbod þet beoþ of þe uttre riwle þet is lute strengþe of forhwon þet te inre beo wel i wist as ich seide i þe frumþe þeos mei beon ichanget hwerse eani neod oþer eani skile hit easkeþ efter þet ha best mei þe leafdi riwle servin as hire eadmode þuften ah sikerliche wiþuten hire þe leafdi feareþ to wundre ancre þe naveþ nawt neh honde hire fode beoþ bisie twa wummen an eaver þe leave ed hame an oþer þe wende ut hwenne driveþ neod ant þeo beo ful unorne wiþuten euch tiffunge oþer a lutel þuftene oþer of feier ealde bi þe wei as ha geaþ ga singinde hire beoden ne ne halde na tale wiþ mon ne wiþ wummon ne sitte ne ne stonde bute þet leaste þet ha eaver mei ear þen ha ham cume nohwider elles ne ga heo bute þider as me send hire wiþute leave ne ne eote ha ne ne drinke ute þe oþer beo eaver inne ne wiþute þe ȝeten ne ga wiþute leave ba beon obedient to hare dame in alle þing bute i sunne ane na þing nabben þet heo hit nute ne undervo na þing ne ne ȝeove nowþer wiþuten hire leave na mon ne leoten in ne þe ȝungre ne speoke wiþ namon bute leave ne ga ha nawt ut of tune wiþuten siker fere ȝef hit swa mei beon ne ne ligge ute ȝef heo ne con o boke segge bi ant bi hire ures ant wurche þet me hat hire wiþute gruchunge habbe eaver hire earen opene toward hire dame nowþer of þe wummen ne beore from hare dame ne ne bringe to hire nane idele talen ne neowe tidinges ne bitweonen hamseolf ne singen ne ne speoken nane worldliche spechen ne lahhen swa ne pleien þet ei mon þet hit sehe mahte hit to uvel turnen over alle þinges leasunges ant luþere wordes heatien hare her beo icorven hare heavedclaþ sitte lahhe eiþer ligge ane hare cop beo hehe isticchet ant bute broche na mon ne seo ham unleppet ne openheaved lah locunge habben heo ne schulen cussen na mon ne cuþmon ne cunnesmon ne for na cuþþe cluppen ne weschen hare heaved ne lokin feaste o na mon ne toggin wiþ ne pleien hare weden beon of swuch schape ant al hare aturn swuch þet hit beo edscene hwerto ha beoþ iturnde hare lates lokin warliche þet nan ne mahe edwiten ham in hus ne ut of hus on alle wise forbeoren to wreaþen hare dame ant as ofte as heo hit doþ ear ha drinken oþer eoten makien hare o cneon dun bivoren hire ant seggen ant undervon þe penitence þet ha leiþ upon hire lutinde hire lahe þe ancre þe refter neaver mare þet ilke gult ne upbreide for na wreaþþe bute ȝef ha eft sone falle i þet ilke ah do hit allunge ut of hire heorte ȝef ei strif ariseþ bitweone þe wummen þe ancre makie eiþer to makien oþer o cneon to þer eorþe ant eiþer rihte up oþer ant cussen on ende ant te ancre legge on eiþer sum penitence mare upo þe ilke þe greatluker gulte þis is a þing witen ha wel þet is gode leovest sahtnesse ant some ant te feond laþest forþi he is eaver umben to arearen sum leaþþe nu siþ þe sweoke wel þet hwen fur is wel o brune ant me wule þet hit aga me sundreþ þe brondes ant he deþ on hond þet ilke luve is fur þet he wule þet bleasie aa i þin heorte ant te deovel blaweþ forte puffen hit ut hwen his blawunge ne geineþ nawt he bringeþ up sum uvel word oþer sum oþer nohtunge hwerþurh ha tohurten eiþer frommard oþer ant te hali gastes fur cwencheþ hwen þe brondes þurh wreaþþe beoþ isundret forþi halden ham i luve feaste togederes ant ne beo ham nawt of hwen þe feond blawe nomeliche ȝef monie beon iveiet somet ant wel wiþ luve ontende þah þe ancre on hire meidnes for openliche gultes legge penitence to þe preost noþeleater schriven ham hwen neod is ah eaver þah wiþ leave ȝef ha ne cunnen nawt þe metegraces seggen in hare stude bivoren ant ant efter mete alswa ant a mare ant segge þus on ende feader sune hali gast an almihti godd ȝeove ure dame his grace se lengre se mare ant leve hire ant us ba neomen god ende forȝelde alle þe us god doþ ant milci hare sawle þe us god idon habbeþ hare sawle ant alle cristene sawles bitweone mel ne gruseli nawt nowþer frut ne oþerhwet ne drinken bute leave ant te leave beo liht in al þet nis sunne ed te mete na word oþer lut ant teo stille alswa efter þe ancre complie aþet prime ne don na þing ne seggen hwerþurh hire silence mahe beon isturbet nan ancre servant ne ahte bi rihte to easkin iset hure bute mete ant claþ þet ha mei flutte bi ant godes milce ne misleve nan godd hwetse tide of þe ancre þet he hire trukie þe meidnes wiþuten ȝef ha serviþ þe ancre alswa as ha ahen hare hure schal beon þe hehe blisse of heovene hwase haveþ ehe of hope toward se heh hure gleadliche wule ha servin ant lihtliche alle wa ant alle teone þolien wiþ eise ant wiþ este ne buþ me nawt blisse ȝe ancres ahen þis leaste stucche reden to ower wummen euche wike eanes aþet ha hit cunnen ant muche neod is þet ȝe neomen to ham muche ȝeme for ȝe mahen muchel beon þurh ham igodet ant iwurset on oþer half ȝef þet ha sungiþ þurh ower ȝemeles ȝe schule beo bicleopet þe rof bivore þe hehe deme ant forþi as ow is muche neod ant ham ȝet mare ȝeornliche leareþ ham to halden hare riwle ba for ow ant for hamseolf liþeliche ant luveliche for swuch ah wummone lare to beonne luvelich ant liþe ant selþwenne sturne ba is riht þet ha ow dreden ant luvien ant þah þet ter beo eaver mare of luve þen of drede þenne schal hit wel fearen me schal healden eoli ant win ba i wunden efter godes lare ah mare of softe eoli þen of bitinde win þet is mare of liþe wordes þen of suhinde for þerof kimeþ þinge best þet is luve eie lihtliche ant sweteliche forȝeoveþ ham hare gultes hwen ha ham icnaweþ ant bihateþ bote as forþ as ȝe mahen of mete ant of claþes ant of oþre þinges þet neode of flesch easkeþ beoþ large toward ham þah ȝe nearowe beon ant hearde to ow seolven swa deþ þe wel blaweþ went te nearewe of þe horn to his ahne muþ ant utward þet wide ant ȝe don alswa as ȝe wulleþ þet ower beoden bemin wel ant dremen i drihtines earen nawt ane to ower ahnes ah to alle folkes heale as ure laverd leve þurh þe grace of himseolf þet hit swa mote amen hwen ower sustres meidnes cumeþ to ow to frovre cumeþ to ham to þe þurl earunder ant overunder eanes oþer twien ant gaþ aȝein sone to ower note gastelich ne bivore complie ne sitte ȝe nawt for ham over riht time swa þet hare cume beo na lure of ower religiun ah gastelich biȝete ȝef þer is eani word iseid þet mahte hurten heorte ne beo hit nawt iboren ut ne ibroht to oþer ancre þet is eþhurte to him hit schal beon iseid þe lokeþ ham alle twa niht is inoh þet ei beo edhalden ant þet beo ful seldene ne for heom ne breoke silence ed te wmete ne for blodletunge bute ȝef sum muche god oþer neod hit makie þe ancre ne hire meiden ne plohien nane worldliche gomenes ed te þurle ne ne ticki togederes for ase seiþ seint unwurþe þing is to euch gastelich mon ant nomeliche to ancre euch swuch fleschlich frovre ant hit binimeþ gastelich þet is wiþute met utnume murhþe ant þet is uvel change as is i seid þe ruppe of þis boc redeþ hwen ȝe beoþ eise euche dei leasse oþer mare ich hopie þet hit schal beon ow ȝef ȝe hit redeþ ofte swiþe biheve þurh godes muchele grace elles ich hefde uvele bitohe mi muchele hwile me were leovere godd hit wite do me toward rome þen forte biginnen hit eft forte donne ȝef ȝe findeþ þet ȝe doþ alswa as ȝe redeþ þonckiþ godd ȝeorne ȝef ȝe ne doþ nawt biddeþ godes are ant beoþ umben þeronuven þet ȝe hit bet halden efter ower mihte feader sune hali gast an almihti godd wite ow in his warde he gleadie ow ant frovri ow mine leove sustren ant for al þet ȝe for him dreheþ ant dreaieþ ne ȝeove ow neaver leasse þen al togedere himseolven beo he aa iheiet from world into world aa on ecnesse amen ase ofte as ȝe habbeþ ired eawiht heron greteþ þe leafdi wiþ an for him þet swonc herabuten inoh meaþful ich am þe bidde se lutel iþench on þi writere i þine beoden sumchearre ne beo hit ne se lutel hit turneþ þe to gode þet tu bidest for oþre
